# 3.10 MU-MIMO Management

## 3.10.0-3 MU-MIMO Management Document Owner Deputy Lisha Chen; Vimal Radhakrishnan (ID: 11141882)

## 3.10.1 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Beam Based)

### 3.10.1.1 Overview

#### 3.10.1.1.0-1 Overview About Spatial Domain (SD) scheduler (ID: 11141902)

**3.10.1.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13458100`)

Overview
13458100:
Overview
If actDlMuMimo in PsCell\_CellSetupReq is true, the SD scheduler shall be executed in every DL slots for scheduling PDSCH with spatial domain multiplexity. The input of SD scheduler, CS2 list, is the output of TD scheduler which includes all candidates for PDSCH scheduling. The SD scheduer shall execute DL pairing algorithm, create multiple CS2 lists and sends them to FD scheduler.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a hierarchical scheduling system. At the top is a "TD scheduler" which feeds into an "SD scheduler" via a "CS2 list". The "SD scheduler" is connected to two "FD scheduler" boxes via "CS2 list 1" and "CS2 list 2" respectively. Additionally, the "SD scheduler" is connected to a third "FD scheduler" box via "CS2 list N". The overall structure suggests a top-down scheduling approach where the TD scheduler manages the SD scheduler, which in turn manages multiple FD schedulers. The connections labeled "CS2 list" likely represent data or task lists passed between these schedulers.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8889.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

Please NOTE: the DL MU-MIMO approach defined under this chapter will be invalid when the new DL MU-MIMO approach is enabled (NRCell/actDlMuMimoEnh = True). In the new approach, the DL pairing is placed in FDM scheduler and users are paired at RBG level. See the detail in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7427\_replaced([11142415](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XVfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If (NRBTS/NRCELL/actDlMuMimo is true) and (NRBTS/actNr​L​B​mMimoR​T​X​Power​Saving is true) and (massive MIMO power saving indicator received from CPRT), 5G-L2-PS shall not execute DL MU-MIMO algorithms in SD scheduler.

If (NRBTS/NRCELL/actDlMuMimo is true) and (NRBTS/actNr​L​B​mMimoR​T​X​Power​Saving is true) and (massive MIMO non-power saving indicator received from CPRT), 5G-L2-PS shall execute DL MU-MIMO algorithms in SD scheduler.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

#### 3.10.1.1.0-2 Overview DL MU-MIMO request FDM scheduler enable (ID: 13457560)

**3.10.1.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13459267`)

Overview
If actDlMuMimo in PsCell\_CellSetupReq is true, the FDM scheduler introduced by 5GC000679 A/B/C/D subfeatures shall be enabled in case of FDM feature is disabled by NIDD. The related R&D parameter of 5GC000679 A/B/C/D need to be activated in L2-PS side.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

#### 3.10.1.1.0-3 Overview The diagram of overall spatial domain scheduler (ID: 13457561)

**3.10.1.1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13459273`)

Overview
13459273:
Overview
The overall flow diagram of DL spatial domain scheduling is defined as below. For each step, the detail can be found via requirement   IDs which are highlighted.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process. The flowchart begins with a "Start" oval.
From "Start", an arrow points to a rectangular process box labeled "Execute DL pairing algorithm to select users which can be paired in spatial domain. See 5G\_RAN\_UP\_13033".
An arrow from this process box leads to a diamond-shaped decision box labeled "# of users in PairSet > 1?".
- If the answer is "NO", an arrow points to a rectangular process box on the left labeled "Schedule users in CS2 list with FDM only. See 5G\_RAN\_UP\_21621".
- If the answer is "YES", an arrow points to a rectangular process box labeled "Build user group for each paired user. See 5G\_RAN\_UP\_21491".
From the "Build user group for each paired user" box, an arrow leads to another diamond-shaped decision box labeled "# of User Groups > 1?".
- If the answer is "NO", an arrow points to the "Schedule users in CS2 list with FDM only. See 5G\_RAN\_UP\_21621" box.
- If the answer is "YES", an arrow points to a rectangular process box labeled "Allocate DMRS ports for each user group. See 5G\_RAN\_UP\_21720".
From the "Allocate DMRS ports for each user group" box, an arrow leads to a rectangular process box labeled "Create CS2 list for each user group. See 5G\_RAN\_UP\_21621".
From the "Create CS2 list for each user group" box, an arrow leads to a rectangular process box labeled "Send all CS2 lists to FD scheduler".
From the "Send all CS2 lists to FD scheduler" box, an arrow leads to a rectangular process box labeled "Schedule users in each CS2 list in frequency domain. See 5G\_RAN\_UP\_21621".
Finally, an arrow from this last process box points to an "End" oval.
The flowchart uses standard flowchart symbols: ovals for start/end, rectangles for processes, and diamonds for decisions. Arrows indicate the flow of the process. Text within the shapes describes the actions or decisions at each step. The text also includes references to specific documents or sections, indicated by "See 5G\_RAN\_UP\_XXXXX".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8891.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

#### 3.10.1.1.0-4 Overview About Pairset and UserGroup (ID: 13457562)

**3.10.1.1.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13459275`)

Overview
**1) PairSet**

The PairSet is a set of users which can only be multiplexed on spatial domain for PDSCH with different beams.

**2) UserGroup**

The user group is a set of users which can only be multiplexed on frequency domain for PDSCH.

The first added user in a user group is the **primary user of this user group. Beams of this user (see definition of beams\_user in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4364\_replaced([11141957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr17H_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) are** primary beams of this user group.\*\*\*\*

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

#### 3.10.1.1.0-5 Overview Common Functions (ID: 13457571)

**3.10.1.1.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `13459283`)

Overview
Here defines some common functions which will be referred by DL MU-MIMO (NIDD:actDlMuMimo = True) algorithms:

**Note: numStreamIndex is the number of streams to be used for each PDCCH and PDSCH transmission, refer to “PDCCH transmission scheme and precoding” (5G\_UP\_ALG\_144\_replaced([11095687](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmnc3PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and “PDSCH transmission scheme and precoding” (5G\_UP\_ALG\_271\_replaced([11096446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmwmyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) respectively.**

**1)**beams\_set\*\*\*\*

beams\_set is a function which returns a set that includes all beam indexes of current beam set.

**2)**beams\_user\*\*\*\*

beams\_user is a function which returns a set that includes indices of beams (pattern IDs) associated with one user for **PDSCH transmission. The below table describes which beams shall be returned by this function under different scenarios:**

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **DL MIMO Mode** | **# of PDSCH layer(s)** | **The best beam** | **The second best beam** | **# of beam(s) per polarization** | **Notes** |
| **2x2** **(open or closed loop)** | 1~2 | √ |  | 1 |  |
| **4x2 or 4x4** **(open or closed loop)** | 1~2 | √ |  | 1 | Port selection up to rank 2 is enabled for DL MU-MIMO;   numStreamIndex shall be set to 2 . |
| **4x2 or 4x4** **(open or closed loop)** | 3~4 | √ | √ | 2 | numStreamIndex shall be set to 4 . |
| **8x4** **(closed loop with 8 CSI-RS ports)** | 1~2 | √ |  | 1 | Port selection at rank 2 is enabled by default for DL MU-MIMO;   numStreamIndex shall be set to 2 .   See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2201\_replaced([11113014](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZrGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) about how to select best beam from reported PMI beams. |
| **8x4** **(closed loop with 8 CSI-RS ports)** | 3~4 | √ | √ | 2 | numStreamIndex shall be set to 4 .   See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2201\_replaced([11113014](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZrGPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) about how to select best beam from reported PMI beams. |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

### 3.10.1.2 DL pairing algorithm

#### 3.10.1.2.0-1 DL pairing algorithm Build pairset for scheduling users on spatial domain (DL pairing algorithm) (ID: 11141973)

**3.10.1.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13459286`)

DL pairing algorithm
13459286:
DL pairing algorithm
The DL pairing algorithm is defined in below flow diagram.

NOTE-1: about definition of **PairSet, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4363\_replaced([11141952](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr17HvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). About the definition of** rrmMaxNumUsersInPairSet, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4372\_replaced([11142017](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr2iJvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*\*\*

NOTE-2: If DL MIMO mode is 8x4 closed loop, the port selection shall be used for users at rank 2.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process for pairing users. The flowchart begins with a "Start" node and proceeds through a series of decision points and actions.
Here's a breakdown of the flowchart's steps:
1. **Start**: The process begins.
2. **Sort users of CS2 list from TD scheduler in descending order according to the PF metric value of users**: Users are sorted based on a specific metric.
3. **Is the first user eligible for pairing?**: A decision point checks the eligibility of the first user.
\* **YES**: If eligible, the user is added to the PairSet.
\* **NO**: If not eligible, the process continues to the next step.
4. **Add the first user into PairSet**: The eligible first user is added to a set for pairing.
5. **Remove all non-eligible users from candidate list. See 5G\_RAN\_UP\_18746 about eligible conditions for pairing**: Non-eligible users are removed from a candidate list, with a reference to a specific document for eligibility criteria.
6. **# of elements in PairSet >= rmMaxNumUsersInPairSet?**: A decision point checks if the number of users in the PairSet has reached a maximum limit.
\* **YES**: If the limit is reached, the process moves to check for unhandled users.
\* **NO**: If the limit is not reached, the process continues to check for unhandled users.
7. **Is there still any unhandled users in CS2 list?**: A decision point checks if there are more users in the CS2 list that haven't been processed.
\* **YES**: If there are unhandled users, the next user is added to the PairSet as a candidate.
\* **NO**: If there are no more unhandled users, the process moves to the end.
8. **Add the next user into PairSet from CS2 list as a candidate**: The next available user from the CS2 list is added as a potential candidate for pairing.
9. **Can this candidate be paired? 5G\_RAN\_UP\_27756**: A decision point checks if the current candidate can be paired, referencing a specific document.
\* **YES**: If the candidate can be paired, the process moves to the next check.
\* **NO**: If the candidate cannot be paired, it is removed from the PairSet.
10. **The current candidate can be paired**: This is a state indicating successful pairing.
11. **5GC000524-G Number of DL layer higher than the maximum? See 5G\_RAN\_UP\_26049**: A decision point checks if the number of DL layers exceeds the maximum, referencing specific documents.
\* **YES**: If the DL layer count is higher than the maximum, the candidate cannot be paired and is removed from the PairSet.
\* **NO**: If the DL layer count is not higher than the maximum, the candidate is considered pairable.
12. **The current candidate cannot be paired, remove it from PairSet**: This action is taken when a candidate fails the pairing criteria.
13. **End**: The process concludes.
The flowchart uses standard flowchart symbols: rounded rectangles for start/end, rectangles for processes, and diamonds for decisions. Arrows indicate the flow of control. The text within the shapes describes the operations and conditions.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8896.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

#### 3.10.1.2.1 Conducting mode

##### 3.10.1.2.1.0-1 Conducting mode DL MU MIMO conduction mode (ID: 13457572)

**3.10.1.2.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13459288`)

Conducting mode
If DL MU-MIMO (FR1, TDD, conduction mode only) is activated via R&D parameter (the R&D parameter is defined by CP3), the DL pairing algorithm is not needed because radio channels of RRC connected UEs are isolated with each other due to RF conduct mode. TD scheduler shall schedule up to 8 UEs in CS1 list by creating multiple CS2 lists and sending them to FD scheduler. For each CS2 list, FD scheduler shall schedule single UE with full downlink bandwidth allocation with one unused DL subcell. Please refer to the 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4258\_replaced([11175719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kulGCPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for further information.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

##### 3.10.1.2.1.0-2 Conducting mode rdMumimoTestMode (ID: 13457574)

**3.10.1.2.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13459291`)

Conducting mode
The New RD parameter (rdMumimoTestMode) need to indicate L2 PS, the testing mode is on or off, the MAX User during the test, which mode (default or on demand)

The RD parameter is built like the following table:

bit [4-7], 4 bit for MAX UE number in the MU MIMO testing:

If it is set to 0, then the testmode is deactive

bit [0-3] 4 bit for next beam index

If it is 0,  it means the default mode..

1. base on the RD parameter setting, there is two mode for such testing and perform the UE pariing:

default beam setting mode:

During the default mode, The UE should be attached and provide DL throughput, one by one.. based on the special beam/pattern sequence

In the default mode, L2 PS always search the new appear RNTI and try to allocate the least special beam id to this new RNTI

if there is exist UE release, like the following scenarios

1.1 UE 0 attach, DL traffic start. L2 PS DL allocate special beam id 0

1.2 UE 1 attach, DL traffic start. L2 PS DL allocate special beam id 1

1.3 UE 2 attach, DL traffic start. L2 PS DL allocate special beam id 2

1.4 UE 1 release, L2 PS DL de-allocate the special beam id 1

1.5 New UE attach, L2 PS DL allocate special beam id 1.

2.On demand beam setting mode:

For the on-demand mode, the test can decide which special beam id will allocate the next attach and traffic starting UE.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

#### 3.10.1.2.2 Number of layers for pairing

##### 3.10.1.2.2.0-1 Number of layers for pairing Maximum number of users in PairSet (ID: 11142017)

**3.10.1.2.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13454023`)

Number of layers for pairing
The maximum number of users in PairSet can be decided according to below equation:

**rrmMaxNumUsersInPairSet = min(X, MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/dlMuMaxNumPairedUEs)**

where:

* X is the limitation on L1 of different deployment scenarios.

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **X** | **# of DL subcells for PDSCH/PDCCH** **per cell** **(C4)** | **# of UL subcells for PUSCH/PUCCH** **per cell** | **FD Beamforming** **on PUCCH/PDCCH** | **Sub-features** |
| 1 | 1 | 1 | No | 5GC002093-A |
| 2 | 2 | 2 | No | 5GC000524-A |
| 2 | 1 | 2 | No | 5GC000524-B |
| 2 | 2 | 2 | No | 5GC000524-B |
| 2 | 1 | 2 | No | 5GC000524-G |
| 2 | 2 | 2 | No | 5GC000524-G |
| 2 | 1 | 1 or 2 | Yes | 5GC000524-D |
| 4 | 2 | 1 or 2 | Yes | 5GC000524-D |

Note: the FD beamforming shall be considered as enabled when the conditions, which are defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4478\_replaced([11178989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), are met.

Note: Input parameters “# of DL subcells for PDSCH/PDCCH per cell (C4)” shall be different for SSB slot and TRS slot comparing to other normal DL slot. One subcell need to be reserved for SSB and CSI-RS transmission while DL MU-MIMO feature is enabled and non-FD BF (CPRI or eCPRi) is used. For example, if total 2 DL subcells are available for SSB slot or TRS, only 1 subcell is available for PDSCH/PDCCH for DL MU-MIMO in CPRI case. For FD BF case, there is no such limitation.

Note: Input parameters “# of DL subcells for PDSCH/PDCCH per cell (C4)” and “# of UL subcells for PUSCH/PUCCH per cell” shall be the subcell amount which is "available for usage" in the particular slot based on subcell pooling (ref to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5230\_replaced([11210126](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw3lB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

##### 3.10.1.2.2.0-2 Number of layers for pairing maximum DL layers in UE data scheduling in DL slot without TRS/SSB (ID: 11142031)

**3.10.1.2.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13459293`)

Number of layers for pairing
If **rdDlMuPairingOption = PairRank1And2 , no need to check the maximum DL layers.**

If **rdDlMuPairingOption = PairRank3And4 (see 5G\_L2\_1273\_replaced([11186688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_277KzfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the below conditions shall be checked to avoid the maximum number of DL layers is exceeded:**

1) If PDSCH of a user is transmitted with one beam per polarization (the beams\_user returns one beam, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4364\_replaced([11141957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr17H_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the number of DL layers is counted as 2.

2) If PDSCH of a user is transmitted with two beams per polarization (the beams\_user returns two beams), the number of DL layers is counted as 4.

3) The maximum number of DL layers for all users in PairSet shall be less than or equal to the value of rrmNumDlSubcells \* N. For non-FD BF case, in DL slots which have Paging/Sibs messages, the maximum number of layers is (rrmNumDlSubcells - 1) \* N. **The rrmNumDlSubcells is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4478\_replaced([11178989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The value N is the maximum number of layers one DL subcell can support. If the DL subcell type is C4, N is 4.**

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

##### 3.10.1.2.2.0-3 Number of layers for pairing maximum DL layers in UE data scheduling in TRS slot (ID: 11142043)

**3.10.1.2.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13459294`)

Number of layers for pairing
In case of MU-MIMO and non-FD BF case in TRS slot, the maximum number of DL layers for all users shall be less than or equal to the value of (rrmNumDlSubcells – 1) \* N. The rrmNumDlSubcells is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4478\_replaced([11178989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The value N is the maximum number of layers one DL subcell can support, for example: N is 4 is the DL subcell is C4.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

##### 3.10.1.2.2.0-4 Number of layers for pairing maximum DL layers in UE data scheduling in SSB slot (ID: 11142056)

**3.10.1.2.2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13459300`)

Number of layers for pairing
In case of MU-MIMO and non-FD BF case in SSB slot, the maximum number of DL layers for all users shall be less than or equal to the value of (rrmNumDlSubcells – 1) \* N. The rrmNumDlSubcells is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4478\_replaced([11178989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The value N is the maximum number of layers one DL subcell can support, for example: N is 4 is the DL subcell is C4.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

##### 3.10.1.2.2.0-5 Number of layers for pairing Downgrade user's ranks (3 or 4) to rank 2 port selection (ID: 11142069)

**3.10.1.2.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11142074`)

Number of layers for pairing
If rdDlMuPairingOption = PairWithRanksDowngrade (see 5G\_L2\_1273\_replaced([11186688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_277KzfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), for users which are eligible for pairing, L2-PS shall downgrade HARQ initial transmission at ranks 3 or 4 to rank 2 with the algorithm defined as below. If no users can be paired, L2-PS shall use original ranks to transmit PDSCH signal.

For users at ranks 3 or 4, PDSCH signal of each user shall be served with two x-pol beams (the best and second best beams). After downgrade them to rank 2 port selection, PDSCH signal of each user shall be served with one x-pol beam (the best reported beam).

To downgrade user's ranks, CSI report and beams from users at ranks 3 or 4 shall be converted as below:

1. The user's rank is changed to rank 2.
2. The CQI value in CSI report is not changed (this part may be changed in the future according to simulation result).
3. The codebook shall be converted from i2 to codebook index according to the below mapping table. About PMI value i2 and codebook index, see tables 5.2.2.2.1-1/5.2.2.2.1-7/5.2.2.2.1-8 in 38.214.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| i2 | Codebook index |
| 0 | 0 |
| 1 | 1 |

1. L2-PS shall use the best beam to transmit PDCCH and PDSCH signals for these users.

Note: this requirement assumes the PMI is based on type I single-panel codebook and codebookMode is 1.

---

#### 3.10.1.2.3 Calculate DL pairing factor

##### 3.10.1.2.3.0-1 Calculate DL pairing factor Correlation of beams (ID: 13457575)

**3.10.1.2.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13458173`)

Calculate DL pairing factor
13458173:
Calculate DL pairing factor
The [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a close-up of a mathematical expression. The expression is written in a blue font with a slight reddish-brown outline. The characters are: "T", "i", ".", and "j". The "i" is a subscript to the "T", and the "." and "j" are also subscripts to the "T". The overall impression is that of a variable or a matrix element.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8912.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] reflects the interference ratio between two beams. It’s a float value, in range of 0.0~1.0, which shall be calculated with the below equation:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a light gray font against a white background. The equation is:
$r\_{i,j} = corr\_{i,j}/255$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8912.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

where

* i and j are pattern IDs of two beams that are associated with users.
* the [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "corrᵢ,ⱼ" in a blurry, stylized font. The text is in a light color with a subtle rainbow effect.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8912.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] is the value read from correlationTable or correlationTable2 as mentioned below.

If dlMimoMode is set to ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing\_8x4, [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains the text "corrᵢ,ⱼ" in a blurry, stylized font. The text is in a light color with a subtle rainbow effect.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8912.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]  is read from correlationTable2 parameter received in Cell PMI Beam Data Set procedure, otherwise [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains the text "corrᵢ,ⱼ" in a blurry, stylized font. The text is in a light color with a subtle rainbow effect.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8912.004.png[/image\_path][/image-4]  is read from correlationTable parameter received in cell setup procedure (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2644\_replaced([11302499](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqfubfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

##### 3.10.1.2.3.0-2 Calculate DL pairing factor (ID: 13457576)

**3.10.1.2.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13458183`)

Calculate DL pairing factor
13458183:
Calculate DL pairing factor
The DL pairing factor of [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains the text "USERk" in a stylized font. The letters are colored with a gradient effect, transitioning from a light orange to a light blue. The letter "k" is smaller and appears as a subscript to the word "USER". The text is set against a white background with a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8913.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] shall be calculated with below equation:

[image-1][image\_desc]dl\_pairing\_factor\_k = Σ\_{j∈Pairset\k} user\_corr\_{k,j}[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8913.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

where

Pairset is a set which includes paired users plus one new candidate for pairing;

Pairset\k is a subset of Pairset which doesn’t include element of [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "USERk" in a stylized font. The letters are colored with a gradient effect, transitioning from a light orange to a light blue. The letter "k" is smaller and appears as a subscript to the word "USER". The text is set against a white background with a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8913.001.png[/image\_path][/image-2];

[image-3][image\_desc]user\_corr\_{k,j}[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8913.003.png[/image\_path][/image-3] is a function for estimating interference level from [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains the text "USER" with a subscript "i" to the right of the "R". The text is in a sans-serif font and appears to be in a dark color with a slight chromatic aberration effect, giving it a subtle rainbow-like outline. The background is white, and the text is enclosed within a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8913.004.png[/image\_path][/image-4] to [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains the text "USERk" in a stylized font. The letters are colored with a gradient effect, transitioning from a light orange to a light blue. The letter "k" is smaller and appears as a subscript to the word "USER". The text is set against a white background with a black border.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8913.001.png[/image\_path][/image-5] which is defined as below:

[image-6][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
user\_corr\_{k,j} = max\_{m \in beams\_user(k)} \sum\_{n \in beams\_user(j)} r\_{m,n}^2[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8913.005.png[/image\_path][/image-6]

where

* k and j are user indexes;
* [image-7][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, colorful representation of the text "T m,n". The letters and numbers are distorted and appear to have a rainbow-like effect.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8913.006.png[/image\_path][/image-7] reflects the interference ratio from beam index n to beam index m (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4386\_replaced([11142111](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3JMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));
* beams\_user is a function which is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4364\_replaced([11141957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr17H_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

#### 3.10.1.2.4 Eligible conditions for pairing

##### 3.10.1.2.4.0-1 Eligible conditions for pairing The eligible users for pairing (ID: 11142166)

**3.10.1.2.4.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `13458195`)

Eligible conditions for pairing
The eligible users for DL pairing shall meet all conditions as below:

1) PDSCH is scheduled by PDCCH using DCI 1\_1 with C-RNTI (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4443\_replaced([11178081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku0Wk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

2) The DL buffer on SRB is empty.

3) User’s SINR is higher than dlMuLowSinrThreshold. The user's SINR shall be calculated from the averaged CQI with OLLA correction (rrmCorrAvgCqi\_k=BR).

4) If rdDlMuPairingOption is PairRank1And2, only users at ranks <= 2 can be paired.

5)  If the **dlMimoMode is 2x2 or 4x4 (OL or CL):**

PDSCH is transmitted with refined beams.

6) If the **dlMimoMode is 8x4 (CL), PDSCH shall be transmitted with PMI beams.**

7)  UE works on basic reliability LA mode in DL**.**

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

##### 3.10.1.2.4.0-2 Eligible conditions for pairing Conditions for adding candidates into PairSet (ID: 11142186)

**3.10.1.2.4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13458205`)

Eligible conditions for pairing
13458205:
Eligible conditions for pairing
To add any new candidate into PairSet, all users in PairSet (including the new candidate) shall meet below conditions:
 The dl\_pairing\_factor of each user (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4387\_replaced([11142153](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3JM_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be less or equal than the value of dlMuPairingThreshold.
 
To add any new candidate into PairSet, the spectrum efficiency shall be checked to ensure below equation is met:
[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical inequality. On the left side, there is a summation symbol (Σ) with the index 'i' belonging to a set labeled 'EPairSet'. This summation is followed by the expression 'rank\_i \* spectralEfficiency\_i'. On the right side of the inequality, there is another summation symbol (Σ) with the index 'j' belonging to a set labeled 'EPairSetC'. This summation is followed by the expression 'rank\_j \* spectralEfficiency\_j'. The inequality symbol between the two summations is '<'.
The text in the image is:
$\sum\_{i \in EPairSet} rank\_i \* spectralEfficiency\_i < \sum\_{j \in EPairSetC} rank\_j \* spectralEfficiency\_j$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8919.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
where:
 pairSet: a set which includes paired user(s);
 pairSetC: a set which includes paired user(s) plus the new candidate;
 rank(i)/rank(j): PDSCH ranks of user(i)/user(j);
 spectralEfficiency(i)/spectralEfficiency(j): spectral efficiency of user(i)/user(j) and according to their selected MCS values. The efficiency values are defined in tables 5.1.3.1-1 (64QAM) and 5.1.3.1-2 (256QAM) in TS 38.214.
NOTE: The selected MCS is roughly estimated according to tables in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3028\_replaced([11126310](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqw9C_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for FR1\TDD supposing wide-band PBRs for transmission, PTRS OFF and 256QAM enabled. Before pairing, the MCS is calculated based on CQI from OLLA. After pairing, the MCS is calculated based on CQI from OLLA plus MU-MIMO CQI adjustment.
 [CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

### 3.10.1.3 Build user groups

#### 3.10.1.3.0-1 Build user groups Build user groups for scheduling users on frequency domain (ID: 11142208)

**3.10.1.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13458207`)

Build user groups
13458207:
Build user groups
After the DL pairing algorithm is executed and there are users which can be paired in PairSet, the SD scheduler shall create user groups for users in PairSet (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4363\_replaced([11141952](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr17HvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to the overall procedure which is defined in below diagram:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process for creating user groups.
The flowchart begins with a "Start" oval.
Next, a rectangular process box states: "Get one user from PairSet See 5G\_RAN\_UP\_13033".
Following this, another rectangular process box reads: "Create a user group and add this user into the group as the primary user".
A larger rectangular box contains a description of conditions for adding more users to the group: "To add more, from CS2 list of TD scheduler, into the current user group, below conditions shall be met: 1) Users are eligible for pairing (see 5G\_RAN\_UP\_18746), and 2) Users are not in any user group, and 3) Users in one user group shall NOT exceed the maximum number of users which is defined in 5G RAN UP 28190, and 4) Users meet beams related conditions which are defined in 5G\_RAN\_UP\_24147".
A diamond-shaped decision box asks: "All users in PairSet are processed?".
There are two arrows originating from this decision box. One labeled "YES" points to an oval labeled "End". The other arrow, labeled "NO", points back to the process of getting another user from PairSet (implied by the loop structure, though not explicitly drawn as a loop back to the "Get one user" step).[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8922.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

#### 3.10.1.3.0-2 Build user groups Beam related conditions for users in the same user group (ID: 13457578)

**3.10.1.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13458208`)

Build user groups
Note: in this requirement, the FD beamforming shall be considered as enabled when the conditions, which are defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4478\_replaced([11178989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), are met.

**FD Beamforming Disabled**

Users, whose associated beams (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4364\_replaced([11141957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr17H_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) are **subset of primary beams of a user group, can be added into the current user group. For example:**

1) The primary beam of a user group is {B1}, only users which are using the beam {B1} can be added into this user group.

2) The primary beams of a user group is {B1, B2}, only users which are using the beams {B1} or {B2} or {B1, B2} can be added into this user group. Note: users using beams {B2, B1} can’t be added into this user group.

**FD Beamforming Enabled**

Users, whose associated beams (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4364\_replaced([11141957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr17H_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) meet conditions which are defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4400\_replaced([11142258](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3wQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), can be added into the current user group.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

#### 3.10.1.3.0-3 Build user groups Check maximum number of users in user group (ID: 11142233)

**3.10.1.3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13454085`)

Build user groups
The maximum number of users which can be added in a user group is defined as maxNumOfUesPerUserGroup.

The value of maxNumOfUesPerUserGroup is rrmMaxNumUesFdmDlSubcell (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4478\_replaced([11178989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The value of maxNumOfUesPerUserGroup is Max(Min(rrmMaxNumUesFdmDlSubcell,  rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl /numOfDlSubcell), 1), if long PUCCH is enabled. numOfDlSubcell is the number of available DL subcells in the cell. For the case of subcell pooling activated, numOfDlSubcell shall be "available for usage" based on subcell pooling

However, for a user group which has one primary x-pol beam, if the number of users in the PairSet is higher than numOfDlSubcell (the number DL subcell per cell), the maximum number of users which can be added in it is maxNumOfUesPerUserGroup / 2.

For the case of non-FD beamforming, in slots which have SI/Paging, the numOfDlSubcell shall be reduced one because one DL subcell is reserved for SI/Paging.

Note:

rrmMaxNumUesFdmDlSubcell and rrmMaxNumUesFdmDl refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4478\_replaced([11178989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

#### 3.10.1.3.0-4 Build user groups Add neighbor users in user group (ID: 13457580)

**3.10.1.3.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13458360`)

Build user groups
13458360:
Build user groups
Each user group has a primary user (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4363\_replaced([11141952](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr17HvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). To add a user into user group, L2-RT shall ensure that this candidate only introduces similar interference, compared with the primary user, to all users in other user groups. It means beams of eligible candidates shall have high correlation with beam(s) of the primary user in user group.

For example, for AEQB with the 5\_3 beam set, the correlation of beam#1 and beam#10 is 0.12673, their correlations with other beams are shown as below:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a line graph titled "Correlation of beams". The x-axis is labeled with numbers from 1 to 32, representing different beams. The y-axis is labeled with values from 0 to 1.2, representing correlation values. There are two lines on the graph: an orange line labeled "Beam#10" and a blue line labeled "Beam#1".
The orange line, representing Beam#10, starts at approximately 0.15 at beam 1, rises to a peak of 1.0 at beam 10, and then generally decreases with some fluctuations. Notable peaks for Beam#10 occur at beam 10 (1.0), beam 12 (0.42), beam 13 (0.4), and beam 27 (0.25).
The blue line, representing Beam#1, starts at 1.0 at beam 1, then sharply decreases to around 0.4 at beam 2, and continues to fluctuate at lower values. Notable peaks for Beam#1 occur at beam 1 (1.0), beam 5 (0.2), beam 6 (0.22), beam 10 (0.12), beam 14 (0.08), beam 21 (0.25), and beam 27 (0.05).
The graph shows the correlation of two different beams across a range of 32 beams.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8926.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

The correlation of beam#22 and beam#23 is 0.55949, their correlations with other beams are shown as below:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is a line graph titled "Correlation of beams". The x-axis is labeled with numbers from 1 to 32, representing "Beam#". The y-axis is labeled with values from 0 to 1.2, representing the correlation. There are two lines on the graph: a blue line labeled "Beam#22" and an orange line labeled "Beam#23".
The blue line (Beam#22) starts at approximately 0.15 at Beam#1, rises to about 0.25 at Beam#2, drops to 0.05 at Beam#3, rises to 0.4 at Beam#4, drops to 0.05 at Beam#5, rises to 0.25 at Beam#6, drops to 0.05 at Beam#7, rises to 0.1 at Beam#8, and then fluctuates between 0 and 0.15 until Beam#20. From Beam#20, it rises sharply to approximately 1 at Beam#22, then drops to 0.15 at Beam#24, and fluctuates between 0.05 and 0.15 from Beam#25 to Beam#32.
The orange line (Beam#23) starts at approximately 0.05 at Beam#1, rises to 0.2 at Beam#2, drops to 0.05 at Beam#3, rises to 0.25 at Beam#4, drops to 0.05 at Beam#5, rises to 0.4 at Beam#7, drops to 0.1 at Beam#8, and then fluctuates between 0 and 0.15 until Beam#20. From Beam#20, it rises sharply to approximately 1 at Beam#23, then drops to 0.15 at Beam#24, and fluctuates between 0.05 and 0.15 from Beam#25 to Beam#32.
Both lines show a significant peak around Beam#22 and Beam#23, indicating a high correlation between these beams.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8926.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

Another example is AEQA with 2D DFT beams (N1 = N2 = 2), the correlation of beam#1 and beam#8 is 0.92388, their correlations with other beams are shown as below:

[image-2][image\_desc]The image is a line graph titled "Correlation of beams". The x-axis represents beam numbers, with labels at intervals such as 1, 10, 19, 28, 37, 46, 55, 64, 73, 82, 91, 100, 109, 118, 127, 136, 145, 154, 163, 172, 181, 190, 199, 208, 217, 226, 235, 244, and 253. The y-axis represents correlation values, ranging from 0 to 1.2, with tick marks at 0, 0.2, 0.4, 0.6, 0.8, 1, and 1.2.
There are two lines plotted on the graph, representing "Beam#1" (in blue) and "Beam#8" (in orange). Both lines show fluctuating correlation values across the different beam numbers. The initial beams (around 1 to 64) show high correlation values, with peaks close to 1. After beam 64, the correlation values drop significantly and remain relatively low, oscillating between approximately 0 and 0.2 for a large portion of the graph. Towards the end of the x-axis, there are some localized increases in correlation for both beams. The blue line and the orange line are very close to each other throughout the graph, indicating a high degree of correlation between Beam#1 and Beam#8.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8926.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

A user can be added into user group if the below conditions are met:

1) NeighborCorr > NRBTS/NRCELL/dlMuNeighborThreshold, and

- About the value of NeighborCorr, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4401\_replaced([11142282](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3wQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

~~2)~~~~dl\_pairing\_factor > dlMuPairingThreshold, and~~

~~-~~~~About the value of dl\_pairing\_factor, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4385\_replaced([11142082](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3JMfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).~~

3) Number of users in this user group is less than the maximum number defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7953\_replaced([11142233](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3wQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

4) Number of beams which are assigned to this user group is not higher than rrmMaxNumBeamsDlStream (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4478\_replaced([11178989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note 1: In 5G20B, the rrmMaxNumBeamsDlStream equals to rrmMaxNumUesFdmDlSubcell, see the definition in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4478\_replaced([11178989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note 2: The meaning of rrmMaxNumBeamsDlStream is defined as the number of beams per symbol per AxC/eAxC. For example, for CPRI case (AxC), the rrmMaxNumBeamsDlStream is 1 because each AxC stream in DL C4 subcell can only support one beam direction per symbol. For eCPRI case (eAxC), if the rrmMaxNumBeamsDlStream is 4, each eAxC stream can support 4 beam directions per symbol. Please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4409\_replaced([11142366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3wTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) about scheduling patterns that L2-RT can support with one DL C4 subcell.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

#### 3.10.1.3.0-5 Build user groups Calculate neighbor correlation (ID: 13457581)

**3.10.1.3.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `13458365`)

Build user groups
13458365:
Build user groups
This requirement defines how to calculate the NeighborCorr when adding a user into user group. The NeighborCorr is a factor to estimate the level of correlation between beam(s) of candidate and beam(s) of primary user in user group. The L2-RT shall check its value and determine which users can be added into a user group (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4400\_replaced([11142258](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3wQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a table with 5 columns and 4 rows. The first row is a header row. The table describes different cases (A, B, C) and their corresponding values for "Primary User" (Best (p1), Second best (p2)), "Candidate" (Best (c1), Second best (c2)), and "NeighborCorr". The last column contains a text explaining that "The value of rk,j is defined in 5G\_RAN\_UP\_21411".
Here is the table in markdown format:

| Case | Primary User | Candidate | NeighborCorr | The value of rk,j is defined in 5G\_RAN\_UP\_21411 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | Best (p1) | Second best (p2) | Best (c1) | Second best (c2) |
| A | Yes | No | Yes | No |
| B | Yes | Yes | Yes | No |
| C | Yes | Yes | Yes | Yes |

Here are some examples to explain how to calculate NeighborCorr for different cases:

Note: P1/P2 are the best and second best beams of primary user. C1/C2 are the best and second best beams of candidate.

Case A:

NeighborCorr is calculated as the correlation between P1 and C1.

[image-1][image\_desc]The image displays two overlapping, elongated oval shapes, colored blue and green. The blue oval is labeled "P1" in white text, and the green oval is labeled "C1" in white text. The shapes are positioned at an angle to each other, with a portion of each shape overlapping the other. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8927.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

Case B:

NeighborCorr is calculated as the maximum correlation from (P1, C1) and (P2, C1). If the beam of candidate has high correlation with any one of beams of primary user, the candidate will be eligible for adding into the user group.

[image-2][image\_desc]The image displays two abstract diagrams, each composed of overlapping elliptical shapes in blue and green. Both diagrams are set against a white background.
The left diagram features a green ellipse labeled "C1" positioned vertically. To its right and slightly above, a blue ellipse labeled "P1" overlaps with "C1" at its upper portion. Further to the right and angled upwards, another blue ellipse labeled "P2" is positioned, with its left end overlapping the upper part of "P1".
The right diagram is similar in composition but with a different arrangement. A blue ellipse labeled "P1" is positioned vertically, angled to the left. Above and to its right, a blue ellipse labeled "P2" is placed horizontally. Overlapping the left end of "P2" and extending upwards and to the right is a green ellipse labeled "C1".
The text within the ellipses is clearly legible.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8927.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

Case C:

To calculate NeighborCorr for this case include below steps:

1) To calculate the maximum correlation from (P1, C1) and (P2, C1).

2) To calculate the maximum correlation from (P1, C2) and (P2, C2).

3) NeighborCorr is calculated as the minimum value from above two correlations.

4) If NeighborCorr is higher than the correlation threshold (dlMuNeighborThreshold), it means above two correlations are all higher than the dlMuNeighborThreshold because the minimum value is used.

[image-3][image\_desc]The image displays two abstract diagrams, each composed of two green ovals and two blue ovals arranged in a similar, yet distinct, configuration. Both diagrams are positioned on a white background.
The left diagram features a green oval labeled "C1" and a blue oval labeled "P1" positioned vertically, with "C1" above "P1". To the right and slightly above these, another green oval labeled "C2" and a blue oval labeled "P2" are arranged horizontally, with "C2" above "P2". The two sets of ovals are connected at a central point, forming an L-shape.
The right diagram mirrors the structure of the left diagram but with a key difference in labeling. The vertical green oval is now labeled "C3" and the vertical blue oval is labeled "P1". The horizontal green oval is labeled "C1" and the horizontal blue oval is labeled "P2". This suggests a potential re-labeling or a different configuration of elements compared to the left diagram.
The ovals are rendered with a slight gradient, giving them a three-dimensional appearance. The colors are solid and distinct. The overall impression is that of a schematic representation, possibly illustrating a process, a relationship, or a comparison between two states or entities.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8927.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

---

### 3.10.1.4 Allocate DMRS ports

#### 3.10.1.4.0-1 Allocate DMRS ports About "Antenna port" and "DMRS sequences initialization" (ID: 11142294)

**3.10.1.4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13458388`)

Allocate DMRS ports
13458388:
Allocate DMRS ports
**In DCI 1\_1**

For the case that NIDD:actDlMuMimo = True, here are definition of 'antenna port(s)' and 'DMRS sequence initialization' fields in DCI 1\_1. The DMRS is configured as type-I and number of front-load DMRS symbol is 1.

**1.DMRS sequence initialization**

It’s one bit field because both scramblingID0 and scramblingID1 are configured in DMRS-DownlinkConfig. The DMRS port assignment algorithm (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4405\_replaced([11142329](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3wSfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) will decide its value according to pairing result.

**2.Antenna port(s)**

It’s 4-bit field because DMRS is configured as type-I and maxLenght is len1.

The DMRS port assignment algorithm (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4405\_replaced([11142329](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3wSfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) will decide its value according to pairing result. Its possible values are defined in the table 7.3.1.2.2-1 in 38.212 (see as below). The number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data is 1 or 2 if actDlDataDmrsFdm is TRUE, otherwise, it's 2 if actDlDataDmrsFdm is FALSE.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a table with three columns: "Value", "Number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data", and "DMRS port(s)". The table has a header that specifies "One Codeword: Codeword 0 enabled, Codeword 1 disabled".

| Value | Number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data | DMRS port(s) |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 0 | 1 | 0 |
| 1 | 1 | 1 |
| 2 | 1 | 0,1 |
| 3 | 2 | 0 |
| 4 | 2 | 1 |
| 5 | 2 | 2 |
| 6 | 2 | 3 |
| 7 | 2 | 0,1 |
| 8 | 2 | 2,3 |
| 9 | 2 | 0-2 |
| 10 | 2 | 0-3 |
| 11 | 2 | 0,2 |
| 12-15 | Reserved | Reserved |

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

#### 3.10.1.4.0-2 Allocate DMRS ports Allocation order for assigning DMRS ports to user groups (ID: 11142311)

**3.10.1.4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13458390`)

Allocate DMRS ports
13458390:
Allocate DMRS ports
To allocate DMRS ports to user groups shall ensure antenna ports with low order values can be allocated at first. The below table defines the allocation orders.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a table with four columns: "Order", "Antenna Ports in DCI 1\_1", "PDSCH antenna ports", and "Notes". The table has 9 rows of data.

| Order | Antenna Ports in DCI 1\_1 | PDSCH antenna ports | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1 | 3 | 1000 |  |
| 2 | 4 | 1001 |  |
| 3 | 5 | 1002 |  |
| 4 | 6 | 1003 |  |
| 5 | 7 | 1000, 1001 |  |
| 6 | 8 | 1002, 1003 |  |
| 7 | 9 | 1000, 1001, 1002 |  |
| 8 | 10 | 1000, 1001, 1002, 1003 |  |
| 9 | 11 | 1000, 1002 | Due to high PAPR issue on DMRS (rel-15), gNB shall avoid allocating DMRS ports to UE which are not in the same CDM group. |

For example,

1) UserGroup1 (rank 2), UserGroup2 (rank 2)

UserGroup1 {1000, 1001}, UserGroup2 {1002, 1003}, Nscid = 0

2) UserGroup1 (rank 1), UserGroup2 (rank 2)

UserGroup1 {1000}, UserGroup2 {1002, 1003}, Nscid = 0

3) UserGroup1 (rank 1), UserGroup2 (rank 1), UserGroup3 (rank 2)

UserGroup1 {1000}, UserGroup2 {1001}, UserGroup3 {1002, 1003}, Nscid = 0

4) UserGroup1 (rank 2), UserGroup2 (rank 2), UserGroup3 (rank 2), UserGroup4 (rank 2)

UserGroup1 {1000, 1001} and UserGroup2 {1002, 1003} with Nscid = 0

UserGroup3 {1000, 1001} and UserGroup4 {1002, 1003} with Nscid = 1

5) UserGroup1 (rank 4), UserGroup2 (rank 3)

UserGroup1 {1000, 1001, 1002, 1003} with Nscid = 0, UserGroup2 {1000, 1001, 1002} with Nscid = 1

6) UserGroup1 (rank 4), UserGroup2 (rank 2), UserGroup3 (rank 1)

UserGroup1 {1000, 1001, 1002, 1003} with Nscid = 0, UserGroup2 {1000, 1001} and UserGroup3 {1002} with Nscid = 1

Following this, another rectangular box reads "Take one user group which has the highest rank among all non-processed users groups".

### 3.10.1.5 Send CS2 lists to FD scheduler

#### 3.10.1.5.0-1 Send CS2 lists to FD scheduler Allocate DL subcells to user groups (ID: 11142366)

**3.10.1.5.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13458428`)

Send CS2 lists to FD scheduler
13458428:
Send CS2 lists to FD scheduler
This requirement defines how to allocate DL subcells to user groups.
 
If (**rdDlMuPairingOption = PairRank1And2)** or (all user groups have single primary beam (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4363\_replaced([11141952](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr17HvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))), the DL subcells allocation algorithm is defined as below:\*\*\*\*
For each user group, dedicated subcell ID and stream indice shall be assigned to it with orders which are defined in the below table ('m' is the number of available DL subcell instances).

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Order |  | DL Subcell instances |  | stream index |  |
| 0 |  | 0 |  | {0,1} |  |
|  | 1 |  | 1 |  | {0,1} |
|  | .. |  | .. |  | .. |
|  | m-1 |  | m-1 |  | {0,1} |
|  | M |  | 0 |  | {2,3} |
|  | m+1 |  | 1 |  | {2,3} |
|  | .. |  | .. |  | .. |
|  | 2m-1 |  | m-1 |  | {2,3} |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| If (**rdDlMuPairingOption = PairRank3And4 )** and (at least one user group has two primary beams (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4363\_replaced([11141952](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr17HvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))), the DL subcells allocation algorithm is defined as below:\*\*\*\* |  |  |  |  |  |
| 1) For user groups which have one primary beam: |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| One C4 DL subcell can schedule users in two user groups which have one primary beam. The below table is an example: |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |

|  |  |  |  |  |
| 3) To ensure DL subcells can be fully utilized, DL subcells shall be allocated to user groups with two primary beams at first. A user group with two primary beams will be the only one mapped on a given C4 DL subcells. (If several user groups have been defined with two primary beams, each of them will be mapped on a dedicated C4 DL subcell.) The other user groups (with one primary beam) will be mapped on the remaining C4 DL subcell and two of them can be set per C4 DL subcell. For example, there are 3 user groups: UG1 (one primary beam), UG2 (two primary beams), UG3 (one primary beam), and there 2 C4 subcells. The subcell allocation shall follow below orders: |  |  |  |  |
| a) The UG2 shall be allocated to subcell-0 with stream index {0, 1, 2, 3}. |  |  |  |  |
| b) The UG1 shall be allocated to subcell-1 with stream index {0, 1}. |  |  |  |  |
| c) The UG3 shall be allocated to subcell-1 with stream index {2, 3}. |  |  |  |  |

#### 3.10.1.5.0-2 Send CS2 lists to FD scheduler Allocate PDSCH stream index for eCPRI when dlMimoMode is CL 8x4 MIMO (ID: 11142387)

**3.10.1.5.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13458429`)

Send CS2 lists to FD scheduler
This requirement defines how to allocate stream index for within one C4 subcells to user for eCPRI cell and dlMimoMode is CL 8x4 MIMO.

Note: when dlMimoMode is not CL 8x4 MIMO, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3171\_replaced([11139234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krlca_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If actDlSrsBm is false:

If actDlMuMimo is ture, stream indexs for different users are the same as 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4409\_replaced([11142366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3wTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

Else (i.e. actDlMuMimo is false):

{

If the PDSCH of this UE need 4 streams, i.e rank 2 without port selection, rank3,rank4), the 4 stream index {0, 1, 2, 3} shall be used for all the FDM UEs.

Else If the PDSCH of this UE need 2 streams, i.e rank 1, the 2 stream index {0, 1} shall be used for all the FDM UEs.

Else: shall not happen

}

If actDlSrsBm is true: For UEs under 8 port CSI-RS mode, rank 2 only have port selection, so only the stream index {0, 1} is used for rank 2. For UEs under 4 port CSI-RS mode, refers to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3171\_replaced([11139234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krlca_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Note: common channels have the same behaviour as Rank1.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]

#### 3.10.1.5.0-3 Send CS2 lists to FD scheduler (ID: 11142400)

**3.10.1.5.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13458430`)

Send CS2 lists to FD scheduler
If no user can be paired, SD scheduler shall send original CS2 list to FD scheduler to schedule users in frequency domain.

If there are users can be paired and multiple user groups are created (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4396\_replaced([11142208](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3JO_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), SD scheduler shall create CS2 lists for each user group according to below rules:

For each user group, up to **rrmMaxNumUesFdmDlSubcell users shall be added into related CS2 list. See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4478\_replaced([11178989](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2y2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) about the definition of** rrmMaxNumUesFdmDlSubcell.\*\*\*\*

For users in each CS2 list, SD scheduler shall provide below information to FD scheduler:

 subcell ID (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4409\_replaced([11142366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3wTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 Nscid and antPort (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25028\_replaced([11142347](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3wS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 dlDmrsLen (always equals to 1 so far)

 dmrsScramblingSequenceInt (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2224\_replaced([11282098](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpcljfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 If Nscid = 0, dmrsScramblingSequenceInt = dmrsScramblingId\_0

 If Nscid = 1, dmrsScramblingSequenceInt = dmrsScramblingId\_1

 streamIndex (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4409\_replaced([11142366](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3wTvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_144\_replaced([11095687](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmnc3PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_271\_replaced([11096446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmwmyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

 direction of PRB allocation by FD scheduler

a. high2low: allocate PRBs in descending order of PRB index

b. low2high: allocate PRBs in ascending order of PRB index

 the first CS2 list shall use the value "high2low", then the second CS2 list shall use the value "low2high", and so on.

[CB013712-A] Not valid for NewFR1 [End CB013712-A]
