## 3.10.2 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)

### 3.10.2.0-2 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) DL pairing algorithm in FD (ID: 11142428)

**3.10.2.0-2.0-8**  (ID: `13362449`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
13362449:
DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
When NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh = True, 5G-L2-PS shall execute DL MU-MIMO algorithms in FD scheduler. The overall DL MU-MIMO algorithms are defined as below.

If (NRBTS/NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh is true) and (NRBTS/actNr​L​B​mMimoR​T​X​Power​Saving is true) and (massive MIMO power saving indicator received from CPRT), 5G-L2-PS shall not execute DL MU-MIMO algorithms in FD scheduler.

If (NRBTS/NRCELL/actDlMuMimoEnh is true) and (NRBTS/actNr​L​B​mMimoR​T​X​Power​Saving is true) and (massive MIMO non-power saving indicator received from CPRT), 5G-L2-PS shall execute DL MU-MIMO algorithms in FD scheduler.

If NRCELL.actExhaustiveScheduling is set to 1 (for DL only) or 3 (for both DL and UL), then

gNB-DU shall calculate the PRB allocation ratio to determine if MU pairing is needed in this slot or not, before execution of MU pairing for both initial and retransmission UEs. The PRB allocation ratio is calculated as a ratio of total required PRBs to the total PRBs available for the slot. The total required PRB calculation must take into account the sum of the required PRBs for all users selected for scheduling including retransmissions for the current slot. Note the required PRBs for each user shall be the minimum number of PRBs required to drain the buffer of one or multiple bearers the user might have. If the PRB allocation ratio is NOT less than NIDD:dlMuPairingPrbRatio, then MU pairing is needed in this slot else MU pairing is not needed in the slot.

[CB015010-A] The below figure depicts the DL ES when NRCELL.actCarPoolLaneMuPairingES is set to a value other than 'DL' or 'DLAndUL'.[End CB015010-A]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process for determining MU pairing and allocating resources. The flowchart begins with a starting point, followed by a decision box.
Here's a breakdown of the flowchart's steps:
1. **Determine if MU pairing is needed or not**: This initial step involves calculating PRBmax for non-GBR users and the prbAllocRatio, defined as totalRequiredPrb/totalPrb \* 100. totalRequiredPrb is the sum of PRBmax needed to drain user buffers, and totalPRB is the total available PRBs in the current DL slot.
2. **Decision**: A diamond-shaped box asks if "prbAllocRatio > NIDDMuPairingrbRatio?".
\* If **Yes**: The process proceeds to "Build MU candidate list (see 11142605)".
\* If **No**: The process branches to "Allocate resources to all UEs in the list SU allocation followed by subarea assignment".
3. **Build MU candidate list (see 11142605)**: This step involves creating a list of potential MU candidates.
4. **Calculate max DL MU layers (see 11142759)**: This step calculates the maximum number of DL MU layers.
5. **Virtual UE construction and FD resource reservation (see 11144618, 11144070)**: This step, highlighted in green, involves constructing virtual UEs and reserving FD resources.
6. **Redistribution of free/remaining FD resources (see 11145129)**: This step deals with redistributing any available or remaining FD resources.
7. **Calculate Tx Power (see 11145459)**: This step calculates the transmission power.
8. **Calculate final MCS (see 11145579)**: This step determines the final Modulation and Coding Scheme (MCS).
9. **Fill FD scheduling info**: This is the final step in this branch, where FD scheduling information is populated.
The flowchart concludes with a final black circle, indicating the end of the process. There is also a line connecting the "Allocate resources to all UEs..." step to the final black circle, suggesting that this branch also leads to the process completion.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-05090929.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CB015010-A] The below figure depicts the DL ES when NRCELL.actCarPoolLaneMuPairingES is set to a value 'DL' or 'DLAndUL'.

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process for determining Multi-User (MU) pairing and resource allocation in a communication system.
The flowchart begins with a starting node, followed by a decision box titled "Determine if MU pairing is needed or not". This box contains calculations for "PRBmax", "prbAllocRatio", "totalRequiredPrb", and "totalPRB".
A diamond-shaped decision node follows, asking "prbAllocRatio > NIDD:dMuPairing? rbRatio?".
- If the answer is "Yes", the process proceeds to "Build MU candidate list (see 11142605)".
- If the answer is "No", the process branches to the right, leading to a box that states "Allocate resources to all UEs in the list SU allocation followed by subarea assignment".
From the "Build MU candidate list" box, the flow continues to "Calculate max DL MU layers (see 11142759)".
Next, there are two boxes with a green background:
1. "Initial virtual UE construction13343587:"
2. "Virtual UE construction and FD resource reservation (see 11144618, 11144070)"
After these, the flow goes to "Redistribution of free/remaining FD resources (see 11145129)".
This is followed by "Calculate Tx Power (see 11145459)".
Then, "Calculate final MCS (see 11145579)".
The penultimate step is "Fill FD scheduling info".
Finally, the flowchart ends with a black circular node, which is also connected from the "Allocate resources to all UEs..." box.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-01191757.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

[End CB015010-A]

ElseIf NRCELL.actExhaustiveScheduling is set to a value other than 1 (for DL only) or 3 (for both DL and UL)

Before execute DL pairing with HARQ initial transmission UEs as root, the PRB allocation ratio shall be calculated. When NRCELL/actRat1Alloc = true, the PRB allocation ratio is calculated as a ratio of total required PRBs for the initial transmission UEs to the total PRBs available for the slot. Note the required PRBs for each user shall be the minimum number of PRBs required to drain the buffer of one or multiple bearers the user might have. If the PRB allocation ratio is NOT less than NIDD:dlMuPairingPrbRatio, then DL pairing with initial transmission UEs as root is needed. Otherwise, DL pairing is not needed. See the detail in the below flow diagram.

[image-2][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process related to Full Duplex (FD) scheduling in a 5G network. The flowchart starts with building a MU candidate list and calculating maximum DL MU layers. It then proceeds to a decision point based on whether PDSCH subarea assignment for re-Tx users is configured.
If it is configured, the process involves performing PDSCH subarea assignment for re-Tx users. If not configured, it proceeds to virtual UE construction and RBG allocation for FD resource reservation with re-Tx UEs as root. This step is further detailed with specific algorithm references.
The flowchart then branches based on the `prbAllocRatio` compared to `NIDD:dlMuPairingPrbRatio`. If the ratio is less, it leads to a check for paired re-Tx UEs. If the ratio is not less, it checks if `actRatiAlloc` is true.
Depending on these conditions, the process either performs PDSCH subarea assignment for re-Tx users, or continues with virtual UE construction and RBG allocation for FD resource reservation with initial-Tx UEs as root.
The process then involves calculating Tx Power, calculating the final MCS, and filling FD scheduling information. There's also a path where resources are allocated to all UEs using a random allocation algorithm if configured. The flowchart concludes with a final black circle, indicating the end of the process.
The flowchart uses standard flowchart symbols:
- Rounded rectangles for start/end points.
- Rectangles for process steps.
- Diamonds for decision points.
- Arrows to indicate the flow of control.
Specific algorithm references like "SG\_UP\_ALG\_7454", "5G\_UP\_ALG\_7446", "CB008927-P", "SG\_UP\_ALG\_4504", "SG\_UP\_ALG\_7430", "SG\_UP\_ALG\_7431", "SG\_UP\_ALG\_26504", "SG\_UP\_ALG\_26505", "SG\_UP\_ALG\_7530", "SG\_UP\_ALG\_7434", "SG\_UP\_ALG\_7435", and "5G\_UP\_ALG\_4510" are mentioned throughout the flowchart.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8952.001.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

EndIf

In DL slot which has HARQ re-Tx for non-GBR, 5G-L2-PS shall execute DL pairing algorithm to build virtual UEs with re-Tx UEs as root at first. After DL pairing, 5G-L2-PS shall execute FD allocation **algorithm to allocate RBGs/PRBs for initial-Tx. After FD allocation algorithm, 5G-L2-PS shall execute DL pairing algorithm again to build virtual UEs with initial-Tx UEs as root.**

After all virtual UE construction, The number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data **for each UE is determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25267\_replaced([11145445](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksATL_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

Mixed DL DMRS types are not allowed between paired UEs; specifically, type 1 DL DMRS can only be paired with type 1 UEs, and type 2 DL DMRS can only be paired with type 2 UEs.

If NRCELL.actExhaustiveScheduling is set to a value other than 1 (for DL only) or 3 (for both DL and UL).

Below is an example why DL paring algorithm shall be executed two steps with re-Tx and initial-Tx UEs at root individually. To execute DL pairing algorithm two times can provide more MU gain. UE1 and UE2 are HARQ re-Tx. UE3 and UE4 are HARQ initial-Tx. UE1 can be paired with UE2. UE3 can be paired with UE4.

In Figures 1 and 2, DL pairing algorithm is executed one time:

- Figure 1: FD allocation alogirthm is executed, UE3 and UE4 are allocated with 2 RBGs/16 PRBs each.

- Figure 2: DL pairing algorithm is executed, UE1 and UE2 are paired. UE3 and UE4 are paired. UE4 gets 4 RBGs/64 PRBs due to pairing with UE3. UE3 gets 8 RBGs/128 PRBs (4 RBGs/64 PRBs are MU, 4 RBGs/64 PRBs are SU).

In Figures 3 and 4, DL pairing algorithm is executed two times:

- Figure 3: DL pairing algorithm with HARQ reTx UEs as root is executed. UE1 and UE2 are paired. Then FD allocation alogrithm **is executed, UE3 and UE4 are allocated with 4 RBGs/64PRBs each.**

- Figure 4: DL pairing algorithm with HARQ initTx UEs as root is executed. UE3 and UE4 are paired, they get 8 RBGs/128PRBs each due to pairing.

[image-3][image\_desc]The image displays a grid with four vertical columns labeled 1, 2, 3, and 4. Each column contains stacked colored blocks with numbers inside them.
Column 1 has four blocks: a blue block labeled "1" at the top, followed by a green block labeled "2", then an orange block labeled "3", and finally a light orange block labeled "4" at the bottom.
Column 2 has five blocks: a blue block labeled "1" at the top, a green block labeled "2", an orange block labeled "3", a light orange block labeled "4", and another orange block labeled "3" at the bottom.
Column 3 has four blocks: a blue block labeled "1" at the top, a green block labeled "2", an orange block labeled "3", and a light orange block labeled "4" at the bottom.
Column 4 has five blocks: a blue block labeled "1" at the top, a green block labeled "2", an orange block labeled "3", a light orange block labeled "4", and another orange block labeled "3" at the bottom.
The grid lines are clearly visible, and the numbers within the blocks are legible. The colors are distinct.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8952.002.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

---

### 3.10.2.0-3 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) Concept of virtual UE (ID: 11142531)

**3.10.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `12436597`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
12436597:
DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Virtual UE includes a group of UEs which are paired in spatial domain and share the same FD resource allocation. In a virtual UE, the first added UE is its root UE. One UE could be assigned to multiple virtual UEs.

[CB012971-C] For the case of DL pairing using SVD-RZF for SB BF UEs, the related virtual UE is called SVD-RZF virtual UE. One UE can only belong to one SVD-RZF virtual UE. UEs in the same SVD-RZF virtual UE may have different number of allocated PRBs for PDSCH. [End CB012971-C]

Some examples of virtual UE are listed as below. In the first case, one virtual UE includes two UEs and two FD resources are allocated to them. In the second case, one virtual UE includes three UEs and three FD resources are allocated to them. In the third case, one virtual UE only includes one UE and two FD resources are allocated to it. It’s the case that a root UE cannot be paired with any MU candidate.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains three tables. Each table has a header row and multiple data rows. The header row contains the label "RBG" and numerical values. The data rows contain labels "UE1", "UE2", and "UE3". Some cells in the tables are filled with a light green color.
Table 1:

| RBG | 0 | 1 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| UE1 |  |  |
| UE2 |  |  |
| Table 2: |  |  |

| RBG | 0 | 1 | 2 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| UE1 |  |  |  |
| UE2 |  |  |  |
| UE3 |  |  |  |
| Table 3: |  |  |  |

| RBG | 0 | 1 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| UE1 |  |  |

The size of virtual UE, [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "sizeVirtualUeA". The text is in a dark blue color and is written in a sans-serif font. The letters are slightly blurred, and there is a faint white background behind the text. The text is positioned in the center of the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8954.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1], represents the number of paired UE in virtual UE.

The number of layers of virtual UE, [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "layerNumVirtualUeA". The text is in a sans-serif font and appears to be slightly blurred. The letters are black and white with some color fringing. The text is centered in the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8954.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2], is the sum of PDSCH layers of paired UEs in virtual UE.

---

### 3.10.2.0-4 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) DL pairing group (ID: 11142569)

**3.10.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13478508`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Pairing group w/ slow pairing

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11142576`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Overview

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `13465666`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
[CB014315-B] This requirement is valid only when NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Basic'. When NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Enhanced', the pairing group algorithm is defined at [13465776: Pairing group w/o slow pairing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_GQ3-EDStEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). [End CB014315-B]

The paring group is a logical group which includes multiple large buffer UEs which can be paired by DL pairing algorithm if they are scheduled in the same slot. The pairing group is maintained by TD scheduler in non-time critical path.

The pairing group only includes SB BF UEs with large amount of data in buffer. The maximum number of UEs that can be added per pairing group is 4. When rdDlZfMuDisableRankDowngrade (see [12654318: rdDlZfMuDisableRankDowngrade](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_y1yCkEbDEfCO0aKCUF-F5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) is True, the maximum number of UEs that can be added per pairing group is 2. The maximum number of pairing groups that can be supported is 4.

The pairing group based link adaption shall be supported to reduce MCS estimation error due to SVD-RZF based DL pairing. One challenge about SVD-RZF based approach is that DL scheduler cannot accurately (or even roughly) estimate DL MU-SINR for paired UEs without knowledge of SRS channel and real-time beamforming weights. This information is placed in radio side on eCPRI 7-2e.

The initial MU-SINR estimation is done by 5G-L2-PS according to formula defined in [11143425: Calculate MU-SINR in virtual UE](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr6MjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). For each UE in a pairing group, the parameter rrmDeltaCqiDlMuZf shall be maintained to adjust pairing group specific OLLA based on last HARQ feedback of PDSCH with MU-MIMO. See the detail in [11125689: Correct average WB-CQI](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqvu6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). To simplify the link adaption implementation, the rrmDeltaCqiDlMuZf shall only be used for calculating MCS for MU-MIMO paired SB BF UEs.

When a UE is added into a pairing group, the rrmDeltaCqiDlMuZf of the new added UE shall be set to 0.

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11142557`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
**DL high performance UE**

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13478528`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
[CB014315-B] This requirement is valid only when NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Basic'. When NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Enhanced', the pairing group algorithm is defined at [13465776: Pairing group w/o slow pairing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_GQ3-EDStEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). [End CB014315-B]

If NIDD:actDlMuPairingGroup = TRUE, 5G-L2-PS shall execute below algorithm to find high buffer and static SB BF UEs which can be added into pairing group.

The algorithm is triggered when 5G-L2-PS receives DL buffer status indication from 5G-L2-LO for SB BF UE. 5G-L2-PS shall check UE’s DL buffer size and long-term CFO to decide whether the UE is eligible for DL pairing group.

IF (UE is at HIGH\_BUFFER status)

IF [DL buffer size (nonGBR) <= NIDD:lowBufferThdMuPairingGroup [PR856931] OR (long-term CFO is enabled (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3340\_replaced([11151369](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksYtq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND long-term CFO > rdDlLongTermCfoHighThd) [End PR856931] ]

The HIGH\_BUFFER status is cleared. If UE is in pairing group, the rrmPairingGroupExitTimer shall be started if it is not started.

ENDIF

ELSE

IF ((DL buffer size (nonGBR) >= NIDD:highBufferThdMuPairingGroup) and (long-term CFO is disabled (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3340\_replaced([11151369](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksYtq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) OR long-term CFO <= rdDlLongTermCfoHighThd)

The HIGH\_BUFFER status is set.

If UE is already in pairing group, the rrmPairingGroupExitTimer shall be stopped, otherwise trigger the pairing group update procedure (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_33171\_replaced([11142599](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4-aPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

ENDIF

ENDIF

About rdDlLongTermCfoHighThd, see [12447558: rdDlLongTermCfoHighThd](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_9LhLUQmOEfCT35inaBGo7g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

About rrmPairingGroupExitTimer, its duration is defined in [12582710: rdPairingGroupExitTimer](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_i0IJFDSJEfCKaNlcHOQWmg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11142587`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Remove UE from pairing group

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13465672`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
[CB014315-B] This requirement is valid only when NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Basic'. When NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Enhanced', the pairing group algorithm is defined at [13465776: Pairing group w/o slow pairing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_GQ3-EDStEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). [End CB014315-B]

A SB BF UE shall be removed from pairing group if below cases happen:

-    When the timer rrmPairingGroupExitTimer expires (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_33166\_replaced([11142557](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4-YfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the UE shall be removed from pairing group.

-    When its correlation values (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32976\_replaced([11143715](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr6zlfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) about APS based correlation) with other UEs in the same pairing group is changed, 5G-L2-PS shall check correlation values between them. If the DL pairing criteria is not met, the UE shall be removed from pairing group.

-    It is configured with SRS for WB BF.

When a UE is removed from pairing group, the pairing group update procedure (5G\_ UP\_ALG\_33171) shall be triggered.

If a pairing group only includes one UE or is empty, the pairing group shall be removed.

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11142599`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Update pairing groups

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-1.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13465675`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
[CB014315-B] This requirement is valid only when NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Basic'. When NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Enhanced', the pairing group algorithm is defined at [13465776: Pairing group w/o slow pairing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_GQ3-EDStEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). [End CB014315-B]

The pairing group update procedure shall be triggered if the status of a UE is changed as below.

* a UE is set to LARGE\_BUFFER status and it’s not in pairing group (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_33166\_replaced([11142557](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4-YfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* a UE is removed from a pairing group (5G\_UP\_ALG\_33181\_replaced([11142587](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4-ZvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

5G-L2-PS shall execute below steps to update pairing groups:

1. Build a candidate list which includes LARGE\_BUFFER UEs which are not in any pairing group or in a pairing group which only includes two UEs.
2. 5G-L2-PS shall try to add candidates into the existing groups in order of group size, starting with the group with the highest number of UEs. 5G-L2-PS shall add candidates, which meet the pairing criteria (see [12442775: Pairing criteria of pairing group](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FVnv8AjUEfCT35inaBGo7g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), into existing pairing groups.
3. If the candidate list is not empty and there is room to create new pairing group, create a new pairing group and add the first candidate in it. Otherwise, exit from the loop.
4. Add candidate(s) which meet the pairing criteria (see [12442775: Pairing criteria of pairing group](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FVnv8AjUEfCT35inaBGo7g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) into current pairing group until the group is full or no more candidates can be found.
5. If the new pairing group only includes single UE, remove the pairing group and go to the step (3).

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `12442775`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Pairing criteria of pairing group

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-1.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `13465774`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
[CB014315-B] This requirement is valid only when NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Basic'. When NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Enhanced', the pairing group algorithm is defined at [13465776: Pairing group w/o slow pairing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_GQ3-EDStEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). [End CB014315-B]

For SB BF UE, a UE is added to a group with existing UEs only if its correlation values with all UEs already in the group are not higher than the threshold NIDD:dlMuMimoZfCorrThd.

For SB BF UE, only UE which is configured with DMRS type I for PDSCH can be added in pairing group.

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13465776`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Pairing group w/o slow pairing

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13478547`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
**Overview (informative)**

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13478550`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
This requirement is valid only when NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Enhanced'.

The paring group is a logical group which includes multiple SB BF UEs that are paired in previous slots. One UE can only belong to one pairing group. 5G-L2-PS shall maintains an age time for each pairing group.

The major purposes of pairing group are listed as below:

* To boost TD scheduling priority for UEs which are suitable for DL MU pairing.
* To increase stability of DL pairing combination for OLLA in link adaption.

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13478564`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
**Create pairing group**

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13478565`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
This requirement is valid only when NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Enhanced'.

The maximum number of pairing groups per cell is defined at rdDlMuMaxPairingGroups ([13478594: rdDlMuMaxPairingGroups](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_CskBYDzSEfG0jPRAdLhzvA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).

At the end of slot(n), for each VUE, 5G-L2-PS shall create a pairing group to include paired SB BF UEs in the same VUE at slot(n) if below conditions are met:

- Same pairing group is not existed. NOTE: if same pairing group is already existed, its age time shall be reset.

- For each paired SB BF UE in the same VUE, remain DL buffer size (for nonGBR) is higher than NIDD:lowBufferThdMuPairingGroup.

For each VUE, when 5G-L2-PS creates a new pairing group, it shall execute below steps:

- Remove other pairing group(s) which include any UE in current pairing group.

- If no room to create a pairing group, 5G-L2-PS shall remove the most aged pairing group.

- Create a pairing group which includes all SB BF UEs in the same VUE at slot n.

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13478566`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Remove pairing group

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13478567`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
This requirement is valid only when NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Enhanced'.

5G-L2-PS shall remove a pairing group if DL buffer size (for nonGBR) of any UE in this group is not higher than NIDD:lowBufferThdMuPairingGroup.

5G-L2-PS shall remove a pairing group if any UE in this group is switched to WB BF.

5G-L2-PS shall remove a pairing group if correlation between any two UEs in this group is higher than correlation threshold.

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `13478599`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Select pairing group

---

**3.10.2.0-4.0-2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13478600`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
This requirement is valid only when NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Enhanced'.

In DL pre-scheduler, 5G-L2-PS shall select up to one pairing group per slot among all existed pairing groups. The pairing group selection algorithm is defined in the bucket algorithm as [12447143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_EGVwwAmBEfCT35inaBGo7g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

### 3.10.2.0-5 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) DL friend list (ID: 13339999)

**3.10.2.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `13340000`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Overview

---

**3.10.2.0-5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13340015`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
A Friend List (FL) is a logical group which shall include multiple MU paired users paired by the DL pairing algorithm in a slot. A FL is maintained per MU paired user in a cell, which shall include all the partner UEs that the user paired with in one or multiple virtual UEs. At one time, there can be multiple FLs for a user.

---

**3.10.2.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `13340001`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Add UE to Friend List

---

**3.10.2.0-5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13340016`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
gNB-DU shall perform the below procedure to add a UE to a Friend List.

* At the end of each slot “n”, MU paired users satisfying the criterion defined in  [13340003](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_UcyggNvUEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)  are marked “friends” to each other.
* These users are put in respective Friend Lists (FL) as per the pairing in this slot, which retains the pairing history for that user. One user can belong to multiple FLs.
* The number of FLs at any point of time that shall be stored for a user shall be limited and given by rdMaxFlPerUser. The FLs shall be stored chronologically within this period with the FL(s) containing the most-recent paired UEs at the top. Note: It is left to the implementation to consider the value for rdMaxFlPerUser.
* If a slot “n” does not need MU pairing, then no UEs shall be added to any FL.

---

**3.10.2.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `13340002`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Remove UE from Friend List

---

**3.10.2.0-5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13340017`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
gNB-DU shall perform the below procedure to remove a UE from a Friend List.

* When a user got scheduled and drained out in slot “n”
* The user if present shall be removed from all FLs of other users
* All the stored FLs of the user shall be dissolved.
* When an active user is not selected for scheduling for in a slot (if not included in CS1 list, for example)
* while the friend(s) got selected and scheduled, but not drained out and have pending buffer, then:
  + The FL(s) of the user not scheduled shall be carried forward as per the chronology. Rationale:Since this user was not scheduled shall be retained in the respective FL(s) with its friends from the past.
* while all friend(s) from all the FL(s) got scheduled and drained out, then:

  + all the FL(s) of the user shall be invalidated or dissolved
* When MU pairing of friends from a FL failed in a slot despite the friends being included in the to-be-scheduled UEs list, then gNB-DU shall dissolve the respective FL as the users no longer exhibit the pairing capability to remain friends further. Note that the same user could be present in another FL with another user that is not selected to be included in the to-be-scheduled UEs list in this slot, in which case it would continue to stay with its respective friends.
* [CB015010-C]If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric (See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31301\_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU overload control handler, is greater than or equal to the value set for the**activation threshold of** rdFriendListDeactOlcDlPerCent [(13365954](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_lxSsBfagEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) then gNB-DU shall
* dissolve all the FL(s) for all the UEs. [End CB015010-C]\*\*\*\*

---

**3.10.2.0-5.0-4**  (ID: `13340003`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Criteria to add UEs to Friend List

---

**3.10.2.0-5.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13426645`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric (See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31301\_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU overload control handler, is below the value set for the**deactivation threshold of** rdFriendListDeactOlcDlPerCent ([13365954](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_lxSsBfagEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) then gNB-DU shall check the following conditions to add a user to a FL:\*\*\*\*

* The user must be scheduled with DL resource allocation Type1.
* The user must be a SRS assisted WB BF MU paired user.
* The user must have enough pending data in buffer that could construct a TBS (based on current Mcs) with needed resources greater than or equal to rrmMuMinPrbNum. See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26957\_replaced([11142663](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5lcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for rrmMuMinPrbNum.
* [CB014699-E]Among the FL candidates, the user from request class criticalDrbTraffic and criticalHarqRetransDrb shall be excluded.[End CB014699-E]

---

### 3.10.2.0-6 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) Build MU candidate list (ID: 11142605)

**3.10.2.0-6.0-9**  (ID: `13420948`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
The MU candidate list, rrmMuCandidateList, includes UEs which can be paired by MU. These candidates shall meet all conditions as below:

- UEs in to-be-scheduled list (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4327\_replaced([11177617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- UE works in Basic Reliability (BR) mode in DL.

- PDSCH is scheduled only for non-GBR ReTx (request class harqRetransDrb [CB014699-E] and criticalHarqRetransDrb [End CB014699-E]) or non-GBR InitTx (request class is [CB014699-E] criticalDrbTraffic or [End CB014699-E] drbTraffic or dtxOptimizedDrbTraffic) or non-GBR InitTx multiplexed with MAC CE(s).

o If actSrsBeamFallbackByRetrx = true, then for non-GBR ReTx the beam does not fallback to legacy PMI/SSB beam. For the case of eCPRI 7-2e, this requirement doesn't apply to SB BF UEs.

o NOTE: non-GBR InitTx includes ~~both~~ [CB014699-E] the critical nonGBR InitTx, [End CB014699-E] the NBR configured nonGBR InitTx (NBR category of drbTraffic, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4178\_replaced([11174242](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuaG5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and normal nonGBR InitTx.

o NOTE: Retransmission with request class harqRetransDrb shall also consider the deprioritized GBR (and no prioritized/deprioritized DC-GBR) since they are using same request class.

o NOTE: Both Initial transmission and Retransmission(with request class harqRetransDrb) for a UE with prioritized DC-GBR data and deprioritized DC-GBR data shall be excluded from MU-MIMO pairing.

- For multiple BWP cases, DL MU-MIMO applies to below BWP:

o For UEs which have different BW capabilities, it only applies to BWP of full bandwidth.

o For multiple BWPs for power saving, it only applies to larger BWP (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1872\_replaced([11111200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpLBnfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- For CA case, DL MU-MIMO applies to UE in Pcell or Scell configured with periodic SRS or **UE in Scell** which has valid beamforming gain information that is synchronized from Pcell (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17257\_replaced([11156051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9VvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*\*\*

- Averaged CoMa (covariance matrices) of UE on vertical and horizontal directions are not aged (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6963\_replaced([11155665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxIIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), or **UE in Scell which has valid beamforming gain information that is synchronized from Pcell (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17257\_replaced([11156051](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksy9VvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

- PDSCH beams for WB BF are oversampled DFT beams (Note: For ranks 1 and 2, the best beam shall be oversampled DFT beam. For ranks 3 and 4, the best and second-best beams shall be oversample DFT beams).

- CQI > NRCELL/NRDLMUMIMO/dlMuMimoCqiThd.

NOTE: the value of CQI shall be calculated as sum of rrmAvgCqi and rrmDeltaCqi (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7557\_replaced([11125689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqvu6fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- When NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true PDSCH is scheduled with RAT1 (resource allocation type 1) else PDSCH is scheduled with RAT0 (resource allocation type 0).

- If NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = False,

allowedRbgUe(i) >= rrmMuMinRbgNum.

About allowedRbgUe(i), see its definition in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7431\_replaced([11144204](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr7arPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). NOTE: if rrmMuMinRbgNum equals to 0, it means UEs which even have no RBG budget can be considered as MU candidates. It can improve pairing possibility. The zero budget UE shall not be selected as root UE in virtual UE construction (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7430\_replaced([11144070](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr7ao_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- If NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = True,

gNB-DU shall calculate the minimum needed resource to drain the buffered bytes for this user. gNB-DU shall consider this UE as MU eligible if the calculated PRBs exceed the value define by rrmMuMinPrbNum. See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26957\_replaced([11142663](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5lcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for rrmMuMinRbgNum and rrmMuMinPrbNum.

Furthermore, for SB BF UE(i), the minimum needed PRBs to drain the buffer shall not less than dlSubbandBfSize. The dlSubbandBfSize is the configured DL subband BF size. NOTE: the reason to add this extra checking is due to L1 RU restriction on the case of allocating multiple SB BF UEs on the same BF SF. This issue can only happen under RAT1 scheme..

- If NRCELL/actDlSrsSubbandBm is set to true:

If NIDD:actDlMuPairingGroup is True,

* L2 shall maintain the latest ratio of SV1/SV3. The SV1 and SV3 are singular values reported by L1 with SVD on SRS CE. If the ratio of SV1/SV3 is less than rdSv1ToSv3Ratio ([13322105: rdSv1ToSv3Ratio](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_HO9c49EWEfCVOOJMfwsFiw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), the related UE shall be considered as NLOS UE and is not MU eligible.

[Before CB014315-B]

* SB BF UE(i) shall be considered as MU eligible for ZF pairing if it is in pairing group and its numbers of valid SRS ports on all SRS subbands are not less than rankMuUe(i).

[CB014315-B]

* The number of valid SRS ports on each SRS subbands is not less than rankMuUe(i). See [11156904: SRS quality measurement (eCPRI 7-2e only)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks4c5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
* If NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Basic', UE shall be in a pairing group.
* If NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Enhanced', LT CFO of UE shall be lower than rdLdLtCfoThdMuMimo ([13478541: rdDlLtCfoThdMuMimo](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uUR-0Ty_EfG0jPRAdLhzvA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)).
* If NIDD:subbandBfSwitchAlgo = 'Enhanced', DL buffer size of UE shall be higher than NIDD:lowBufferThdMuPairingGroup.

[End CB014315-B]

Else

If rdDlMuSbBfMode (5G\_UP\_ALG\_22164\_replaced([11149741](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksPjvPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is 0, SB BF UE is not MU eligible;

If rdDlMuSbBfMode is set to 1, SB BF UE is MU eligible and related PDSCH beams shall fallback to oversampled DFT beams when it is paired.

NOTE: for the case of eCPRI 7-2a, the above SB BF UE means UE has valid SB BWVs (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14111\_replaced([11156776](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For the case of eCPRI 7-2e, the above SB BF UE means UE is configured with SB BF.

End If

[Before CNI-142411-A]

- If If NIDD:NRCELL/NRDLMUMIMO/actExcludeLowBufferUser equals to TRUE, the UE with HARQ initial transmission shall NOT be considered as MU candidate if below DL buffer condition is met. Please NOTE, to simplify the solution, this estimation method applies to RAT1 scheme as well.

**ROUNDUP[dlDataInBufferUe(i) \* rbgSize / avgTbsPerRbgUe(i)] <= ROUNDUP{numPrbBw / MAX(1 , ROUNDUP[avgNumOfScheduledUe])}**

- dlDataInBufferUe(i): total non-GBR buffer size of UE(i) in unit of bit.

- avgTbsPerRbgUe(i): it’s TBS bit size assuming allocation of one RBG for UE(i) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4622\_replaced([11192072](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvivUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- numPrbBw: the number of PRBs in current DL BWP.

- avgNumOfScheduledUe: average number of scheduled UEs in DL slots. 5G-L2-PS shall maintain this average with the IIR filter as below:

avgNumOfScheduledUe = 0.6 \* avgNumOfScheduledUe + 0.4 \* numOfUeInDlTTI

where numOfUeInDlTTI is the number of scheduled UEs in the latest DL slot. The initial value of avgNumOfScheduledUe is 1.0.

- rbgSize: the number of PRBs per RBG.

When NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = True, the NIDD parameter NRCELL/NRDLMUMIMO/actExcludeLowBufferUser shall be set to false.

[End CNI-142411-A]

---

### 3.10.2.0-7 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) Minimum FD resources for MU pairing (ID: 11142663)

**3.10.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11142669`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
The rrmMuMinRbgNum/rrmMuMinPrbNum defines the minimum FD resource for MU pairing.

gNB-Du shall perform the check on the minimum resources for MU pairing during the inital rrmMuCandidateList preparation as described below:

* For PDSCH allocation with RAT1 (NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = True),
* gNb-Du shall set the rrmMuMinPrbNum to **[Before PR798723] 8** [PR798723] rdMuMinPrbNum (See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31569\_replaced([11149949](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **[End PR798723]PRBs for MU pairing below which the user even though, has passed the checks in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7454\_replaced([11142605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4-afvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), is deemed ineligible.**[PR788282] For transmission including MAC-CE (alone or multiplexed with DL Data), this check with rrmMuMinPrbNum shall not be performed. **[End PR788282].** [PR802102] Since this check is supposed to allow initial pairing for the user, note that gNB-DU shall use the value of the needed resource to drain the buffered bytes for this user. Thus, the user shall be removed from the rrmMuCandidateList and treated as SU user in case the needed resources for this user is below the value given by rdMuMinPrbNum. **[End PR802102]*****\******\***
* **[Before PR829066-25R1]**Rationale: With RAT1, the significance of minimum PRBs for MU pairing is to avoid pairing for UEs with smaller PRB demands lower than the size of a RBG of the largest BWP  (usally 16) to which the MU-MIMO is applicable. **[PR798723] Note if a lower value (as low as 1 PRB) is used for MU initial pairing, considerable processing load due to increase in potential number of virtual UEs per slot, can be observed. The implementation in such case is free to choose a suitable value for initial MU pairing to bring down the cpu processing load.** [End PR798723] [End PR829066-25R1]***\****\*
* When an initial Tx user is paired with a reTx Ue during the reTx MU pairing ~~that happens before the WRR, at which stage the allowedPrbUe(i) is not yet determined, the UE is allowed to be called as MU eligible and therefore further probable pairing.~~ **[PR802102] ~~However~~, when NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true, the initial Tx user shall be disallowed from pairing if the above check of rrmMuMinPrbNum fails** [End PR802102]\*\*\*\*

gNB-Du shall not perform any check on rrmMuMinPrbNum during subsequent DL pairing among the pairable users once they made into the rrmMuCandidateList based on the checks in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7454\_replaced([11142605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4-afvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the MU-WRR has estimated the needed FD resource budget for the user. This means that the FD resource budget can be as low as 0 during subsequent DL pairing. This improves DL pairing as described below:

* ~~It may so happen that for a new Tx user that is MU eligible, the allowedPrbUe(i) is as small as 0 due to assigment to a sub-area which allows maximum MU pairing for this user (atleast greater than the fair-share of PRBs for this user based on it's scheduling weight that is non-zero and greater than rrmMuMinPrbNum.~~ **[PR788282] For transmission including MAC-CE (alone or multiplexed with DL Data), this check with rrmMuMinPrbNum shall not be performed.** [End PR788282]), but still the user shall be deemed as MU-eligible.\*\*\*\*
* For PDSCH allocation with RAT0 (NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = False),
* gNB-Du can set a default value to rrmMuMinRbgNum as minimum as 0.
* **Rationale: With RAT0, the minimum resource is one RBG (usally 16 for the largest BWP).  The significance of setting rrmMuMinRbgNum is not to disallow the user to be selected as MU eligible for the first time in the rrmMuCandidateList (See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7454\_replaced([11142605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4-afvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as with RAT1, but to allow MU pairing for a zero-budget UE in general.**

Note that the zero budget UE shall not be selected as root UE in virtual UE construction (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7430\_replaced([11144070](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr7ao_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

### 3.10.2.0-8 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) DL rank adaption (ID: 11142677)

**3.10.2.0-8.0-3**  (ID: `13322050`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
5G-L2-PS shall support rank adaption algorithm which is defined in this requirement. The DL rank of MU UE(i) is defined as rankMuUe(i). The DL rank of SU UE(i) is defined as rankSuUe(i).

The concept of rank adaption is to downgrade ranks of paired UEs from 3 or 4 to rank 2. For example, one UE’s rank is 4 which needs 2 x-pol beams for transmitting PDSCH signal. If it’s paired with others in one TTI, its rank can be reduced to rank 2 which only needs 1 x-pol beam for transmitting PDSCH signal. The gain of rank downgrade can be observed in MoRSE simulation and field test we did for 5GC000524 feature. For more information, please find the slides at the link of <https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:p:/r/sites/morse/_layouts/15/Doc.aspx?sourcedoc=%7B87E6778B-0753-40E5-9DA9-28BA032C58F9%7D&file=CB008305_MoRSE_simulation_report_final.pptx&action=edit&mobileredirect=true.>

The rank adaption algorithm shall be executed when UE(i) is added into virtual UE at the first time. After the adaption algorithm is executed, the decision shall apply for UE(i) in all virtual UEs.

For SB BF UEs which are paired with SVD-RZF VUE:

[Before CB012971-F-UPD002]

- If rdDlZfMuDisableRankDowngrade = False, the rank downgrade is always enabled whatever which value is configured in NRCELL/NRDLMUMIMO/dlMuMimoRankAdaption.

- If rdDlZfMuDisableRankDowngrade = True, the rank downgrade is always disabled whatever which value is configured in NRCELL/NRDLMUMIMO/dlMuMimoRankAdaption.

- About rdDlZfMuDisableRankDowngrade, see [12654318: rdDlZfMuDisableRankDowngrade](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_y1yCkEbDEfCO0aKCUF-F5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

[CB012971-F-UPD002]

- If number of paired UEs in the same pairing group is more than 2, the rank downgrade shall be always enabled.

- If number of paired UEs in the same pairing group is 2, the rank downgrade shall be disabled if {(correlation value is NOT higher than rdDlMuZfTwoUePairingCorrelation ([13322074: rdDlMuZfTwoUePairingCorrelation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_HGM-8dEVEfCVOOJMfwsFiw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))) AND (numbers of valid SRS ports on all SRS subbands are not less than rankSuUe(i)) }, otherwise rank downgrade shall be enabled.

**[End CB012971-F-UPD002]**

For WB BF UEs which are paired with VUE, the rank downgrade is decided by below algorithm:

- If NRCELL/NRDLMUMIMO/dlMuMimoRankAdaption equals to ‘Disabled’,

- DL rank adaption is disabled, rankMuUe(i) = rankSuUe(i).

- If NRCELL/NRDLMUMIMO/dlMuMimoRankAdaption equals to ‘Always’,

- If rankSuUe(i) > 2, rank downgrade is applied (rankMuUe(i) = 2).

- Otherwise, rankMuUe(i) = rankSuUe(i).

- If NRCELL/NRDLMUMIMO/dlMuMimoRankAdaption equals to ‘Adaptive’,

- The value of rankMuUe(i) is decided in the min-max correlation algorithm. See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7436\_replaced([11143836](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr6zm_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB012971-C] For DL pairing with WB BF UEs, [End CB012971-C], to downgrade UE’s rank from high ranks to rank 2, 5G-L2-PS shall adjust beams/power/SINR/precoding for PDSCH according to below rules:

- To transmit PDSCH signal only with the best DL beam.

- The PDSCH transmission power shall be updated by removing power reduction for ranks 3 and 4. See DL power related requirements are defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2565\_replaced([11118485](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDLVvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2567\_replaced([11118493](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDLW_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- The SU-SINR in MU-SINR formula shall be compensated with the value of rrmRankDowngradeSinrAdjust. See the detail in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7440\_replaced([11143425](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr6MjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- The precoding codebook index for PDSCH (rank 2) shall be calculated from the i2 bits in PMI report according to below table.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **i2 in PMI report** **(see tables 5.2.2.2.1-7 and 5.2.2.2.1-8 in 38.214)** | **Codebook index** **(see the table 5.2.2.2.1-1 in 38.214)** |
| 0 | 0 |
| 1 | 1 |

For more information about solution of rank downgrade, please refer to the slides at the link of <https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:p:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CB/CB008000%20-%20CB008499/CFAM/CB008305%20DL%20MU-MIMO%20Enhancement/Reference%20Documents/Rank%20downgrade_v0.2.pptx?d=w525f6109193643b7bdd6f20ebee658ec&csf=1&web=1&e=y6pBI7>

---

### 3.10.2.0-9 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) Dynamic DL tapering (ID: 11142690)

**3.10.2.0-9.0-4**  (ID: `13468360`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
13468360:
DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
If DL tapering is disabled, value of rrmTaperingCompensation(i) equals to 1.0.
 
If NIDD:actDlMuPairingGroup = True, rrmTaperingCompensation(i) is always 1.0 for paired SB BF UEs. Otherwis , the DL BF gain loss shall be estimated according to below equation:
 
[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a sans-serif font. The equation is:
`rrmTaperingCompensation_i = G̃_{i,wt} / G̃_{i,w}`
The equation defines `rrmTaperingCompensation_i` as the ratio of `G̃_{i,wt}` to `G̃_{i,w}`. The tildes above the G's indicate that these are likely modified or estimated values. The subscripts `i,wt` and `i,w` suggest that these quantities are associated with a specific index `i` and possibly represent weighted (`wt`) and unweighted (`w`) components.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8977.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
where:
 
- When DL searching algorithm is ‘sequential searching’ (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11618\_replaced([11156117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kszkYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))): w is **the** best DL beam of UE(i) without tapering, wt is the related tapered beam.\*\*\*\*
- When DL searching algorithm is ‘joint searching method 1’ (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11619\_replaced([11156173](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kszkafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or ‘joint searching method 2’ (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11620\_replaced([11156247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kszkbvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):
 if rankMuUei(i) is 1 or 2, w is the best DL beam of UE(i) at ranks 1 or 2, wt is the related tapered beam.
 if rankMuUei(i) is 3 or 4, w is the stronger DL beam in selected beam pair of UE(i) at ranks 3 or 4, wt is the related tapered beam.
[CB015122-J]
-   if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1, the DL BF gain is taken from the product of rrmBNFGainTable values of [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry mathematical expression. The expression appears to be $\tilde{G}'*{i,w\_h}$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8996.010.png[/image\_path][/image-1] and [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is written in a stylized font and appears to be in a digital format. The expression is:
$\bar{G}'*{i,w}$
The expression consists of the following elements:
- A capital letter 'G'
- A prime symbol (') above and to the right of the 'G'
- A macron symbol (a horizontal bar) above the 'G'
- A subscript 'i' to the right of the 'G'
- A subscript 'w' to the right of the 'i'[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8996.011.png[/image\_path][/image-2], [11143159](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr6MifvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
[End CB015122-J]
During the cell setup procedure, L3 shall send weights of all horizontal and vertical DFT beams without tapering to 5G-L2-PS. If DL tapering is enabled, L3 shall send weights of all horizontal and vertical DFT beams with tapering to 5G-L2-PS as well. There is one-to-one mapping relationship between non-tapered and tapered beams.
 
For SU UE, gNB shall still use non-tapered beams for transmitting DL signals. For MU UE, gNB shall use tapered beams for transmitting PDSCH signal.
 
Based on simulation from MoRSE, it's not always optimal to use tapered beams for MU UEs. The benefit of tapering depends on ratio of UE's SINR and interference power. See some proprosals in the below link. Considering no optimal and doable solution can be identified in the CP2 stage. The feature will only support the simplified solution: always use tapered beams for MU UEs. It shall be improved in the future.

---

### 3.10.2.0-10 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) Max MU layer supported by L1 (ID: 11142718)

**3.10.2.0-10.0-5**  (ID: `11142751`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
The maximum number of MU layers that L1 can support in a cell is decided by the number of C4 DL subcell that 5G-L2-PS can use to schedule PDSCH per slot.

For example, in a cell, if the number of C4 subcell is N in a slot, the maximum number of MU layers that L1 can support can be calculated as rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 = N \* 4. The number of N is related with configuration of nrCellType (see 5G\_UP\_2530\_replaced([11390617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufUiI_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If DL subcell pooling is enabled, the number of DL subcell(s) per slot could be changed according to the pooling algorithm, the value of rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 shall be updated as well according to the number of DL subcell(s) per slot.

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is True and the total amount of usable DL PRB (subcell PRBs) allocated from the BBRM (numAllocCellPrb) is not greater than the total number of DL PRBs in the BW of the cell, dlBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), only one C4 DL subcell shall be used and rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 = 4.

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE, and the total number of usable PRBs for MU-MIMO allocated by the BBRM (rrmMaxNumUsableMuMimoPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) is not greater than the total number of DL PRBs in the BW of the cell, dlBandwidth (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), only one C4 DL subcell shall be used and rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 = 4.

Furthermore, the value of rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 may change during virtual UE creation based on the remaining layer PRB resources as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27790\_replaced([11145090](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr-d_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB010630-E] The above is valid for RBG based RAT0 allocation as well as PRB based RAT1 allocation schemes.[End CB010630-E]

When large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed is true and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is true,  the rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 calculation shall take the total amount of usable DL subcells allocated from the BBRM (numAllocSubcell) as N in above formula (rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 = N \* 4), instead of nrCellType.

When L1 ARM based subcell deactivation procedure is enabled in DL i.e. dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 calculation shall consider the number of Active DL Subcells received from the BBRM (numActiveDlSubcell) as N in above formula (rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 = N \* 4), instead of nrCellType. This shall be valid also when layer PRB pooling is enabled (slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE)

---

### 3.10.2.0-11 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) Max MU layer from DL buffer size (ID: 11142759)

**3.10.2.0-11.0-5**  (ID: `11143095`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
11143095:
DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
[CB008927-P] The below requirement is not valid when NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = True, and the maximum number of MU layers per slot is given by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7955\_replaced([11142718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5lefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the below R&D parameter is always disabled.[End CB008927-P]

5G-L2-PS shall estimate the maximum number of MU layers per slot, maxDlMuMimoLayer, according to DL buffer size of UEs in MU candidate list.

The algorithm shall be enabled/disabled by RD parameter (disabled by default):

- If it’s disabled, maxDlMuMimoLayer = MIN(rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1, NIDD:dlMuMaxNumLayerPerMuRbg). About the definition of rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7955\_replaced([11142718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5lefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- If it’s enabled, value of maxDlMuMimoLayer is calculated according to below algorithm:

1) Calculate normalized required PRB for each UE in rrmMuCandidateList

 For InitTx UE

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
normReqPrbUeᵢ = min ( (dlDataInBufferUeᵢ / avgTbsPerRbgUeᵢ) \* rbgSize, numPrbBw ) \* rankSuUeᵢ[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8989.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

If sliceAwareSchedulerCellActivation = True, for the computation of total non-GBR buffer size, the non-GBR and deprioritized GBR DRBs of an RG with RG weight = 0 (rrmRGWeight = 0, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7389\_replaced([11188798](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kved7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), Note: DRB is not associated with an RG or associated with an unconfigured RG is handled by default RG.) should be excluded..

the number of PRBs in current DL BWP.

End

availablePrb = numUsablePrb - usedPrb

End

numUsablePrb : rrmMaxNumUsablePrb described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

4) Calculate max allowed MU layer

maxDlMuMimoLayerDlBuff = ROUNDUP( rdDlMuLayerFactor \* normReqPrbSlot / availablePrb)

maxDlMuMimoLayer = MIN( rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1, maxDlMuMimoLayerDlBuff, NIDD:dlMuMaxNumLayerPerMuRbg)

- rdDlMuLayerFactor: it shall be implemented as a RD parameter; its default value is 1.5 (TBD).

- NIDD:dlMuMaxNumLayerPerMuRbg: it’s defined as a NIDD parameter to restrict the max number of MU layer.

- rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1: see its definition in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7955\_replaced([11142718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5lefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

* If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) = TRUE,  and subcellDeactionDlAllowed = FALSE the value of maxDlMuMimoLayer may change during virtual UE creation as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14518\_replaced([11144879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr924_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB012605-E]

* If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) = TRUE, the value of rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 may change during virtual UE creation based on the remaining layer PRB resources as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27790\_replaced([11145090](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr-d_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CB012605-E]

### 3.10.2.0-12 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) Average size of virtual UE (ID: 11143103)

**3.10.2.0-12.0-2**  (ID: `11143153`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
11143153:
DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Virtual UE size represents the number of UEs in a virtual UE. Considering a MU UE could belong to multiple virtual UE, and each virtual UE could have different size, the average virtual UE size of UE(i) shall be calculated according to below equation:

[CB008927-P] If NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = False, [End CB008927-P]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
$$ \text{avgVirtualUeSizeOfUe}*i = \text{round} \left( \frac{\sum*{A \in {\text{all virtual UEs of UE}*i}} (\text{virtualUeSize}\_A \cdot \text{allocatedRbgVirtualUe}\_A)}{\sum*{A \in {\text{all virtual UEs of UE}\_i}} \text{allocatedRbgVirtualUe}\_A} \right) $$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8992.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

- [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "allocatedRbgVirtualUe" followed by a subscript "A". The text is blurry and appears to be in a sans-serif font. The background is a light color with some subtle color variations.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8992.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]: the number of allocated RBGs of virtualUE(A).

[CB008927-P] Else,

[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
avgVirtualUeSizeOfUeᵢ = rounddown { (∑*{A∈{all virtual UEs of UEᵢ}} (VirtualUeSize\_A \* allocatedPrbVirtualUe\_A)) / (∑*{A∈{all virtual UEs of UEᵢ}} allocatedPrbVirtualUe\_A) }[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8992.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

### 3.10.2.0-13 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) Estimate DL BF gain (ID: 11143159)

**3.10.2.0-13.0-4**  (ID: `13453427`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
13453427:
DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
[CB015122-J]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The values of [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry mathematical expression. The expression appears to be $\tilde{G}'*{i,w\_h}$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8996.010.png[/image\_path][/image-0] and [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is written in a stylized font and appears to be in a digital format. The expression is:
$\bar{G}'*{i,w}$
The expression consists of the following elements:
- A capital letter 'G'
- A prime symbol (') above and to the right of the 'G'
- A macron symbol (a horizontal bar) above the 'G'
- A subscript 'i' to the right of the 'G'
- A subscript 'w' to the right of the 'i'[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8996.011.png[/image\_path][/image-1], the vertical and horizontal directional DL beam gain components, are provided by L1-DU, [13454898](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Vl6Isyw5EfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), to L2-PS for non-tapered and tapered beam set and stored in rrmBfGainTable.

The DL BF gain of UE(i) is the product of vertical and horizontal directional DL beam gain component.

i indicates the user.

else

[End CB015122-J]

The DL BF gain of UE(i) with beam w can be calculated with the below equation:

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in white text against a black background. The equation is:
$G\_{i,w} = |w^T h\_i|^2 = (w^T h\_i)(w^T h\_i)^H = w^T h\_i h\_i^H w^ *= w^H h\_i^* h\_i^T w = w^H R\_i w$

- w is vector of beamforming weight.

Considering L1 reports short-term CoMa on horizontal and vertical directions separately, 5G-L2-PS uses IIR filter to calculate long-term CoMa, and DL beams are oversample 2D-DFT beams, then the DL BF gain can be approximately calculated as below equation:

[image-5][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in white text against a black background. The equation is:
$\tilde{G}*{i,w}' = w^H \tilde{R}\_i w = (w\_v \otimes w\_h)^H (\tilde{R}*{i,v} \otimes \tilde{R}*{i,h}) (w\_v \otimes w\_h) = (w\_v^H \tilde{R}*{i,v} w\_v)(w\_h^H \tilde{R}*{i,h} w\_h)$
$= \tilde{G}*{i,w\_v}' \tilde{G}*{i,w\_h}'$
The equation involves several variables with tildes and superscripts, as well as matrix multiplication and Kronecker products (indicated by the circled cross symbol $\otimes$). The equation appears to be defining or manipulating a quantity denoted by $\tilde{G}*{i,w}'$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8996.004.png[/image\_path][/image-5]

A more general equation of DL BF gain can be defined as:

[image-14][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$\tilde{G}*{i,w}(j,m) = \delta(j) \* \tilde{G}'*{i,w}(j,m)$
The equation involves the following symbols:
- $\tilde{G}\_{i,w}(j,m)$: This likely represents a complex-valued function or a tensor with indices i, w, j, and m. The tilde above G suggests it might be a transformed or modified version of G.
- $=$: The equals sign indicates that the expression on the left is equivalent to the expression on the right.
- $\delta(j)$: This is the Dirac delta function, which is zero everywhere except at j=0, where it is infinite. It is often used to represent impulses or point sources.
- $*$: This symbol typically denotes convolution in the context of signal processing or image processing.
- $\tilde{G}'*{i,w}(j,m)$: Similar to $\tilde{G}*{i,w}(j,m)$, this is another complex-valued function or tensor. The prime symbol (') might indicate a different state or a related but distinct quantity.
In essence, the equation states that the function $\tilde{G}*{i,w}(j,m)$ is obtained by convolving the Dirac delta function $\delta(j)$ with another function $\tilde{G}'*{i,w}(j,m)$. The convolution with a Dirac delta function at j=0 effectively returns the original function, meaning $\tilde{G}*{i,w}(j,m) = \tilde{G}'*{i,w}(j,m)$ if the convolution is performed with respect to the 'j' index and $\delta(j)$ is centered at 0. However, the exact interpretation depends on the context from which this equation is taken.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8996.014.png[/image\_path][/image-14]* *The [image-15][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, close-up view of the Greek letter delta (δ) followed by the letter 'f' in parentheses, which appears to be a mathematical or scientific notation. The colors are muted and the edges are indistinct, suggesting a low-resolution or out-of-focus capture.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8996.015.png[/image\_path][/image-15] is beam power scale factor applied on the beam w associated with UE(j) (note: UE(i) and UE(j) can be the same or different UEs) .* *The value of [image-16][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, close-up view of the Greek letter delta (δ) followed by the letter 'f' in parentheses, which appears to be a mathematical or scientific notation. The colors are muted and the edges are indistinct, suggesting a low-resolution or out-of-focus capture.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8996.015.png[/image\_path][/image-16] is 1.0 by default.*\*\*\*

[image-17][image\_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression "10(-rrmRimPowerReduction/10)". The text is blurry and difficult to read.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8996.016.png[/image\_path][/image-17]

The reduction shall be applied in the slots as determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29878\_replaced([11161157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktSslPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) 'Determine RIM DL power reduction applicability'.\*\*

It shall be implemented as RD parameter with default value 1.0.
If DL tapering is enabled (see NIDD parameters of dlMuMimoTaperingH and dlMuMimoTaperingV):
- rrmDlMuSinrFactor = rrmDlMuSinrFactor / rrmTaperingCompensation(i).
- About rrmTaperingCompensation(i), see the DL tapering algorithm defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7835\_replaced([11142690](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5ldvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
If rank adaption is not disabled (see NIDD parameter of dlMuMimoRankAdaption) and UE(i)’s rank is downgraded:
- rrmDlMuSinrFactor = rrmDlMuSinrFactor / rrmRankDowngradeSinrAdjust.
- About the rank adaption algorithm, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7563\_replaced([11142677](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5ldPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
- The rrmRankDowngradeSinrAdjust shall be calculated with below formula:
rrmRankDowngradeSinrAdjust = min(2.0 \* P\_strong/P\_weak, 20)
 When DL searching algorithm is ‘sequential searching’ (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11618\_replaced([11156117](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kszkYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), P\_strong is the BF gain of the best DL beam, P\_weak is the BF gain of the second-best DL beam.
 When DL searching algorithm is ‘joint searching method 1’ (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11619\_replaced([11156173](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kszkafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or ‘joint searching method 2’ (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11620\_replaced([11156247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kszkbvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), P\_strong is the BF gain of best DL beam for ranks 1 or 2, P\_weak is the BF gain of the weak beam in beam pair for ranks 3 or 4.
 Please NOTE, in this formula, the BF gain, P\_strong and P\_weak, are BF gain of beam without DL tapering.
 For more information, please refer to
 
The MU-SINR of UE(i), in unit of dB, in virtualUE(A) can be calculated from MU-SINR of layers according to below equation.
[Before CNI-137616-B] The rrmDlMuSinrMethod shall be defined as RD parameter with default value of 0.
If rrmDlMuSinrMethod is equal to 0: [End CNI-137616-B]
 [image-8][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
muSinrUeDBA,i = 10 / rankMuUei \* Σlayer ∈ {0, ..., rankMuUei - 1} log10(muSinrUeLinearA,i,layer)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8999.009.png[/image\_path][/image-8]
[Before CNI-137616-B] If rrmDlMuSinrMethod is equal to 1:
 [image-9][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
muSinrUeDBA,i = minlayer ∈ {0, ..., rankMuUei-1} 10log10(muSinrUeLinearA,i,layer)
This formula defines a variable `muSinrUeDB` with subscripts `A,i` as the minimum value of a logarithmic function applied to `muSinrUeLinear` with subscripts `A,i,layer`. The minimum is taken over a range of `layer` values from 0 up to `rankMuUei-1`.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_8999.010.png[/image\_path][/image-9]
[End CNI-137616-B]
NOTE: a correct MU-SINR averaging could require the application of a mutual information function. A simplified version is to cut the SINR within the sum at a modulation-dependent upper limit which reflects the SINR where the raw bit error rate approaches 0. However, it might be that we don't need this finally as in practice, its performance will be measured during feature test stage.

**3.10.2.0-14.0-2**  (ID: `13477926`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
For MU pairing with ZF (option 1)

---

**3.10.2.0-14.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13477931`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
If SB BF UEs are paired with SVD-RZF in VUE(A) and rdDlMuAlgoOption = 0 ([13478075: rdDlMuAlgoOption](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_unJOQzywEfG0jPRAdLhzvA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), the linear value of MU-SINR for each UE(i) can be calculated as the below equation:

muSinrUeLinear(A, i) = rrmDlZfMuFactor/[rrmDlZfMuSinrFactor\*M/suSinrUeLinear(i) + rrmDlZfMuIntfFactor \* corrMaxVue(A, i)]

* rrmDlZfMuFactor: a factor to adjust value of MU-SINR. It shall be implemented as a RD parameter which is defined in [12581849](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_GWPNsTJ8EfCfjdcwDn2YOQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).
* rrmDlZfMuSinrFactor: a factor to adjust value of SU-SINR. It shall be implemented as a RD parameter which is defined in [12581855](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_IjIGkTJ9EfCfjdcwDn2YOQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

- rrmDlZfMuIntfFactor: a factor to adjust ratio of interference from paired UEs. It shall be implemented as RD parameter which is defined in [12581857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_O44uwDJ9EfCfjdcwDn2YOQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

* suSinrUeLinear(i): the linear value of SU-SINR which is calculated from rrmCorrAvgCqi within ILLA without OLLA correction. See [11125595: Averaging of the WB-CQI reports](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqvu4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

- corrMaxVue(A, i): maximum correlation value between UE(i) and other paired UEs in virtualUE(A).

- M: it's a rough estimation of relative power per layer due to DL pairing. It is calculated as layerNumVirtualUe(A)/rankSuUe(i). The layerNumVirtualUe(A) is the total layers number of VUE(A). The rankSuUe(i) it the rank of PDSCH for DL SU-MIMO.

---

**3.10.2.0-14.0-3**  (ID: `13478046`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
For MU pairing with ZF (option 2)

---

**3.10.2.0-14.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13478047`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
If SB BF UEs are paired with SVD-RZF in a VUE(A) and rdDlMuAlgoOption = 1 ([13478075: rdDlMuAlgoOption](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_unJOQzywEfG0jPRAdLhzvA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), the linear value of MU-SINR for each UE(i) can be calculated as the below equation:

muSinrUeLinear(A, i) = suSinrUeLinear(i) \* rrmPairingPowerLoss \* rrmZfPowerLoss

- rrmZfPowerLoss: it equals to [1 - corrSquareSum(A, i)]. The corrSquareSum(A, i) equals to square sum of correlation values between UE(i) and other UEs in VUE(A).

- rrmPairingPowerLoss: it is calculated as rankSuUe(i)/layerNumVirtualUe(A). The layerNumVirtualUe(A) is the total layers number of VUE(A). The rankSuUe(i) it the rank of PDSCH for DL SU-MIMO.

* suSinrUeLinear(i): the linear value of SU-SINR which is calculated from rrmCorrAvgCqi within ILLA without OLLA correction. See [11125595: Averaging of the WB-CQI reports](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqvu4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

---

### 3.10.2.0-15 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) Average MU-SINR (ID: 11143643)

**3.10.2.0-15.0-2**  (ID: `11143701`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
11143701:
DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Considering a UE can be paired with different ones in different virtual UE, it means this UE may have different MU-SINR on each allocated RBG. 5G-L2-PS needs to calculate average MU-SINR of allocated RBGs for each MU UE according to the below equation:
[CB008927-P] If NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = False, [End CB008927-P]
[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is for calculating the average MU SINR in dB. It is represented as:
$$ \text{avgMuSinrUeDB}*{i,dB} = \frac{\sum*{A \in {\text{all virtual UEs of UE}*i}} (\text{muSinrUe}*{A,i,dB} \* \text{allocatedRbgVirtualUe}*A)}{\sum*{A \in {\text{all virtual UEs of UE}\_i}} \text{allocatedRbgVirtualUe}\_A} $$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9002.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
- [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "allocatedRbgVirtualUeA". The text is blurry and appears to be in a sans-serif font. The background is a light color with some subtle color variations.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9002.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]: the number of allocated RBGs of virtualUE(A).
[CB008927-P] Else,
[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is for `avgMuSinrUeDBi,dB` and is defined as a fraction. The numerator is the sum over `Ae` (all virtual UEs of `UEi`) of `muSinrUeAidB` multiplied by `allocatedPrbVirtualUeA`. The denominator is the sum over `Ae` (all virtual UEs of `UEi`) of `allocatedPrbVirtualUeA`.

---

avgMuSinrUeDBi,dB = $\frac{\sum\_{A \in {all \ virtual \ UEs \ of \ UE\_i}} (muSinrUe\_{A,i,dB} \* allocatedPrbVirtualUe\_A)}{\sum\_{A \in {all \ virtual \ UEs \ of \ UE\_i}} allocatedPrbVirtualUe\_A}$

About MU-SINR estimation in virtualUE(A), see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7440\_replaced([11143425](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr6MjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
