[image-3][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a sans-serif font. The formula is:
TBS(reqPrbUeᵢ + allocatedPrbUeᵢ, UE(i)) ≥ dlDataInBufferUeᵢ
The formula appears to be related to telecommunications or network resource allocation, where:
- TBS likely stands for Transport Block Size.
- reqPrbUeᵢ represents the requested Physical Resource Blocks for User Equipment i.
- allocatedPrbUeᵢ represents the allocated Physical Resource Blocks for User Equipment i.
- UE(i) represents User Equipment i.
- dlDataInBufferUeᵢ represents the downlink data in the buffer for User Equipment i.
The formula states that the Transport Block Size for User Equipment i, considering both requested and allocated Physical Resource Blocks, must be greater than or equal to the downlink data in its buffer.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9057.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9057.007.png[/image\_path][/image-11]: the total number of allocated PRBs for UE(i) in other processed virtual UE(s).

If no value can be found in the range of {1, [image-12][image\_desc]The image contains the text "totalAllowedPrbVirtualUe". The text is in a dark color and is slightly blurry. The background is white with some light blue and yellow hues.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9057.008.png[/image\_path][/image-12]},

[image-13][image\_desc]reqPrbUe = totalAllowedPrbVirtualUeA[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9057.009.png[/image\_path][/image-13].

[image-14][image\_desc]The image depicts a diagram illustrating resource allocation. A blue rectangle labeled "allocatedPrbUe(i)" is positioned to the left, followed by an orange rectangle labeled "totalAllowedPrbVirtualUe(A)". A dashed green arrow originates from the left edge of the blue rectangle and extends to the right edge of the orange rectangle, indicating a total duration or range. NOTE: how to optimize this algorithm can be defined in CP3 (see 5G\_L2\_4441\_replaced([11166747](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_252uMPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**3.10.2.0-22.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11144718`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Allocate PRB to virtual UE

---

**3.10.2.0-22.0-2.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `12520440`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
12520440:
DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
3) Allocate PRB to virtual UE

[CB012971-C] For the case of SVD-RZF VUE for pairing SB BF UEs, the number of PRB that can be allocated to virtualUE(A) is the maximum number of requested PRB among all UEs in virtualUE(a).

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a bar chart illustrating resource allocation for virtual UEs. The chart displays four bars labeled "reqPrbUe(1)", "reqPrbUe(2)", "reqPrbUe(3)", and "reqPrbUe(4)". The bars are of varying lengths, with "reqPrbUe(4)" being the longest and "reqPrbUe(1)" being the shortest. Above the bars, two dashed green arrows indicate ranges labeled "totalAllowedRbgVirtualUe(A)" and "reqRbgVirtualUe(A)". The "totalAllowedRbgVirtualUe(A)" arrow spans the entire width of the chart, while the "reqRbgVirtualUe(A)" arrow spans a slightly shorter width. Two dashed red vertical lines mark the rightmost extent of the "totalAllowedRbgVirtualUe(A)" and "reqRbgVirtualUe(A)" ranges. The bars are colored in shades of orange and blue.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04141629.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

For other cases, [End CB012971-C] the number of PRB that can be allocated to virtualUE(A) is the minimum number of requested PRB among all UEs in virtualUE(A). All the UEs shall belong to the same PDSCH subarea. The equation is defined as below:

[image-1][image\_desc]reqPrbVirtualUe\_A = min\_{i ∈ A} reqPrbUe\_i[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9060.001.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

[image-2][image\_desc]The image displays a Gantt chart illustrating resource allocation for four user equipment (UE) entities, labeled reqPrbUe(1) through reqPrbUe(4). The chart uses horizontal bars to represent the duration of resource allocation for each UE.
- **reqPrbUe(1)** is allocated resources for a shorter duration, starting at the beginning of the chart and ending before the second vertical red dashed line. A portion of its allocated time is shown in blue, while the remaining allocated time is represented by a white space.
- **reqPrbUe(2)** is allocated resources for a longer duration than reqPrbUe(1), starting at the beginning of the chart and ending before the rightmost edge of the chart. Its allocation is shown in orange.
- **reqPrbUe(3)** is allocated resources for a duration shorter than reqPrbUe(2) but longer than reqPrbUe(1). Its allocation is shown in orange.
- **reqPrbUe(4)** is allocated resources for the longest duration among all UEs, starting at the beginning of the chart and extending to the rightmost edge. Its allocation is shown in orange.
Two vertical red dashed lines divide the chart into segments, indicating specific points in time. Green dashed arrows above the chart indicate time intervals. The top green arrow spans the entire width of the chart, while the lower green arrow spans a shorter duration, aligning with the end of the blue portion of reqPrbUe(1)'s allocation.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9060.002.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is True and layerNumVirtualUeA(5G\_UP\_ALG\_7444\_replaced([11142531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) > 4 and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is False.

* apply PRB allocation limit, rrmPrbAllocLimitToVue, computed in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14517\_replaced([11144909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr925_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to the reqPrbVirtualUeA and update the PRB allocation as below:

reqPrbVirtualUeA = min{rrmPrbAllocLimitToVue, reqPrbVirtualUeA }

End

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE, the PRB allocation is further limited by the available number of layer PRBs for MU-MIMO.

The PRB allocation is updated as below :

**reqPrbVirtualUe**A **= min{reqPrbVirtualUeA, vUeReqLayerPrbBasedAllocLimit}**\*\*\*\*

where,

vUeReqLayerPrbBasedAllocLimit is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27774\_replaced([11145109](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr_FAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

End

---

**3.10.2.0-22.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `11144752`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Update PRB status for each UE in virtual UE

---

**3.10.2.0-22.0-2.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `12504430`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
12504430:
DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
4) Update PRB status for each UE in virtual UE

- [image-0][image\_desc]allocatedPrbUeᵢ = allocatedPrbUeᵢ + reqPrbVirtualUeᵢ[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9062.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

**If root UE is HARQ re-Tx UE:**

- For each HARQ re-Tx UE, [image-1][image\_desc]allowedPrbUe = allowedPrbUe - reqPrbVirtualUe[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9062.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]. If allowedPrbUe(i) = 0, remove UE(i) from rrmMuCandidateList.

- For each HARQ initial-Tx UE, [CB014861-B] If NRCELL.actExhaustiveScheduling is set to a value other than 1 (for DL only or 3 (for both DL and UL) [End CB014861-B] no update on allowedPrbUe because its value is 0 before WRR algorithm [CB014861-B] else allowedPrbUe is already calculated in step1 [End CB014861-B]. It’s piggyback pairing with re-Tx UE. If DL buffer of UE(i) is drained out completely, remove it from rrmMuCandidateList.

If sliceAwareSchedulerCellActivation = True, DL buffer of UE(i) should exclude initial-Tx of non-GBR DRBs and deprioritized GBR DRBs of a resource group (RG) with RG weight = 0 (rrmRGWeight = 0, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7389\_replaced([11188798](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kved7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), Note: DRB is not associated with an RG is handled by default RG.

**If root UE is HARQ initial-Tx UE:**

- Calculate remaining PRBs of virtual UE(A):

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
`remainPrbVirtualUe_A = sum_{i in A} (allowedPrbUe_i - reqPrbVirtualUe_A)`[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9062.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

- The set A’ includes all UE(s) in virtualUE(A) which meet condition of reqPrbUe(i) = reqPrbVirtualUe(A).

- Distribute remaining PRBs, remainPrbVirtualUe(A), to all UEs (excluding UEs in the set A’) in virtualUE(A) equally. Please note, remainPrbVirtualUe(A) could be negative or positive values, the algorithm about how to distribute remaining PRBs to these UEs can be optimized in CP3.**If remainPrbVirtualUe(A) is still positive and there are no more UEs (excluding UEs in the set A’) in virtualUE(A), then the virtual UE construction shall be over and the PRBs worth remainPrbVirtualUe(A), shall be made available as free PRBs for other UEs (as SU or vUE).**

- For each UE in the set A’, set allowedPrbUe = 0.

---

**3.10.2.0-22.0-2.0-6**  (ID: `11144778`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Update remaining cell PRBs for MU-MIMO with Layer PRB pooling

---

**3.10.2.0-22.0-2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11144784`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE, RBG allocation for MU-MIMO is additionally constrained by the available layer PRB preocessing capacity.

gnB shall always ensure that the sum of layer PRB capacity required for the allocated PRBs to all virtual UEs and PRBs allocated to SU-MIMO UEs including broadcasting does not exceed the available layer PRB capacity per slot (rrmMaxNumLayerPrbPerSlot; refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The remaining cell PRBs defined as rrmRemainingCellPrbForMuMimo is intialised and updated as follows :

Before the contruction of the first virtual UE, rrmRemainingCellPrbForMuMimo is initialised as :

rrmRemainingCellPrbForMuMimo = rrmMaxNumUsablePrb - rrmNonMuAllocatedCellPrb

where,

* rrmMaxNumUsablePrb is the number of available cell PRBs based on the layer PRBs allocated to the cell by the BBRM in the current pooling period (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* rrmNonMuAllocatedCellPrb: the total number of cell PRBs allocated in the slot to all UEs not in the rrmMuCandidateList (as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4500\_replaced([11179300](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku4oDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) including broadcast UEs.

Once initialised, after every virtual UE allocation, rrmRemainingCellPrbForMuMimo shall be updated as :

rrmRemainingCellPrbForMuMimo = max {0, (rrmRemainingCellPrbForMuMimo - reqPrbVirtualUeA))}

where,

* reqPrbVirtualUeA is the number of PRBs allocated to the virtual UE (A) (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26514\_replaced([11144718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr9P0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

**3.10.2.0-22.0-2.0-7**  (ID: `11144828`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Example

---

**3.10.2.0-22.0-2.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `12506414`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
12506414:
DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
[CB014861-B] The following is not applicable when NRCELL.actExhaustiveScheduling is set to 1 (for DL only) or 3 (for both DL and UL) [End CB014861-B]
Following is a list of UEs (for simplicity purpose only new Tx users are considered) with respective scheduling weights, maximum needed PRBs, MU eligibility. The maximum needed PRBs for each user is based on the buffered data and the MCS derived from corrected average Cqi based on SU-SINR.
[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a table with five columns and nine rows. The columns are labeled "UEs in descending order of tdmetric", "Is Mu eligible", "PRB\_Max", and "Sched Wt". The first column lists user equipment identifiers (MS1, MS0, MS4, MS5, MS3, MS8, MS9, MS7). The second column indicates whether each UE is eligible for "Mu" (Y for yes, N for no). The third column shows a numerical value for "PRB\_Max", and the fourth column shows a numerical value for "Sched Wt". The table appears to be a snapshot of data related to network resource allocation or scheduling.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9070.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
 
There are two subareas SA0 and SA1 respectively with sizes 140 and 150. The intention of this exampe is to demonstrate the PDSCH subarea assignments to users and pairing.
 
Step-1: Sort the users as specified in step 2 of the WRR algorithm specified under 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23755\_replaced([11179805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku7ET_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
 
Step-2: Start the WRR for the users and derive the number of reservable PRBs for each user as specified in step 3 of the WRR algorithm specified under 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23755\_replaced([11179805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku7ET_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
 
Step-3: Assign the best suitable subarea for each user, MU or non-MU as per the rules specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26464\_replaced([11176645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuqllvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_23683\_replaced([11176637](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuqllPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The MU users are placed such that:
- MS0, MS3, MS4 can be paired
- MS3, MS4, MS9 can be paired
 
Step-4: For the SU users the reservation and subarea assignments ends here. For the MU users, the allowedPrbUe(i) is set to the initial number of PRBs to start the MU pairing.
 
At the end following is the PDSCH subarea allocation and occupancy.
The yellow boxes against each row for a user, shows the reserved #PRBs for non-MU users which happens to be in SA0 in this example.
The blue boxes against each row for a user, shows the reserved #PRBs (initial PRBs to start the pairing) for the MU users which happens to be in SA1 in this example.
With each user reserved in a respective SA, the remaining PRBs in the SA are reduced and that is tracked in the yellow boxes for SA0 and blue boxes for SA1 at the top.
 
[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a spreadsheet with several columns and rows, displaying data related to mobile stations (MS) and their metrics. The data appears to be organized for resource allocation or scheduling purposes.

### 3.10.2.0-23 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) Restriction due to stream PRB Pooling (ID: 11144852)

**3.10.2.0-23.0-1**  (ID: `11144856`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Overview

---

**3.10.2.0-23.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11144872`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
With PRB Pooling and MU-MIMO enabled, the maximum amount of layer/stream PRB L1 processing capacity available per cell is limited by the total amount of subcells PRBs granted to the cell by the BBRM (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For each physical cell RBG/PRBs allocated to MU-paired UEs, the required amount of layer/stream PRB processing with MU-MIMO depends on whether the Paired UEs are scheduled on one or more than one subcells and the corresponding amount of subcell PRBs needed.

* Example. the same amount of physical cell RBG/PRBs allocated for MU-paired UEs would require up to twice layer/stream PRB processing capacity (subcell PRBs) if scheduled on two subcells compared to one subcell.
* If rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 = 4 (only one subcell is used)  (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7955\_replaced([11142718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5lefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), MU-paired UEs (if any) are always scheduled on one subcell, hence, the amount of subcell PRBs required for these MU-paired UEs is the same as the physical Cell PRBs allocated to them, RBG/PRB allocation behaviour is same as the legacy and no additional condition is needed with PRB pooling for the RBG/PRB allocation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7431\_replaced([11144204](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr7arPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* If rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 [Before CB013288-B-UPD001] = 8 (two subcells are used) [CB013288-B-UPD001] > 4 (more than one subcell is used) [End CB013288-B-UPD001],  however, scheduling MU-paired UEs with layerNumVirtualUeA (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7444\_replaced([11142531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) > 4 (if any) on multiple subcells requires to have availability of sufficient amount of subcell PRBs in the cell to support the MU-paired UEs in rrmMuCandidateList (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7454\_replaced([11142605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4-afvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Hence, for this case both the available physical and subcell PRB amount shall be determined (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14518\_replaced([11144879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr924_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and additional check conditions are defined (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14517\_replaced([11144909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr925_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[CB013288-B-UPD001] Additionally, the maximum number of subcells and subsequently the maximum number of layers available for every MU-MIMO UE shall also be determined and updated as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29907\_replaced([11145007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr-d8_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[End CB013288-B-UPD001]

When large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is True and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is True, with PRB/subcell pooling and MU-MIMO enabled, it always has sufficient subcell PRBs granted to the cell by the BBRM (5G\_UP\_ALG\_13411\_replaced([11212398](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). For each physical cell RBG/PRBs allocated to MU-paired UEs, no additional conditions need to be checked, the legacy MU-MIMO virtual UE RBG/PRB allocation (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7431\_replaced([11144204](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr7arPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is applicable.

[CB013288-B-UPD001]

Note : Please update the ACSCT/M flag in the next release based version of the requirement and remove this Note

[End CB013288-B-UPD001]

---

**3.10.2.0-23.0-2**  (ID: `11144879`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Available FD Subcell Resources for MU-MIMO with PRB Pooling

---

**3.10.2.0-23.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11144902`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
This section is valid only if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is True and layerNumVirtualUeA(5G\_UP\_ALG\_7444\_replaced([11142531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) > 4 and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is False.

This section is computed only if rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7955\_replaced([11142718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5lefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [Before CB013288-B-UPD001] = 8 (two subcells are used) [CB013288-B-UPD001] > 4 (more than one subcell is used) [End CB013288-B-UPD001] in the cell during the slot. If so, the availability of both physical and subcell PRBs (subcell Resources) shall be checked before and during MU-MIMO pairing as described below.

1.  L2PS shall ensure that the total amount of subcell PRBs consumed by all RBGs when PDSCH is allocated with RAT0 or simply in terms of PRBs when PDSCH is allocated with RAT1 with NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true allocated to UEs in rrmMuCandidateList (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7454\_replaced([11142605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4-afvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), shall not exceed the usable subcell PRB limit, rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb, available in the slot for rrmMuCandidateList. Thus, before any virtual UE construction, the amount of usable physical cell PRBs, rrmMuAvailableNumCellPrb, and subells PRBs, rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb, available in the slot for UEs in the rrmMuCandidateList shall be determined, as below:

* rrmMuAvailableNumCellPrb      = rrmNumUsableCellPrbPerSlot - rrmNonMuAllocatedNumPrb;

[Before CB013288-B-UPD001]

* rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb = min {numAllocCellPrb - rrmNonMuAllocatedNumPrb, 2\*rrmMuAvailableNumCellPrb};

[CB013288-B-UPD001]

* rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb = min {numAllocCellPrb - rrmNonMuAllocatedNumPrb, numSubcells\*rrmMuAvailableNumCellPrb};

[End CB013288-B-UPD001]

where:

* rrmNumUsableCellPrbPerSlot: determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4278\_replaced([11176996](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kurzv_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for each slot types considering PRB pooling restriction.
* numAllocCellPrb: total subcell PRBs allocated to the cell by the BBRM (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* rrmNonMuAllocatedNumPrb: When PDSCH is allocated with RAT0 the total number of PRBs within all RBGs allocated in the slot excluding the RBGs available to UEs in rrmMuCandidateList (as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4500\_replaced([11179300](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku4oDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  or simply rrmNonMuAllocatedNumPrb when PDSCH is allocated with RAT1 with NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true.

[CB013288-B-UPD001]

* numSubcells : When L1 ARM based subcell deactivation procedure is enabled in DL i.e. dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), consider the number of Active DL Subcells received from the BBRM (numActiveDlSubcell) at the beginning of the pooling period, else consider the number of subcells related with configuration of nrCellType (see 5G\_UP\_2530\_replaced([11390617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufUiI_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[End CB013288-B-UPD001]

Note: UEs not in rrmMuCandidateList are scheduled on one subcell (in SU-MIMO mode), thus, the amount of the subcellPRB they use is the same as the number of physical PRBs within the RBGs when PDSCH is allocated with RAT0 or simply the physical PRBs otherwise with NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true, allocated to the UEs (rrmNonMuAllocatedNumPrb).

2. Before each virtual UE creation (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7430\_replaced([11144070](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr7ao_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

* the total amount of subcell/cell PRB resources available before any virtual UE creation is determined as below:

-if virtual UE creation is to be done for the first time in the slot, the values of the rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb/rrmMuAvailableNumCellPrb initialized in (1) are used, afterwards the values of these parameters which are updated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14950\_replaced([11144944](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr927PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be used.

* despite the availability of two [CB013288-B-UPD001]or more[End CB013288-B-UPD001] subcells with rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 [Before CB013288-B-UPD001] = 8 [CB013288-B-UPD001] > 4 [End CB013288-B-UPD001](5G_UP_ALG_7955_replaced([11142718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5lefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the maximum number of allowed subcells that can be used for the next virtual UE scheduling [CB013288-B-UPD001](maxNumAvailableSubcells)[End CB013288-B-UPD001] shall be restricted by comparing the total amount of available subcells PRBs and physical cell PRBs as [Before CB013288-B-UPD001]below :[CB013288-B-UPD001]described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29907\_replaced([11145007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr-d8_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[End CB013288-B-UPD001]

[Before CB013288-B-UPD001]

-if NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = false AND (rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb - rrmMuAvailableNumCellPrb) < rbgSize;

else,

* if NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true AND (rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb - rrmMuAvailableNumCellPrb) < rrmMuMinPrbMargin
* only single subcell is allowed to use,
* the maximum layer per a virtual UE to be created (if any) will be restricted by the single subcell, thus the value of maxDlMuMimoLayer (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7446\_replaced([11142759](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr6MgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be restricted up to 4 as below:

maxDlMuMimoLayer = min {maxDlMuMimoLayer ,4},

otherwise, no restriction (up to two subcells can be used)

-where: rbgSize is the number of PRBs per RBG for RAT0, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4459\_replaced([11178370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2LwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

: rrmMuMinPrbMargin is the number of PRBs needed for MU eligibility, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26957\_replaced([11142663](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5lcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CB013288-B-UPD001]

[CB013288-B-UPD001]

Note : Please update the ACSCT/M flag in the next release based version of the requirement and remove this Note

[End CB013288-B-UPD001]

---

**3.10.2.0-23.0-3**  (ID: `11144909`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Condition Check for Allocating RBG to virtual UE with PRB Pooling

---

**3.10.2.0-23.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11144937`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
-Before allocating RBGs/PRBs to a virtual UE (virtualUE(A)) in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11855\_replaced([11144425](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr8Bt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = false or 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26514\_replaced([11144718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr9P0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true, if layerNumVirtualUeA(5G\_UP\_ALG\_7444\_replaced([11142531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) > 4, L2PS shall compute the maximum number of RBG/PRB limit that can be allocated to the virtual UE as below:

If NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = false, then;

[Before CB013288-B-UPD001]

rrmRbgAllocLimitToVue = floor((rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb - rrmMuNumAvailableCellPrb)/rbgSize) + nLastRbg

[CB013288-B-UPD001]

//Limit based on FD resources

* rrmRbgAllocLimitToVue = floor(rrmMuNumAvailableCellPrb/rbgSize)

//Limit further based on Spatial domain resource availability

* rrmRbgAllocLimitToVue = min{floor((rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb - ((β - 1) \* rrmMuNumAvailableCellPrb))/rbgSize), rrmRbgAllocLimitToVue}

End If

* rrmRbgAllocLimitToVue = rrmRbgAllocLimitToVue + nLastRbg

[End CB013288-B-UPD001]

Else,

[Before CB013288-B-UPD001]

rrmPrbAllocLimitToVue = rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb - rrmMuNumAvailableCellPrb

[CB013288-B-UPD001]

//Limit based on FD resources

* rrmPrbAllocLimitToVue = rrmMuNumAvailableCellPrb

//Limit further based on Spatial domain resource availability

* rrmPrbAllocLimitToVue = min{(rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb - ((β - 1) \* rrmMuNumAvailableCellPrb)), rrmPrbAllocLimitToVue}

Where:

* β (the number of subcells required for the virtual UE) is defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29902\_replaced([11144994](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr-d8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CB013288-B-UPD001]

If NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = false, then;

[Before CB013288-B-UPD001]

if (last RBG is already used) or (rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb – rrmMuNumAvailableCellPrb) mod rbgSize) < lastRbgSize

[CB013288-B-UPD001]

[Before CB013288-B-UPD002]

if (last RBG is already used) or (rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb – ((maxNumAvailableSubcells - 1) \* rrmMuNumAvailableCellPrb)) mod rbgSize) < lastRbgSize

[CB013288-B-UPD002]

if (last RBG is already used) or (rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb – ((maxNumAvailableSubcells - 1) \* rrmMuNumAvailableCellPrb)) mod rbgSize) < [PR808053](maxNumAvailableSubcells - 1) \*[End PR808053] lastRbgSize

[End CB013288-B-UPD002]

[End CB013288-B-UPD001]

nLastRbg = 0

else

nLastRbg = 1

* where:

rbgSize is the number of PRBs per RBG for RAT0, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4459\_replaced([11178370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2LwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

lastRbgSize is the number of PRBs in last RBG for RAT0

[CB013288-B-UPD001]

maxNumAvailableSubcells : Maximum number of subcells that can be used for the current virtual UE allocation (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14518\_replaced([11144879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr924_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) &  5G\_UP\_ALG\_29907\_replaced([11145007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr-d8_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Note : Please update the ACSCT/M flag in the next release based version of the requirement and remove this Note

[End CB013288-B-UPD001]

**3.10.2.0-23.0-4**  (ID: `11144944`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Update Available FD Subcell Resource PRB Pooling

**3.10.2.0-23.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `11144988`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
11144988:
DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
The value of rrmMuReqNumSubcellPrb and rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb shall be updated before RBG/PRB allocation is started to a virtual UE, as follows based on the RBG/PRB allocation made to the previous virtual UE:

* rrmMuAvailableNumCellPrb and rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb : updated every time after RBG/PRB allocation in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7431\_replaced([11144204](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr7arPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is done sucessfully in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7431\_replaced([11144204](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr7arPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The value of rrmMuAvailableNumCellPrb/rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb considered in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14517\_replaced([11144909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr925_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) during the current virtual UE RBG allocation is updated during the previous RBG/PRB allocation as shown below:
* remaining physical cell PRB update:

if NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = false;

rrmMuNumAvailableCellPrb = rrmMuNumAvailableCellPrb - PRB (reqRbgVirtualUeA)

if NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true,

rrmMuNumAvailableCellPrb = rrmMuNumAvailableCellPrb - reqPrbVirtualUe

* remaining subcell PRB update:

if NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = false;

rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb = min⁡ {rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb - β*PRB (reqRbgVirtualUeA), [Before CB013288-B-UPD001]2[CB013288-B-UPD001]numSubcells[End CB013288-B-UPD001]*rrmMuAvailableNumCellPrb}

else

rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb = min⁡ {rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb - β*reqPrbVirtualUeA, [Before CB013288-B-UPD001]2[CB013288-B-UPD001]numSubcells[End CB013288-B-UPD001]*rrmMuAvailableNumCellPrb}

* where:
* PRB (x): returns the number PRBs available within RBG x when NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = false.

[CB013288-B-UPD002]

Note : The PRB function should consider also the difference in the number of PRBs in the partial/last RBG

[End CB013288-B-UPD002]

* if NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = false [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains the text "reqRbgVirtualUeA". The text is blurry and appears to be in a sans-serif font. The background is a light color, possibly white or off-white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9087.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] : allocated RBG to virtual UE A while being processed 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11855\_replaced([11144425](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr8Bt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* if NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true, [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "reqPrbVirtualUeA". The text is in a dark color and appears to be slightly blurred. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9087.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]: allocated PRB to virtual UE A while being processed, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26505\_replaced([11144618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr8oyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[Before CB013288-B-UPD001]

* β = 2: if layerNumVirtualUeA (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7444\_replaced([11142531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))>4,  and is to be scheduled on two subcells (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7955\_replaced([11142718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5lefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), otherwise β = 1:

[CB013288-B-UPD001]

* numSubcells : When L1 ARM based subcell deactivation procedure is enabled in DL i.e. dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), consider the number of Active DL Subcells received from the BBRM (numActiveDlSubcell) at the beginning of the pooling period, else consider the number of subcells related with configuration of nrCellType (see 5G\_UP\_2530\_replaced([11390617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufUiI_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* β = The number of subcells used by the virtual UE defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29902\_replaced([11144994](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr-d8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CB013288-B-UPD001]

* rrmMuReqNumSubcellPrb: is updated right before step 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11855\_replaced([11144425](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr8Bt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the current virtual UE, as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14518\_replaced([11144879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr924_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) based on the current UEs in rrmMuCandidateList.

**3.10.2.0-23.0-5**  (ID: `11144994`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Determine the number of subcells used by virtual UE

---

**3.10.2.0-23.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11145001`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
[Before CB013288-B-UPD002]

For every virtual UE (vUE), the number of subcells that it would use depends on the number of layers required by the virtual UE (layerNumVirtualUeA). It is defined as below :

* Number of subcells used by virtual UE : β = roundup{layerNumVirtualUeA (5G\_UP\_ALG\_7444\_replaced([11142531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) / Maximum number of layers that can be used in the primary subcell of the cell (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8985\_replaced([11212013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))}

Where:

* The subcell type of the primary subcell for a cell is defined by the nrCellType (5G\_UP\_2530\_replaced([11390617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufUiI_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[CB013288-B-UPD002]

For every virtual UE (vUE), the number of subcells used is defined as below :

* Number of subcells used by virtual UE : β = the number of unique subcells that will be used for allocating all the UEs in the virtual UE vUE (Subcell allocation for a UE can be checked in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4327\_replaced([11177617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End CB013288-B-UPD002]

---

**3.10.2.0-23.0-6**  (ID: `11145007`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Maximum layers & subcell limit with Stream  PRB Pooling

---

**3.10.2.0-23.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11145014`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2268\_replaced([11692786](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3pqm_9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is True and layerNumVirtualUeA(5G\_UP\_ALG\_7444\_replaced([11142531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) > 4 and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_2387\_replaced([11692644](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_D3n1Yf9nEe-D3seUwaI0tg))) is False, the remaining subcell PRBs available for MU-MIMO pairing shall determine [PR808053]the maximum number of subcells to be used by each virtual UE (maxNumAvailableSubcells) and[End PR808053] the maximum number of layer to be used for a transmission[PR808053](i.e. the maximum number of layers during virtual UE construction (refer 5G_UP_ALG_7430_replaced([11144070](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr7ao_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))), thus also restricting the number of subcells to be used (maxNumAvailableSubcells). This also causes restrictions on the maximum number of layers during virtual UE construction (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7430\_replaced([11144070](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr7ao_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).[End PR808053]

The constraints mentioned below shall be used considered before every virtual UE construction in a slot.

Based on the available number of subcell PRB resources (rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb; refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14518\_replaced([11144879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr924_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the PRBs available after every virtual UE allocation (rrmMuAvailableNumCellPrb; refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14518\_replaced([11144879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr924_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

* minMuPrbSize = rbgSize

If NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = true, then;

* minMuPrbSize = rrmMuMinPrbMargin

End If

* additionalSubcell = 0

If (mod(rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb, rrmMuAvailableNumCellPrb) > minMuPrbSize), then;

* additionalSubcell = 1

End If

maxNumAvailableSubcells = min{numSubcells, (floor(rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb / rrmMuAvailableNumCellPrb) + additionalSubcell)}

[PR808053]

gnB-DU shall ensure that

Number of subcells used by virtual UE : β (defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29902\_replaced([11144994](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr-d8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) <= maxNumAvailableSubcells

[End PR808053]

Subsequently, based on the maximum number of available subcells, the maximum number of allowed layers shall be updated as follows :

rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 = maxNumAvailableSubcells \* Maximum number of layers that can be used in the primary subcell of the cell (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8985\_replaced([11212013](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw-5wPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

layerNumVirtualUeA <= rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1

where,

* rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb is the available number of subcell PRB resources in the cell as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14518\_replaced([11144879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr924_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmMuAvailableNumCellPrb is the remaining number of cell/physical PRBs for MU-MIMO allocation as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14518\_replaced([11144879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr924_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rbgSize is the number of PRBs per RBG for RAT0, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4459\_replaced([11178370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2LwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmMuMinPrbMargin is the number of PRBs needed for MU eligibility, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26957\_replaced([11142663](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5lcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* numSubcells : When L1 ARM based subcell deactivation procedure is enabled in DL i.e. dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), consider the number of Active DL Subcells received from the BBRM (numActiveDlSubcell) at the beginning of the pooling period, else consider the number of subcells related with configuration of nrCellType (see 5G\_UP\_2530\_replaced([11390617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufUiI_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayer is the maximum number of MU layers that L1 can support in a cell as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7955\_replaced([11142718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5lefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* The subcell type of the primary subcell for a cell is defined by the nrCellType (5G\_UP\_2530\_replaced([11390617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufUiI_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* layerNumVirtualUeA is the summed rank of all UEs in the virtual UE (A) defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7444\_replaced([11142531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB013288-B-UPD001]

Note : Please update the ACSCT/M flag in the next release based version of the requirement and remove this Note

[End CB013288-B-UPD001]

---

**3.10.2.0-23.0-7**  (ID: `11145023`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Examples: MU-MIMO with PRB Pooling when PDCH is allocated with RAT0

---

**3.10.2.0-23.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11145028`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Example:#1

---

**3.10.2.0-23.0-7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11145039`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
11145039:
DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
This example explains how to allocate RBG to virtual UEs step by step, there are 5 UEs in one slot with below assumptions:

 UE1 can be paired with UE2 and UE3.

 UE3  can be paired with UE4.

 UE4 can be paired with UE5.

 UE1 is HARQ re-Tx UE, others are initial-Tx UEs.

 UE2 has limited buffer data for 3RBGs.

 Total number of RBGs is 17.

 UE1 has 5 RBGs for HARQ re-Tx.

* Rank of UEs: UE1=rank2, UE2=rank4, UE3 =rank2, UE4=rank4, UE5=rank4,
* rrmNonMuAllocatedNumPrb =0
* rrmNumUsableCellPrbPerSlot  = 272
* numAllocCellPrb = 352
* PRB (#RBG) = #RBG\*rbgSize  : mapping function from RBG to PRB and rbgSize  = 16

numAllocCellPrb > dlBandwidth (two subcells), thus, 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14518\_replaced([11144879](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr924_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))  additional check is needed (1) MU available resoruces per slot

rrmMuAvailableNumCellPrb = 272, rrmMuAvailableNumSubcellPrb =352

Algorithms Steps:

* During Step#1/2 : ReTx UE1 is used as a root UE
* MU-WRR is run before beginning of Step#3 and resulting allocations for each UE is as follows:
* UE3=3 RBGs, UE4=4RBGs, and UE5=5RBGs

The sixth row contains the text "HARQ ReTransmission" in the first column and is otherwise empty. The remaining rows are filled with colored cells, some of which are green and some are light yellow. The last column has the label "SU-MIMO" in the fifth row.

| vUE1[p=2] | vUE2[p=1] | vUE 3[p=2] | vUE4[p=1] | vUE5[p=1] | SU-MIMO |

### 3.10.2.0-24 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) Restriction due to layer PRB Pooling (ID: 11145064)

**3.10.2.0-24.0-1**  (ID: `11145070`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Overview

---

**3.10.2.0-24.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11145084`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
With layer PRB Pooling and MU-MIMO enabled, the maximum amount of layer/stream PRB L1 processing capacity available per cell is limited by the layer PRBs granted to the cell by the BBRM (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25709\_replaced([11214021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLHCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The number of layer PRBs consumed by each virtual UE depends on the total rank of the virtual UE (refer layerNumVirtualUeA in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7444\_replaced([11142531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the number of [Before CB010630-E]RBGs[CB010630-E]FD resources (RBGs in case of RAT0 based allocation scheme; PRBs in case of RAT1 based allocation scheme)[End CB010630-E] allocated to the virtual UE.

Such constraints lead to a restriction in the maximum number of layers that can be supported in a virtual UE, thus also causing a change in the number of subcells that could be used for a particular virtual UE's allocation.

The maximum layers that can be used and hence, the number of subcells available for a virtual UE allocation is described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27790\_replaced([11145090](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr-d_vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**3.10.2.0-24.0-2**  (ID: `11145090`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Maximum layers & subcell limit with Layer PRB Pooling

---

**3.10.2.0-24.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11145102`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE, the remaining layer PRBs available for MU-MIMO pairing shall determine the maximum number of layer to be used for a transmission, thus also restricting the number of subcells to be used. This also causes restrictions on the maximum number of layers during virtual UE construction (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7430\_replaced([11144070](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr7ao_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The constraints mentioned below shall be used considered during every virtual UE construction in a slot.

Based on the available number of layer PRB resources (rrmRemainingDlMuMimoLayerPrb; refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27723\_replaced([11144557](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr8owvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the PRBs available after every virtual UE allocation (rrmRemainingCellPrbForMuMimo; refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27778\_replaced([11144545](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr8owPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

[Before PR804667]

rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 = floor { rrmRemainingDlMuMimoLayerPrb / rrmRemainingCellPrbForMuMimo}

[PR804667]

rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 = min{(N \* floor { rrmRemainingDlMuMimoLayerPrb / rrmRemainingCellPrbForMuMimo}), (N \* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb)}

[End PR804667]

layerNumVirtualUeA <= rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1

If rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 <= 4

Only 1 subcell shall be used for the next MU-MIMO resource allocation.

End

If rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 <= 2

Stop MU-MIMO pairing. Allocate the remaining PRBs to the UEs with SU-MIMO based FDM allocation.

End

where,

* rrmRemainingDlMuMimoLayerPrb is the remaining Layer PRB capacity for MU-MIMO allocation in the cell as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27723\_replaced([11144557](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr8owvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmRemainingCellPrbForMuMimo is the remaining number of cell/physical PRBs for MU-MIMO allocation as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27778\_replaced([11144545](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr8owPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmMaxDlMuMimoLayerL1 is the maximum number of MU layers that L1 can support in a cell as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7955\_replaced([11142718](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr5lefvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[PR804667]

* N is the number of Active DL Subcells received from the BBRM (numActiveDlSubcell) for the current pooling period (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25713\_replaced([11214271](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxMVL_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27687\_replaced([11214642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOxZfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* maxNumberOfLayerPerCellPrb is the maximum number of layers supported by the primary subcell of the cell (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28507\_replaced([11214135](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxLuG_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

[End PR804667]

* layerNumVirtualUeA is the summed rank of all UEs in the virtual UE (A) defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7444\_replaced([11142531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

NOTE: The limit to check for 4 layers is considering that the primary subcell of the cell is a C4 subcell which supports maximum 4 layers

---

**3.10.2.0-24.0-3**  (ID: `11145109`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Resource allocation limit with Layer PRB Pooling

---

**3.10.2.0-24.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11145122`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE, the RBG allocation is limited by the available number of layer PRBs for MU-MIMO. The limit based on available layer PRB resources is defined as :

[Before CB010630-E]

vUeReqLayerPrbBasedAllocLimit = floor(floor(rrmRemainingDlMuMimoLayerPrb / layerNumVirtualUeA) / rbgSize) + nLastRbg

[CB010630-E]

If NRCELL.actRat1Alloc = False

vUeReqLayerPrbBasedAllocLimit = floor(floor(rrmRemainingDlMuMimoLayerPrb / layerNumVirtualUeA) / rbgSize) + nLastRbg

Else

vUeReqLayerPrbBasedAllocLimit = floor(rrmRemainingDlMuMimoLayerPrb / layerNumVirtualUeA)

End If

[End CB010630-E]

where,

* rrmRemainingDlMuMimoLayerPrb is the remaining Layer PRB capacity for MU-MIMO allocation in the cell as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27723\_replaced([11144557](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr8owvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* layerNumVirtualUeA is the summed rank of all UEs in the virtual UE (A) defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7444\_replaced([11142531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr4XXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rbgSize is the number of PRBs per RBG for RAT0, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4459\_replaced([11178370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2LwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

if (last RBG is already used) or (floor(rrmRemainingDlMuMimoLayerPrb / layerNumVirtualUeA) mod rbgSize) < lastRbgSize

nLastRbg = 0

else

nLastRbg = 1

end

lastRbgSize is the number of PRBs in the last RBG for RAT0

End

---

### 3.10.2.0-25 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) Restriction due to overload control (ID: 12436592)

**3.10.2.0-25.0-1**  (ID: `13367032`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
If NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) *is set to 0 and HwVariant used is not ABIL, due to potential scheduler processing overload issue, the maximum number virtual UEs per TTI shall be controlled by parameter rrmMaxNumberVuePerTTI as described below. Note that rrmMaxNumberVuePerTTI shall include only those virtual UEs that have more than one paired UEs with only initial Tx UEs. If NRCELL.actRat1Alloc=True, then after the limit for rrmMaxNumberVuePerTTI , as per the load situation given below, is crossed gNB-DU shall still continue to pair into new vUEs in order to finish those initTx UEs that were paired in the vUEs before the limit was reached. However in the subsequent pairing no new InitTx UEs shall be paired.*

If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric (See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31301\_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU overload control handler, is below the value set for **rdMuMimoRedvUeLowOlcDlPerCent (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31831\_replaced([11216833](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-qPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then, gNB-DU shall not apply any restriction to of rrmMaxNumberVuePerTTI**.

Else if the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric is greater than or equal to the value set for **activation threshold of rdMuMimoRedvUeLowOlcDlPerCent (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31831\_replaced([11216833](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-qPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and less than the activation threshold of rdMuMimoRedvUeMedOlcDlPerCent (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31832\_replaced([11216846](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-qvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))  then, gNB-DU shall set the value of rrmMaxNumberVuePerTTI to rdMaxNumVueInMedLoad (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32414\_replaced([11217267](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxeB8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

Else if real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric value is greater than or equal to the value set for **the activation threshold of rdMuMimoRedvUeMedOlcDlPerCent (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31832\_replaced([11216846](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-qvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and less than the activation threshold of** rdMuMimoRedvUeHighOlcDlPerCent (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31833\_replaced([11216858](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))then, gNB-DU shall set the value of rrmMaxNumberVuePerTTI to rdMaxNumVueInHighLoad (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32418\_replaced([11217280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxeB8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*\*\*

Else if real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric value is greater than or equal to the value set for **the** activation threshold of **rdMuMimoRedvUeHighOlcDlPerCent (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31833\_replaced([11216858](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-rPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and less than the** activation threshold of rdMuMimoDeactOlcDlPerCent (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31834\_replaced([11216871](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-rvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then, gNB-DU shall set the value of rrmMaxNumberVuePerTTI to rdMaxNumVueInCriticalLoad (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32420\_replaced([11217293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxeB9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).***\****\*

Else if real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric value is greater than or equal to the value set for **the** activation threshold of rdMuMimoDeactOlcDlPerCent (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31834\_replaced([11216871](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxa-rvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then, gNB-DU disable vUE creation with more than one paired UEs.\*\*\*\*

[CB015010-C]If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric (See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31301\_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU overload control handler, is below the value set forrdCplDeactOlcDlPerCent ([13367695](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_j2S6gfdGEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) then, gNB-DU shall perform or resume initial vUE creation ([13343587](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_m8n-Md8cEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) and TD metric of vUE update ([13347880](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_YR589-kyEfCnwLcpJWh_Zw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) if suspended.

If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric is greater than or equal to the value set for **activation threshold of** rdCplDeactOlcDlPerCent ([13367695](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_j2S6gfdGEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) then, gNB-DU shall suspend initial vUE creation ([13343587](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_m8n-Md8cEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) and TD metric of vUE update ([13347880](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_YR589-kyEfCnwLcpJWh_Zw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), if already being performed [End CB015010-C].

---

### 3.10.2.0-26 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) Allocate remaining RBGs/PRBs (ID: 11145129)

**3.10.2.0-26.0-8**  (ID: `12436589`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
After all virtual UEs are constructed and allocated with RBG/PRB, 5G-L2-PS shall allocate remaining RBG/PRB to UEs according to below algorithm:

[Before CB012971-C]

**1) If [rdEnableSbBfDlMuMimoL2 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_28945\_replaced([11149844](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQKzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is True], to simplify solution in L1 Radio, SB BF UEs which are already paired in VUE shall NOT be allocated to any PRBs with SU mode.**

[CB012971-C]

**1) If NIDD:actDlMuPairingGroup = True, SB BF UEs which are already paired in SVD-RZF VUE shall NOT be allocated to any additional PRBs for PDSCH with SU mode.**

[End CB012971-C]

2) If actRat1Alloc = False, for UEs which have non-zero allowedRbgUe(i), allocate RBG to them respectively with SU mode.

3) If actRat1Alloc = True, only to the last UE in the last virtual UE or the last non-paired UE with non-zero allowedPrbUe(i) with SU mode [PR864641] within the same PDSCH subarea allocated [End PR864641]. **Note: PR811466 reverts PR795459 to initial MU MIMO RAT1 implementation for software alignment**.\*\*\*\*

[PR864641]

3.1) If actRat1Alloc = True, the following steps shall be performed at the end of each subarea's virtual UEs construction and allocation. Across available PDSCH subareas, gNB-DU shall perform the following only for the SRS assisted WB BF MU eligible users. Note that the following steps are not applicable to SVD-RZF MU paired users or SVD/RZF SB BF MU eligible users (i.e which are not paired).

1>if there are remaining Prbs available in another subarea(s) AND

2> there is atleast one MU eligible user (newTx or reTx) that failed to pair in any vUE with existing MU users in a PDSCH subarea and still has remaining data in buffer AND

3> current allocation to the UE in the already assigned sub area is zero AND

4> there are no fresh UEs in the CS2 list to distribute the remaining resources.

Then:

> Sort the PDSCH subareas in descending order of available PRBs remaining.
>
> Re-assign the user to the 'new' PDSCH subarea with the largest available PRBs
>
> gNB-DU shall check for possible MU pairing with any existing user in the 'new' PDSCH subarea.
>
> If the user is a reTx user, and the available PRBs in the target PDSCH subarea cannot fulfill its demand, then downgrade the user to a newTx user.

[End PR864641]

4) If there are still free RBG/PRB, 5G-L2-PS shall allocate them to any UE, which have DL data in buffer (If sliceAwareSchedulerCellActivation = True, for the computation of DL data in buffer, the initial-tx of non-GBR DRBs and deprioritized GBR DRBs of a resource group (RG) with RG weight = 0 (rrmRGWeight = 0, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7389\_replaced([11188798](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kved7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), Note: DRB is not associated with an RG or associated with an unconfigured RG is handled by default RG.) should be excluded. ) one by one according to their PF metric priorities.

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eDlAllowed = TRUE, after allocating FD resources to a UE as mentioned above, gNB-DU shall determine the number of layer PRBs consumed (**rrmNumLayerPrbUsedPerAllocation described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and use it to keep track of the used, as well as remaining layer PRB resources (**rrmNumUsedPdschLayerPrbPerSlot, **rrmRemainingPdschLayerPrbPerSlot described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**\*\*\*\*

In the case that while allocating FD resources to a UE, the additional required layer PRB resources (can be calculated using **numReqLayerPrb described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is greater than the available layer PRB resources, gNB-DU shall reduce the number of FD resources allocated to the UE such that the layer PRB restriction is satisfied (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26597\_replaced([11214606](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).(The maximum usable FD resources based on the currently available layer PRB resources and the UEs rank can be calculated using** numReqFdPrb described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))\*\*\*\*

**[CB010630-E]**

The above layer PRB constraints are valid also when actRat1Alloc = true

**[End CB010630-E]**

### 3.10.2.0-27 DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based) DMRS port(s) and DL subcell related (ID: 11145181)

**3.10.2.0-27.0-1**  (ID: `12436704`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
DMRS port allocation algorithm (for SB BF UE)

---

**3.10.2.0-27.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `12436706`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
12436706:
DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
After SVD-RZF VUE is constructed, 5G-L2-PS shall execute below algorithms to allocate DMRS ports to paired UEs in SVD-RZF VUE.

1) For UEs in SVD-RZF VUE, 5G-L2-PS shall sort UEs with sum of correlation values with others in descending order and allocate DMRS ports to them one by one.

For example, UE0~UE3 are paired in one SVD-RZF VUE, their correlation values are listed in the below table.

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | UE0 | UE1 | UE2 | UE3 |
| UE0 |  | 0.5 | 0.55 | 0.1 |
| UE1 | 0.5 |  | 0.6 | 0.4 |
| UE2 | 0.55 | 0.6 |  | 0.2 |
| UE3 | 0.1 | 0.4 | 0.2 |  |

Sum of correlation values for each UE is UE0 = 1.15 (0.5 + 0.55 + 0.1), UE1 = 1.5 (0.5 + 0.6 + 0.4), UE2 = 1.35 (0.55 + 0.6 + 0.2), UE3 = 0.7 (0.1 + 0.4 + 0.2).

Then DMRS ports shall allocate to UEs in order of UE1 -> UE2 -> UE0 -> UE3.

2) Allocate DMRS ports from 0 to 3 with scramblingID0 at first. If no DMRS ports can be allocated, use scramblingID1.

* For PDSCH at rank 1, the DMRS port can be assigned is {0}, {1}, {2}, {3}.
* For PDSCH at rank 2, the DMRS ports can be assigned is {0, 1}, {2, 3}.
* For PDSCH at rank 3, the DMRS ports can be assigned is {0~2}.
* For PDSCH at rank 4, the DMRS ports can be assigned is {0~3}.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a table with two rows and five columns. The first column contains the text "DMRS scrambling ID0" and "DMRS scrambling ID1". The remaining columns are headed by "DMRS Type I" and then "0 (1000)", "1 (1000)", "2 (1000)", and "3 (1000)". There are blue arrows indicating relationships between the rows and columns. The arrow from "DMRS scrambling ID0" to "0 (1000)" is solid and points to the right. The arrow from "DMRS scrambling ID0" to "1 (1000)" is dashed and points to the right. The arrow from "DMRS scrambling ID0" to "2 (1000)" is solid and points to the right. The arrow from "DMRS scrambling ID0" to "3 (1000)" is solid and points to the right. The arrow from "DMRS scrambling ID1" to "0 (1000)" is solid and points to the left. The arrow from "DMRS scrambling ID1" to "1 (1000)" is dashed and points to the left. The arrow from "DMRS scrambling ID1" to "2 (1000)" is solid and points to the left. The arrow from "DMRS scrambling ID1" to "3 (1000)" is solid and points to the left.

|  | DMRS Type I | 0 (1000) | 1 (1000) | 2 (1000) | 3 (1000) |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| DMRS scrambling ID0 |  |  |  |  |  |
| DMRS scrambling ID1 |  |  |  |  |  |

**3.10.2.0-27.0-2**  (ID: `12446222`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Subcell allocation algorithm (for SB BF UE)

---

**3.10.2.0-27.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12446223`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
12446223:
DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
When add a SB BF UE into SVD-RZF VUE, 5G-L2-PS shall execute below algorithms to allocate subcell to ones which are not assigned.

In the below table, each column represents stream index of subcell, each row represents an instance of subcell for transmitting PDSCH. The number of subcell instances rely on nrCellType.

When large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is True and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is True, L2-PS shall assign DMRS port(s) on available DL subcell which are assigned by BBRM (numAllocSubcell and DL subcell ID list), not rely on nrCellType.

When L1 ARM based subcell deactivation procedure is enabled in DL i.e. dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed **= TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2-PS shall assign DMRS port(s) on the active DL subcells received from the BBRM (numActiveDlSubcells & listOfActiveDlSubcells), not rely on nrCellType.**

After DMRS ports are allocated to all UEs in virtualUE, 5G-L2-PS shall allocate unused subcell and stream index to UE in increasing order of:

* Different streams at first.
* Then different subcells.[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a table with two columns and five rows. The first column is labeled "Subcell" and the second column is labeled "Stream Index". The "Stream Index" column is further divided into four sub-columns labeled 0, 1, 2, and 3. The rows are labeled "Subcell (0)", "Subcell (1)", "Subcell (2)", and "Subcell (3)".
  Within the table, there are several lines representing data streams.
* In the row "Subcell (0)", there is a solid line extending from the "Stream Index 0" column to the "Stream Index 3" column.
* In the row "Subcell (1)", there is a dashed-dotted line extending from the "Stream Index 0" column to the "Stream Index 3" column, and a dashed line extending from the "Stream Index 1" column to the "Stream Index 3" column.
* In the row "Subcell (2)", there is a dashed line extending from the "Stream Index 0" column to the "Stream Index 3" column, and a dashed-dotted line extending from the "Stream Index 1" column to the "Stream Index 3" column.
* In the row "Subcell (3)", there is a dashed-dotted line extending from the "Stream Index 0" column to the "Stream Index 3" column, and a dashed line extending from the "Stream Index 1" column to the "Stream Index 3" column.
  The lines in the table appear to represent data flow or connections between subcells and stream indices. The arrows at the end of some lines indicate the direction of the flow.
  ```markdown

| Subcell | Stream Index 0 | Stream Index 1 | Stream Index 2 | Stream Index 3 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Subcell (0) | ───────────> |  |  |  |
| Subcell (1) | - . - . - . - | - - - - - - - |  |  |

For UEs which are scheduled with ranks 1 or 2, the streamConfig parameter for transmitting PDSCH signal shall be filled with numStreamIndex = 2, streamIndex = {0, 1} or {2, 3}. About definition of streamConfig, see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15591\_replaced([11512962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRteY_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more detail.

For UEs which are scheduled with ranks 3 or 4, the streamConfig parameter for transmitting PDSCH signal shall be filled with numStreamIndex = 4, streamIndex = {0, 1, 2, 3}.

**DMRS port and subcell allocation algorithm with Type I (for WB BF UE)**

**3.10.2.0-27.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13337094`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
**DMRS port and subcell allocation algorithm**

---

**3.10.2.0-27.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11145195`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
When adding a candidate into a virtual UE, if DMRS port(s) of current candidate has already been assigned, 5G-L2-PS shall ensure allocated port(s) is not conflicted with ports which are assigned to other paired UEs in current virtual UE.

After virtual UE is constructed, 5G-L2-PS shall allocate DMRS port(s) and DL subcell to paired ones which have no DMRS ports assigned.

The detailed algorithms can be found in below requirements:

If nrCellType is 8DLnUL or 4DLnUL,

* DMRS port(s) and DL subcell allocation, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11372\_replaced([11145207](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr_sEvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* Example for 8DLnUL or 4DLnUL, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11373\_replaced([11145246](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr_sF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB008701-A]

If nrCellType is 16DLnUL,

* DMRS port(s) and DL subcell allocation, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11377\_replaced([11145267](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr_sGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* Example for 16DLnUL, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11379\_replaced([11145303](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksATIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB008701-A]

**3.10.2.0-27.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11145202`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
nrCellType is 4DLnUL or 8DLnUL for DMRS configuration type 1

---

**3.10.2.0-27.0-3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11145207`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
DMRS port(s) and DL subcell allocation algorithm

---

**3.10.2.0-27.0-3.0-2.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11145238`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
[CB008830-B]

NOTE: For Port allocation, subcell allocation algorithm for DMRS type 2, please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25104\_replaced([11145315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksATI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_25222\_replaced([11145426](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksATLfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For DMRS Type1:

[End CB008830-B]

When adding a candidate into a virtual UE, if DMRS port(s) of current candidate has already been allocated, 5G-L2-PS shall ensure allocated port is not conflicted with ports which are assigned to other paired UEs in current virtual UE. A DMRS port conflict means the same DMRS port is assigned to multiple UEs with the same scramblingID value.

After virtual UE is constructed, 5G-L2-PS shall allocate DMRS port(s) to paired UEs which have no assigned DMRS port(s), 5G-L2-PS shall allocate port(s) according to below orders. Note: values of scramblingID0 and scramblingID1 are sent from CP-RT in user addition procedure, see 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_2227\_replaced([11282131](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpdMk_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

* To allocate unused port(s) to candidate with scramblingID0.
* To allocate unused port(s) to candidate with scramblingID1.

If the candidate is the 2nd MU UE in a virtual UE and if the candidate and the 1st MU UE are rank1 or rank2 UEs, 5G-L2-PS shall allocate unused port(s) to the candidate with the same scramblingID as the 1st MU UE.

Value of the field ‘Antenna port(s)’ in DCI 1\_1 shall be found from the table 7.3.1.2.2-1 in TS 38.212 according to allocated DMRS port(s) per UE.

The number of CDM group(s) without data is determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3054\_replaced([11129150](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq6uCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

After DMRS port(s) and scramblingID are assigned for each UE in current virtual UE, the DL subcell shall be assigned as well according to below rules:

* For UEs which are scheduled with DMRS ports using scramblingID0, they shall be scheduled with subcell#0;
* For UEs which are scheduled with DMRS ports using scramblingID1, they shall be scheduled with subcell#1;
* For UEs which are scheduled with DMRS ports {0}, {1}, {0, 1}, the streamConfig parameter for transmitting PDSCH signal shall be filled with numStreamIndex = 2, streamIndex = {0, 1}. About definition of streamConfig, see 5G\_L1\_IF\_15591\_replaced([11512962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRteY_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for more details;
* For UEs which are scheduled with DMRS ports {2}, {3}, {2, 3}, the streamConfig parameter for transmitting PDSCH signal shall be filled with numStreamIndex = 2, streamIndex = {2, 3};
* For UEs which are scheduled with DMRS ports {0, 1, 2} or {0, 1, 2, 3}, the streamConfig parameter for transmitting PDSCH signal shall be filled with numStreamIndex = 4, streamIndex = {0, 1, 2, 3}.

When large BB pooling is enabled, i.e., if slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is True and subcellDeactivationDlAllowed is True, L2-PS shall assign DMRS port(s) on available DL subcell which are assigned by BBRM (numAllocSubcell and DL subcell ID list), not rely on nrCellType.

When L1 ARM based subcell deactivation procedure is enabled in DL i.e. dlSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_8225\_replaced([11232681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TmKoDfvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2-PS shall assign DMRS port(s) on the active DL subcells received from the BBRM (numActiveDlSubcells & listOfActiveDlSubcells), not rely on nrCellType.

**3.10.2.0-27.0-3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11145246`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Allocation examples

**3.10.2.0-27.0-3.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11145252`)

DL MU-MIMO for mMIMO TDD FR1 (Virtual UE Based)
Some examples are listed as below to illustrate how to allocate DMRS ports to paired UEs:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| UE0 (rank 4) | UE1 (rank 4) |
| {0, 1, 2, 3} with scramblingID0 | {0, 1, 2, 3} with scramblingID1 |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| UE0 (rank 4) | UE1 (rank 2) |
| {0, 1, 2, 3} with scramblingID0 | {0, 1} with scramblingID1 |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| UE0 (rank 2) | UE1 (rank 2) |
| {0, 1} with scramblingID0 | {2, 3} with scramblingID0 |

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| UE0 (rank 2) | UE1 (rank 2) |
| {0, 1} with scramblingID1 | {2, 3} with scramblingID1 |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| UE0 (rank 2) | UE1 (rank 2) | UE2 (rank 4) |
| {0, 1} with scramblingID1 | {2, 3} with scramblingID1 | {0, 1, 2, 3} with scramblingID0 |

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| UE0 (rank 4) | UE1 (rank 2) | UE2(rank 2) |
| {0, 1, 2, 3} with scramblingID0 | {0, 1} with scramblingID1 | {2, 3} with scramblingID1 |

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| UE0 (rank 2) | UE1 (rank 2) | UE2 (rank 2) | UE3 (rank 2) |
| {0, 1} with scramblingID0 | {2, 3} with scramblingID0 | {0, 1} with scramblingID1 | {2, 3} with scramblingID1 |
