**3.10.3.2.0-1.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `12693171`)

Overall MU pairing algorithm in SD
Beam groups pairing

---

**3.10.3.2.0-1.0-5.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13254867`)

Overall MU pairing algorithm in SD
13254867:
Overall MU pairing algorithm in SD
This requirement describe how to construct virtual UEs with beam groups only.
**Initialization step:**
1) Initialize all elements of numOfAvailablePrbPerLayer with InitialAvailablePrb,where InitialAvailablePrb is calculated as follows.
\* If two virtual UEs will be constructed by beam groups, refer to [12692821](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0X118VgAEfCMqIX_zEVxAQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
+ When L2RT construct the first virtual UE(A), InitialAvailablePrb = rrmAvailablePrbForMu (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9513\_replaced([11146443](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksD9i_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) − maxGapsPrb , where maxGapsPrb is obtained by examining all beam groups that can't participate in the current vUE(A) and taking the maximum requested PRB among these groups. See example in [12692821](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0X118VgAEfCMqIX_zEVxAQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).
+ When L2RT construct the second virtual UE(B)，InitialAvailablePrb = maxGapsPrb
\* If only one virtual UE will be constructed by beam groups ([12692821](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0X118VgAEfCMqIX_zEVxAQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), InitialAvailablePrb = rrmAvailablePrbForMu (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9513\_replaced([11149214](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksMgevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
2)  Initialize the beam group index j = 0, starting from the first un-used beam group in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29212\_replaced([11149214](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksMgevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
3)  Initialize the MU-MIMO layer index n = 0, representing the first MU-MIMO layer.
4) Initialize maxNumOfAvailableBeamGroups with the total number of un-used beam groups defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29212\_replaced([11149214](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksMgevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
The steps to construct a new virtual UE with the UEs from different beam groups are as follows.
After all of virtual UEs are constructed completely with the following procedure in flowchart, L2RT shall update the number of MU-MIMO layers for this virtual UE by removing empty layers, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32425\_replaced([11148356](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksJdHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
Note:
\* The same beam group shall not exist in more than one virtual UE simultaneously.
\* During the construction of a virtual UE, there may be cases where the current beam group can't be inserted into any empty MU-MIMO layers due to the sub-area limitations. In such cases, [Before CB008235-D] L2RT shall exclude this beam group. [CB008235-D] Refer to [12553426](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_EXqIACUREfCNjfqfyUlvmw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and [12794577](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_IG4YI5eWEfC7Wp-sWxcfJw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [End CB008235-D]
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a flowchart illustrating a process. The flowchart begins with a "Start" node, followed by an "Intilization Steps (see same requirement)" process box.
From the initialization step, a decision point asks "Is rrmRequiredMuPrbNum (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9513) > rrmAvailablePrbForMu (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9513) \* rdUIPrbScaleRatio(5G\_UP\_ALG\_14881)".
If the answer to the above is "Yes", the flow proceeds to a decision box: "Is numOfReqPrbPerBeamGroup[j] >= InitialAvailablePrb?".
If the answer to "Is numOfReqPrbPerBeamGroup[j] >= InitialAvailablePrb?" is "Yes", a process box states: "Add this group into the empty layer with the smallest layer index I, where I <= max number of MU-MIMO layer (11146235). - If the layer of group (11149309) is 2, the eligible layer index is 0, 2,4,6. - If the layer of group (11149309) is 1, the eligible layer index is 1,3,5,7." This is followed by "Update numOfAvailablePrbPerLayer[1] = 0".
If the answer to "Is numOfReqPrbPerBeamGroup[j] >= InitialAvailablePrb?" is "No", the flow proceeds to a decision box: "Is numOfReqPrbPerBeamGroup[j] (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29226) <= numOfAvailableProPerLayer[n]?".
If the answer to "Is numOfReqPrbPerBeamGroup[j] (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29226) <= numOfAvailableProPerLayer[n]?" is "Yes", a process box states "Assign group j into layer n". This is followed by "Update numof AvailablePrbPerLayer[n] = numOf AvailablePrbPerLayer[n] - numOfReqPrbPerBeamGroup[j] (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29206) Update rrmRequiredMuPrbNum;".
If the answer to "Is numOfReqPrbPerBeamGroup[j] (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29226) <= numOfAvailableProPerLayer[n]?" is "No", the flow proceeds to a process box: "Go to the next layer by updating n = n + the layer of group(11149309)". This is followed by a decision box: "Is n < max number of MU-MIMO layer (11146235)?".
If the answer to "Is n < max number of MU-MIMO layer (11146235)?" is "Yes", the flow loops back to the decision box "Is numOfReqPrbPerBeamGroup[j] >= InitialAvailablePrb?".
If the answer to "Is n < max number of MU-MIMO layer (11146235)?" is "No", the flow proceeds to a process box: "add group j into the non-empty layer which has the minimum number of PRB.".
After either the "Assign group j into layer n" path or the "add group j into the non-empty layer which has the minimum number of PRB." path, the flow proceeds to a process box: "Go to the next beam group by updating beam group j = j +1". This is followed by a decision box: "Is j <= maxNumOf AvailableBeamGroups?".
If the answer to "Is j <= maxNumOf AvailableBeamGroups?" is "Yes", the flow loops back to the decision box "Is numOfReqPrbPerBeamGroup[j] >= InitialAvailablePrb?".
If the answer to "Is j <= maxNumOf AvailableBeamGroups?" is "No", the flowchart ends with an "End" node.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-11211700.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
**File Name: Step4 Construct new vUEs.sheet**
**File path:**

- The "4th layer" is allocated to "beam group6" initially, and then to "beam group7".

**3.10.3.2.0-1.0-6**  (ID: `13284435`)

Overall MU pairing algorithm in SD
Step5: Construct virtual UE from beam groups including mixed waveform UEs

**3.10.3.2.0-1.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `13310410`)

Overall MU pairing algorithm in SD
Algorithm Overview

---

**3.10.3.2.0-1.0-6.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13310411`)

Overall MU pairing algorithm in SD
When NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.actUlMuMimoGroupPairing is TRUE, after the previous rounds of MU pairing, if there are still CP-OFDM UEs and DFT-s-OFDM MU eligible UEs remain and rrmRequiredMuPrbNum (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9513) is still larger than rrmAvailablePrbForMu  (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9513) \* rdUlPrbScaleRatio(5G\_UP\_ALG\_14881), L2RT shall re-divide the UEs into the beam groups.

After re-division, the same beam group could include the UEs with mixture waveform, at the same time, the beam group related information [13254093,](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_AzgDgMbdEfCYBIz6acpPHw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)[11149288](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNHc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), [11149309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNHdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and so on shall be updated accordingly,

In this step, L2RT shall perform [12692821](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_0X118VgAEfCMqIX_zEVxAQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)to determine the number of virtual UE constructed in this stage , one virtual UE or two virtual UEs.

After deciding the number of virtual UEs constructed in this step, the detailed algorithmic procedure can be found in [12693171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PL8pS1gPEfCMqIX_zEVxAQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

At this step, when constructing each virtual UE,

* the value of InitialAvailablePrb use in [12693171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PL8pS1gPEfCMqIX_zEVxAQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)shall be set to the total requested PRBs of all UEs belonging to the beam groups eligible for this virtual UE, divided by 2.
* the maximum number of MU-MIMO layer use in [12693171](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PL8pS1gPEfCMqIX_zEVxAQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)shall refer to [13248427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PSomy8SREfCnuMJFWtMTpQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)
* the maximum number of beam groups share the same PRB is two.

Note:

* If no CP-OFDM UEs remain and only DFT-s-OFDM UEs are left, L2RT shall not perform re-division, because the beam group classification for DFT-s-OFDM UEs has already been completed in earlier steps.

**3.10.3.2.0-1.0-7**  (ID: `13249645`)

Overall MU pairing algorithm in SD
UE waveform type dependent step selection in UL MU-MIMO when NRCELL.ulMaxMuMimoLayer > 4

---

**3.10.3.2.0-1.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `13249721`)

Overall MU pairing algorithm in SD
For step1~step5 mentioned in this requirement, refer to overview requirement defined in [11145777](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksBhR_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

For CP-OFDM UEs, they are allowed to participate in step1 to step4 ([11145811](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksBhSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9),[11145856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCIUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9),  [11145918](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCIV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and [11146093](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCvZvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) of the pairing procedure.

The actual step in which a CP-OFDM UE participates is determined by

* NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.actUlMuMimoGroupPairing, and
* rdUlMuMimoGroupPairing ([11149883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) indication.

For DFT-s-OFDM UEs,

* L2RT shall schedule initial and re-transmission traffic UEs to participate in Step2:correlation based pairing([11145856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCIUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) regardless of rdUlMuMimoGroupPairing.bit3 ([11149883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to ensure the maximum number of MU-MIMO layers can be achieved.
* DFT-s-OFDM UE's eligibility to participate in Step3 is determined by both NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.actUlMuMimoGroupPairing and rdUlMuMimoGroupPairing.bit1 ([11149883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* DFT-s-OFDM beam groups can't join in pairing in step4 ([11146093](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCvZvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) which limited to CP-OFDM beam groups pairing regardless of NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.actUlMuMimoGroupPairing and rdUlMuMimoGroupPairing.bit2 ([11149883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) setting
* Mixed DFT-s-OFDM and CP-OFDM beam groups or only DFT-s-OFDM beam group shall join in step5 ([13284435](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Uc6tMMuKEfCYBIz6acpPHw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) when NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.actUlMuMimoGroupPairing is TRUE.

Note, for two closed UEs pairing, it will be refreshed in a new feature and not consider it in this feature.

---

**3.10.3.2.0-1.0-8**  (ID: `13310564`)

Overall MU pairing algorithm in SD
DFT-s-OFDM MU-MIMO pairing constraints

---

**3.10.3.2.0-1.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `13310565`)

Overall MU pairing algorithm in SD
\* DFT-s-OFDM UEs can achieve the configured maximum MU-MIMO layer count (e.g., 4 layers or 8 layers) only when their requested PRB number are identical or sufficiently similar to get the optimal performance since under this condition, DMRS sequence for paired MU-MIMO UEs are orthogonal. For CP-OFDM UEs, there are no such kind of limitation.
\* [CB008148-E] If the DFT-s-OFDM MU-MIMO UEs in the same virtual UE have different PRB number or different start PRB index, they shall be placed into different CDM groups. In this case, at most two beam groups can be share the same frequency resource [End CB008148-E]
\* Within the same CDM group, only UE with the same waveform type are allowed to share the same frequence resource.  Mixing different waveform UEs within the same CDM group use the same frequence resource is not allowed.

Note: Simulation result refer to [CB008148\_1+1\_v3.pptx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:p:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CB/CB008000%20-%20CB008499/CFAM/CB008148%20DFT-s-OFDM%20Enhancements/MU-MIMO/CB008148_1+1_v3.pptx?d=w81eb4490e0ff42e0ba13418a80465fd3&csf=1&web=1&e=0LWOyV)

### 3.10.3.3 Build non-GBR UE list and virtual UE list

#### 3.10.3.3.0-1 Build non-GBR UE list and virtual UE list Build non-GBR UE list (ID: 11146141)

**3.10.3.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11146147`)

Build non-GBR UE list and virtual UE list
Create rrmUlMuCandidateList and rrmUlNonMuCandidateList

---

**3.10.3.3.0-1.0-1.0-10**  (ID: `13455656`)

Build non-GBR UE list and virtual UE list
At the beginning of UL slot before any virtual UE construction, L2RT shall create the MU candidate list **rrmUlMuCandidateList, which is initialized with non-GBR UEs which satisfy the MU candidates conditions and** rrmUlNonMuCandidateList which is initialized with non-GBR initial transmission UEs which don't satisfy the MU candidates conditions.\*\*\*\*

MU candidate UEs shall meet all the below conditions:

**con1: UEs in CS2 to-be-scheduled list,**

**con2: UL traffic for UEs which shall not have CG occasion in the UL slot [CB014699-E]including critical non-GBR and non-critical [End CB014699-E] non-GBR initial transmission, or [CB014699-E] critical non-GBR and non-critical [End CB014699-E] non-GBR retransmission traffic which satisfy the requirement in 5G\_UP\_ALG**\_11084\_replaced([11148246](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_5q9dgPvLEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*\*\*

* Note:**non-GBR traffic (both initialTx and re-Tx) includes [CB014699-E]critical non-GBR, [End CB014699-E] NBR configured non-GBR and other normal non-GBR traffic.**
* Note: Reason that the CG UE is excluded is due to the fact that CG PUSCH scheduled shall not be discarded due to MU pairing constraints
* Note: For initial transmission of prioritized DC-GBR data and/or Deprioritized DC-GBR data shall be excluded from UL MU-MIMO pairing. For retransmission with request class harqRetransDrb for data in corresponding initial transmission with any deprioritized DC-GBR shall be excluded from UL MU-MIMO pairing.

**con3:  For multiple BWP cases, UL MU-MIMO applies to below BWP:**

**- For UEs which have different BW capabilities, it only applies to BWP of full bandwidth.**

- For multiple BWPs for power saving, it only applies to larger BWP (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1872\_replaced([11111200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpLBnfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**Note: For the UEs in the transition period switching from large BWP to small BWP, they shall NOT be selected as MU-MIMO eligible UEs even if over-sampled DFTbeams are configured or averaged covariance matrices are not aged.**

**con4: Averaged covariance matrices on vertical and horizontal directions are not aged (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2136\_replaced([11154035](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqac_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),**

**con5: PUSCH beams are over-sampled DFT beams,**

**con6: The rescaled SINR which is the resacled SINR(5G\_UP\_ALG\_17271\_replaced([11131543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to the number of required PRBs and the WB-SINR rrmCorrAvgSinr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3074\_replaced([11130160](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq-_e_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** which doesn't include rrmDeltaSinr[i,j,t]  (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3151\_replaced([11137856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krbrbvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be equal or larger than NIDD:NRBTS/NRCELL/ulMuMimoParaSet/ulMuMimoSinrThd,\*\*\*\*

**con7: UEs with number of required PRBs > alpha \* the number of PRBs for the UL carrier bandwidth(5G\_UP\_ALG\_1795\_replaced([11110609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpGJHfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , where**

alpha is equal to NRBTS/NRCELL/NRULMUMIMO.ulCandidatePrbRatio,

con8: Limited to UEs using CP-OFDM UEs and DFT-s-OFDM UEs. Note, DFT-s-OFDM UEs can be selected into this list only when NIDD:actUlTransPreUsageEnh is set to DCI01\_TpOn\_MuMimo

The UEs which are in transient period of switching from CP-OFDM to transform precoder (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3301\_replaced([11141079](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krxCl_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be excluded.

The UEs which are in transient period of switching from DFT-s-OFDM to CP-OFDM shall be excluded also.

**con9:  If UE is in Basic Reliability (HR) mode in the Uplink (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15105\_replaced([11125150](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqsrnPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),**

**con10: If NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is equal to 4 [CNI-142411] and NRCELL.actUlMuMimoSimplification is false [End CNI-142411], then for UEs with number of layer equal to 1,**

-  if mcs-Table is 256QAM is used, exclude those UEs whose AbsoluteFO\_Hz (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11388\_replaced([11151008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksWRcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) calculated from longTermCfoMetric (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6911\_replaced([11151021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksW4cfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is bigger than *NIDD:foThresh256Qam AND rescaled SU SINR according to the number of required PRBs is larger than rdSINR256QAM(5G\_UP\_ALG\_14873\_replaced([11149399](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNugPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*

- if mcs-Table with 64QAM or mcs-Table with 64QAMLowSE is used, exclude those UEs whose AbsoluteFO\_Hz (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11388\_replaced([11151008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksWRcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) calculated from longTermCfoMetric (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6911\_replaced([11151021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksW4cfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is bigger than *NIDD:foThreshNon256Qam AND rescaled SU SINR according to the number of required PRBs is larger than rdSINR64QAM(5G\_UP\_ALG\_14875\_replaced([11149409](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNugvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Rationale: Since 5GMax simulation results show that only high end MCS index matters and the spectral efficiency of high end MCS index in 64QAMLowSE table is lower than that in 64QAM it is fine to reuse the same threshold for 64QAMLowSE with that for 64QAM.*

**con11: If PUSCH is received over 8**or 16 spatial streams in a given subcell (5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):\*\*\*\*

- if rdActUlMuMimoNlos (5G\_UP\_ALG\_20051\_replaced([11149670](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksO8r_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is false, limited to the UEs which are located in LOS channel; else limited to the UEs which are located in either LOS or NLOS channel. **The requirement to identify LOS and NLOS UEs refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19956\_replaced([11148257](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksJdFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

con12: If ((NIDD:numberOfRxBeamforming equals 8RX or 16RX) [CNI-142411] OR (NIDD:numberOfRxBeamforming equals 4RX and NRCELL.actUlMuMimoSimplification is TRUE)[End CNI-142411])  , then L2RT shall exclude a UE from the MU-MIMO eligible list under either of the following conditions:

* CFO disabling ([11151369](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksYtq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is not triggered, and the long term UE specific CFO is invalid; or
* CFO disabling ([11151369](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksYtq_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is triggered

---

#### 3.10.3.3.0-2 Build non-GBR UE list and virtual UE list Build virtual UE list (ID: 11146198)

**3.10.3.3.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11146206`)

Build non-GBR UE list and virtual UE list
The virtual UE list rrmvUEList includes the virtual UEs (5G\_UP\_ALG\_8267\_replaced([11145665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksBhQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

When a new UE is added into the virtual UE successfully, L2RT shall update virtual UE scheduling information (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9548\_replaced([11147793](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHn8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The initialization of rrmvUEList is empty at the beginning of the slot.

---

#### 3.10.3.3.0-3 Build non-GBR UE list and virtual UE list UE order in rrmUlMuCandidateList (ID: 11146213)

**3.10.3.3.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `13421337`)

Build non-GBR UE list and virtual UE list
L2RT shall re-order the UEs in rrmUlMuCandidateList according to the following sequence:

a) Re-transmission UEsincluding both DFT-s-OFDM UEs and CP-OFDM UEs shall be placed at the beginning of the list and shall be sorted in descending order of priority resource request (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10506\_replaced ([11194320](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv0cIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4773\_replaced ([11194371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv0cKfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

b) After all re-transmission UEs, initial transmission UEs including both DFT-s-OFDM UEs and CP-OFDM UEs shall follow, with the following ordering rules:

[CB014699-E]

b1) Critical non-GBR initial transmission UEs shall be sorted in descending order of required PRBs (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5010\_replaced ([11201008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwTkUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5016\_replaced ([11201086](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwULYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[End CB014699-E]

b2) NBR initial transmission UEs shall be placed [CB014699-E] after critical non-GBR UEs and [End CB014699-E] sorted in descending order of required PRBs (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5010\_replaced ([11201008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwTkUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5016\_replaced ([11201086](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwULYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

b3) Normal non-GBR initial transmission UEs shall be placed after NBR UEs and sorted in descending order of required PRBs (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5010\_replaced([11201008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwTkUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5016\_replaced([11201086](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwULYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

### 3.10.3.4 Maximum number of MU layers

#### 3.10.3.4.0-1 Maximum number of MU layers Maximum number of MU layers per slot (ID: 13248448)

**3.10.3.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13248454`)

Maximum number of MU layers
The number of UL MU-MIMO layers per slot shall be common in [11145764: Overall MU pairing algorithm in SD](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksBhRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) which is decided in [11146241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksDWePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ), except for certain special processing where a different number of layers needs to be defined in [11145764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksBhRfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). Refer to [13248427](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PSomy8SREfCnuMJFWtMTpQ) for details.

---

#### 3.10.3.4.0-2 Maximum number of MU layers Common rule to decide the maximum number of MU layers per slot (ID: 11146241)

**3.10.3.4.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11146253`)

Maximum number of MU layers
L2RT shall estimate the maximum number of MU layers maxUlMuMimoLayer at the beginning of the slot as following:

If rdUlMuMimoLayerFactor (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14877\_replaced([11149423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuhPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is configured to zero:

maxUlMuMimoLayer is decided by NIDD:NRCELL/ULMUMIMOPARASET/ulMaxMuMimoLayer (5G\_UP\_4480\_replaced([11355720](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucTDXfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

If rdUlMuMimoLayerFactor (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14877\_replaced([11149423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuhPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is configured to a non-zero value: **maxUlMuMimoLayer = MIN(maxUlMuMimoLayer, ROUNDUP(rdUlMuMimoLayerFactor (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14877\_replaced([11149423](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuhPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) \* rrmRequiredMuPrbNum / rrmAvailablePrbForMu)), where**

- The definition of rrmAvailablePrbForMu and rrmRequiredMuPrbNum see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9513\_replaced([11146443](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksD9i_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- maxUlMuMimoLayer is decided by NIDD:NRCELL/ULMUMIMOPARASET/ulmaxMuMimoLayer (5G\_UP\_4480\_replaced([11355720](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucTDXfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If NIDD: actUlMuMimo = true AND PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell(5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND number of subcells per cell is two (5G\_UP\_2470\_replaced([11389618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufPCk_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the secondary UL subcell shall be used for SDM (spatial domain multiplexing) purpose (see 5G\_UP\_1712\_replaced([11369575](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_udq8W_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or re-transmission traffic with the following case.

For UE i with re-transmission traffic, L2RT shall allocate the same subcell index in re-transmission traffic as the one in initial transmission traffic.

**[PR783809, CB012605-I]**

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1Ecpri72eUlAllowed = TRUE:

- If ROUND(rrmMaxNumLayerPrbPerSlot(UL) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26582\_replaced([11214591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxOKXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) / availableUlPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4876\_replaced([11196884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwGI9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) >=2, the maximum number of MU layers in this slot is min(ROUNDUP(rrmMaxNumLayerPrbPerSlot(UL) / availableUlPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4876\_replaced([11196884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwGI9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))), NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMaxMuMimoLayer);

- Else, MU-MIMO shall not be triggered in this slot.

**[End PR783809, CB012605-I]**

---

#### 3.10.3.4.0-3 Maximum number of MU layers Special definitions for MU-MIMO layer number per slot (ID: 13248427)

**3.10.3.4.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13248430`)

Maximum number of MU layers
This requirement defines the maximum number of MU-MIMO layers in step2 and step4 when NRCELL.ulMaxMuMimoLayer > 4 under some special cases.

1. When NRCELL.ulMaxMuMimoLayer > 4, then the maximum number of MU-MIMO layers used during Step 2: Correlation-based pairing (as described in [11145856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCIUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) , for pairing UEs with a similar number of PRBs, shall be determined according to the rules defined in [12703788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PlNxoV5hEfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).
2. [CB008148-E]

When NRCELL.ulMaxMuMimoLayer  > 4, NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.actUlMuMimoGroupPairing == TRUE, the maximum number of MU-MIMO layer per PRB in Step5 ([13284435](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Uc6tMMuKEfCYBIz6acpPHw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) shall be decided as follows:

1) If the maximum number of layer among all beam groups' layer[(11149309)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNHdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) is 2 in current slot,

* If the number of MU-MIMO layers decided in [11146241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksDWePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) is greater than or equal to 4, then then the maximum number of MU-MIMO layers used in Step5 ([13284435](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Uc6tMMuKEfCYBIz6acpPHw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) shall be 4.
* Otherwise, Step5 ([13284435](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Uc6tMMuKEfCYBIz6acpPHw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) shall not be triggered, even if NIDD:actUlMuMimoGroupPairing == TRUE

2) If the maximum number of layer among all beam groups' layer[(11149309)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNHdfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) is 1 in current slot,

* If the number of MU-MIMO layers (as determined in [11146241](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksDWePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is greater than or equal to 2, then the the maximum number of MU-MIMO layers used in Step5 ([13284435](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Uc6tMMuKEfCYBIz6acpPHw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) shall be 2
* Otherwise, Step5 ([13284435](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Uc6tMMuKEfCYBIz6acpPHw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) shall not be triggered, even if NIDD:actUlMuMimoGroupPairing == TRUE

[End CB008148-E]

---

### 3.10.3.5 Receiver Model in MU-MIMO

#### 3.10.3.5.0-1 Receiver Model in MU-MIMO Receiver Model in MU-MIMO with 4RX (ID: 11146266)

**3.10.3.5.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11146290`)

Receiver Model in MU-MIMO
11146290:
Receiver Model in MU-MIMO
[CB009363-F]If PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell(5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then: [End CB009363-F]

For the SU-MIMO UEs, 4RX SU-IRC receiver is always used, only primary subcell can be used even if two C4 UL subcells (NIDD:nrCellType = xDL8UL) are configured.

For the MU-MIMO UEs, the receiver model is indicated as following:

 If the number of C4 UL subcells per cell is one (NIDD:nrCellType = 4DL4UL or 8DL4UL), only MU-IRC receiver should be used for the paired UEs.

The maximum number of MU layers in this configuration is up to 2.

 If the number of C4 subcells per cell is two (NIDD:nrCellType = xDL8UL), L2RT should indicate L1 which receiver model is used according to the number of paired UEs.

The maximum number of MU layers in this configuration is up to 4.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Case No. | Description | 1st C4 subcell |  |  | 2nd C4 subcell |  |  |
| UE allocation | Receiver Model |  | UE allocation | Receiver Model |  |  |  |
| Su-Receiver | Mu-Receiver | Su-Receiver | Mu-Receiver |  |  |  |  |
| 1 | No pairing | 1xUE(max rank is 2) | √ |  |  |  |  |
| 2 | 2x UEs are paired | 1xUE(rank2) | √ |  | 1xUE(rank2) | √ |  |
| 1xUE(rank2) | √ |  | 1xUE(rank1) | √ |  |  |  |
| 1xUE(rank1) paired with 1xUE(rank1) |  | √ |  |  |  |  |  |
| 3 | 3x UEs are paired | 2xUE with rank1 |  | √ | 1xUE(max rank is 2) | √ |  |
| 4 | 4x UEs are paired | 2xUE with rank1 |  | √ | 2xUE with rank1 |  | √ |

For the MU-IRC receiver, when the virtual UE is constructed by 3 or 4 UEs and the number of layers for all of them is one, L2RT shall decide which two UEs use the same MU-IRC receiver model as following:

The UEs with minimum horizontal degree separation shall be assigned to the same MU-IRC receiver, the remaining UE(s) will be assigned to aother SU-IRC or MU-IRC receiver depending on number of paired UEs.

If root UE is paired with a candidate UE group (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9690\_replaced([11148139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksI2BPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), SU-IRC receiver in the 1st subcell will be used by root UE and SU-IRC receiver in the 2nd subcell will be used by the UEs which are included in candidate UE group. The UEs which are included in candidate UE group shall only support FDM. Here is one[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a table with two rows and multiple columns. The first row is labeled "root UE" and contains a single cell spanning several columns, filled with yellow and labeled "UE2". The second row is labeled "candidate UE group" and is divided into three colored cells. The first cell is green and labeled "UE4". The second cell is peach-colored and labeled "UE5". The third cell is orange and labeled "UE6". The table has a grid background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9219.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]example:

NOTE: If a root UE is paired with a candidate UE group (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9690\_replaced([11148139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksI2BPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), only SU-IRC receiver can be used due to the limitation of MU-IRC receiver.

---

#### 3.10.3.5.0-2 Receiver Model in MU-MIMO Receiver Model in MU-MIMO with 8RX / 16RX (ID: 11146299)

**3.10.3.5.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11146311`)

Receiver Model in MU-MIMO
8RX [CB010708-E] or 16RX [End CB010708-E] MU-IRC receiver (5G\_UP\_ALG\_19607\_replaced([11104182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kn52RPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19619\_replaced([11104193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kn52R_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be always used for the paired UEs, refer to 5G\_UP\_4977\_replaced([11355544](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucR1PPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The MU-IRC receiver order is indicated by NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming. 28972

### 3.10.3.6 Virtual UE construction

#### 3.10.3.6-1 Candidate UE group

**3.10.3.6-1.0-5**  (ID: `12716317`)

Candidate UE group
If UL MU-MIMO is enabled (see NIDD parameters of actUlMuMimo) AND UL tapering is enabled (see NIDD parameters of actUlMuMimoTapering) :

For UE(i), dynamic tapering for this UE shall be enabled if the following condition is satisfied:

- The rescaled SINR of UE(i) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22977\_replaced([11149153](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksMgYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is NOT smaller than the value of rdTaperingSINRThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29531\_replaced([11149696](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksPjtfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or the value of rdTaperingSINRThreshold8RX (5G\_UP\_ALG\_20562\_replaced([11149685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksPjsvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if PUSCH is received over 8 or larger than 8 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**NOTE:**

1) For SU UE, gNB shall always use non-tapered beams to receive UL signals.

2) For MU UE which is paired with other UEs successfully, if dynamic tapering is enabled for this UE, gNB shall use tapered beams to receive PUSCH signals; otherwise, gNB shall use non-tapered beams to receive PUSCH signals.

3) [CB014094-C] Note: Since osDFT beams are refreshed at the t0 of each beam update period, it is possible that NIDD:actUlMuMimoTapering and NIDD:actUlMuMimo become enabled after t0 but before the next update period begins. During this transient interval, if both parameters are set to true but no tapered beams are yet available, L2RT shall temporarily use the non‑tapered beam for MU-MIMO UEs until the tapered beams become available.. [End CB014094-C]

---

#### 3.10.3.6-2 Candidate UE group

**3.10.3.6-2.0-4**  (ID: `12716323`)

Candidate UE group
Tapering status in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9866\_replaced([11148389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be updated only if PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and number of subcells per cell is two (5G\_UP\_2470\_replaced([11389618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufPCk_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

When a virtual UE is constructed completely, L2PS shall decide whether tapering status of the UE (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9866\_replaced([11148389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) included in virtual UE shall be updated or not.

1) If paired UEs are scheduled in the same MU-IRC receiver, tapering shall not happen on these paired UEs.

2) If three UEs paired and scheduled in the different subcells, UE1 and UE2 are scheduled in the 1st subcell, UE3 is scheduled in the 2nd subcell.

If **at least one of DeltaHorDeg(UE3,UE1), DeltaHorDeg(UE3,UE2) is larger than rdMinTaperingDegThreshold(5G\_UP\_ALG\_15700\_replaced([11149594](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksO8ovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** AND smaller than rdMaxTaperingDegThreshold(5G\_UP\_ALG\_15841\_replaced([11149607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksO8pPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ,\*\*\*\*

Tapering status in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9866\_replaced([11148389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall not update.

Else

Tapering shall not be applied to all UEs.

End

3) If four UEs paired and scheduled in the different subcells, UE1 and UE2 are scheduled in the 1st subcell, UE3 and UE4 is scheduled in the 2nd subcell.

If **at least two of DeltaHorDeg(UE1, UE4) , DeltaHorDeg(UE1, UE3), DeltaHorDeg(UE2, UE3) and DeltaHorDeg(UE2, UE4) is larger than rdMinTaperingDegThreshold(5G\_UP\_ALG\_15700\_replaced([11149594](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksO8ovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** AND smaller than rdMaxTaperingDegThreshold(5G\_UP\_ALG\_15841\_replaced([11149607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksO8pPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ,\*\*\*\*

The tapering status in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9866\_replaced([11148389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall not update.

Else

Tapering shall not be applied to all UEs.

End

4) If only two UEs paired and scheduled in different SU-IRC receiver:

If DeltaHorDeg(UE1, UE2) is larger than rdMinTaperingDegThreshold **(5G\_UP\_ALG\_15700\_replaced([11149594](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksO8ovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** AND smaller than rdMaxTaperingDegThreshold (5G\_UP\_ALG\_15841\_replaced([11149607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksO8pPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ,\*\*\*\*

Tapering status in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9866\_replaced([11148389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall not update.

Else

Tapering shall not be applied to all UEs.

End

1. If PUSCH is received over 8 or 16 spatial streams, tapering status in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9866\_replaced([11148389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be updated as follows:

For UE(i) within virtual UE(A), [PR843278] when determining whether to apply a tapered beam or a non‑tapered beam, gNB shall exclude UEs performing FDM on the same MU-MIMO layer as UE(i) firstly. Subsequently, only the paired UEs from the remaining MU‑MIMO layers shall be considered, and perform the check of horizontal angle difference DeltaHorDeg(UEi,UEj). [End PR843278] If at least one paired UE has an angle difference with UE(i) ---DeltaHorDeg(UEi,UEj) which is less than or equal to the threshold rdMinTaperingDegThreshold, UE(i) will be reconfigured with a non‑tapered beam.

**NOTE:**

1) DeltaHorDeg(UE(i),UE(j)) = abs(HorDeg(UE(i)) - HorDeg(UE(j))), HorDegUE(i) shall be the 1st best beam of UE(i) in horizontal degree, detailed information refer to 5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_5955\_replaced([11296085](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TqFesPvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) Tapering status in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9866\_replaced([11148389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall not be updated always if root UE paired with the candidate UE group.

3) [CB014094-C] Note: Since osDFT beams are refreshed at the t0 of each beam update period, it is possible that NIDD:actUlMuMimoTapering and NIDD:actUlMuMimo become enabled after t0 but before the next update period begins. During this transient interval, if both parameters are set to true but no tapered beams are yet available, L2RT shall temporarily use the non‑tapered beam for MU-MIMO UEs until the tapered beams become available. [End CB014094-C]

[End PR840715]

NOTE: For re-transmission UE(i), it shall be neither paired with a candidate UE group nor be added to a candidate UE group .

#### 3.10.3.6.1 Decision to execute virtual UE construction

#### 3.10.3.6.1-1 Decision to execute virtual UE construction

**3.10.3.6.1-1.0-1**  (ID: `11146526`)

Decision to execute virtual UE construction
Only the UEs with the  same IEs in DMRS-UplinkConfig could be paired with each other:

* The same additional DMRS position and DMRS type.

The detailed algorithm refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9536\_replaced([11147413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksGZyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Rationale: If DMRS symbol's position is different between the paired UEs, DMRS signal of UE will be interferenced with other UE's PUSCH signal and it will impact MU performance.

---

#### 3.10.3.6.1-2 Decision to execute virtual UE construction

**3.10.3.6.1-2.0-1**  (ID: `11146560`)

Decision to execute virtual UE construction
1) If PRB requirement of the root UE is below NIDD:NRCELL/ulMuMimoParaSet/ulMinPrbThreshold, the required number of PRBs of candidate UE(i) need to satisfy the following condition:

abs(UEi *∈ rrmUlMuCandidateList | Nroot - Ni )*≤ ulMuMimoPrbThresholdAbsolute

2) If PRB requirement of the root UE is above NIDD:NRCELL/ulMuMimoParaSet/ulMinPrbThreshold, the required number of PRBs of candidate UE(i) need to satisfy the following condition:

(abs(UEi *∈ rrmUlMuCandidateList | Nroot - Ni ) / Nroot* ) ≤ ulMuMimoPrbThresholdRatio

where,

- Ni is the number of required PRB for UE(i) **[CB008360-B] or a candidate UE group (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9690\_replaced([11148139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksI2BPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The required number of PRBs of a candidate UE group is the sum of number of PRBs for UEs which are included in this candidate UE group.**[End CB008360-B].\*\*\*\*

- Nroot  is the required number of PRBs of root UE.

-  ulMuMimoPrbThresholdRatio may be different according to the number of PRBs of the root UE. For normal UE pairing ([11145856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCIUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)),  ulMuMimoPrbThresholdRatio is equal to NIDD parameters of prbThreshRangeOne, prbThreshRangeTwo and prbThreshRangeThree. **[PR745811] For candidate UE group pairing ([11148139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksI2BPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), it is equal to equal to rdUeGroupPrbThdRatio ([5G\_UP\_ALG\_26254](https://gates.nsn-net.net/requirement/5G_UP_ALG_26254))**[End PR745811]\*\*\*\*

-  **ulMuMimoPrbThresholdAbsolute may be different according to the number of PRBs of the root UE. For normal UE pairing ([11145856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCIUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)),  ulMuMimoPrbThresholdRatio is equal to NIDD parameters of prbThreshRangeOne, prbThreshRangeTwo and prbThreshRangeThree.** [PR745811] For candidate UE group pairing([11148139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksI2BPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), it is equal to rdUeGroupPrbThdAbsolute ([5G\_UP\_ALG\_26253](https://gates.nsn-net.net/requirement/5G_UP_ALG_26253)) **[End PR745811]**\*\*\*\*

---

##### 3.10.3.6.1.0-1 Decision to execute virtual UE construction Overall of MU Trigger Condition (ID: 11146450)

**3.10.3.6.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11146471`)

Decision to execute virtual UE construction
Step1: At the beginning of the slot before any virtual UE construction, L2RT should calculate the rrmAvailablePrbForMu, rrmRequiredMuPrbNum for non-GBR UEs which are included in rrmUlMuCandidateList (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9554\_replaced([11146147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCvavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rrmUlNonMuCandidateList  (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9554\_replaced([11146147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCvavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))).

1.1) Total available PRB number rrmAvailablePrbForMu which can be used for non-GBR UEs;

rrmAvailablePrbForMu =  availablePrbNumForPusch – rrmPrbNumNotAvailableForMu which is initialized with non-GBR initial transmission UEs which don't satisfy the MU candidates conditions, where availablePrbNumForPusch see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4876\_replaced([11196884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwGI9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)); rrmPrbNumNotAvailableForMu see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4871\_replaced([11196450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwCepPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));

Note: rrmAvailablePrbForMu shall keep the same value at the same slot.

1.2) Total required PRB number rrmRequiredMuPrbNum for UEs of all non-GBR UEs in current slot;

Step2: During the period of a virtual UE construction when adding a new candidate UE to the legacy virtual UE successfully or after this virtual UE is constructed completely, rrmRequiredMuPrbNum will be updated according to the total number of required PRBs for virtual UEs and remaining UEs.

If rrmRequiredMuPrbNum > rrmAvailablePrbForMu \* rdUlPrbScaleRatio(5G\_UP\_ALG\_14881\_replaced([11149436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2RT shall continue constructing virtual UE.

When NRBTS.actUlMuMimo = TRUE and slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = FALSE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2PS shall check the condition in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10778\_replaced([11146450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksD9jPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) before any virtual UE construction;

when NRBTS.actUlMuMimo = TRUE and slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB009363-F] and PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and number of subcells per cell is two (5G\_UP\_2470\_replaced([11389618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufPCk_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))): [End CB009363-F]

* L2PS shall check the additional condition with PRB pooling defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14781\_replaced([11146479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksEkkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) before any virtual UE construction;
* the value of rrmAvailablePrbForMu, rrmRequiredMuPrbNum and rrmSchedWeights could be updated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9573\_replaced([11147551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHA3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

##### 3.10.3.6.1.0-2 Decision to execute virtual UE construction MU Trigger Condition With Stream PRB Pooling (ID: 11146479)

**3.10.3.6.1.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11146511`)

Decision to execute virtual UE construction
- If NRBTS.NRCELL.actUlMuMimo = TRUE and slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE [CB009363-F] and PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and number of subcells per cell is two (5G\_UP\_2470\_replaced([11389618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufPCk_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB009363-F] , at the beginning of the slot before any virtual UE construction, L2RT should check:

IF numAllocCellPrb <= maxNumPrbLimitToUsePerUlBw OR ((TddUlPrbMutingWorkaroundAllowed = TRUE OR ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed = TRUE) AND numActiveUlSubcells <= 1)

* only primary subcell is allowed to be used
* Physical cell PRB condition check in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10778\_replaced([11146450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksD9jPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is enough and if the condition therein is satisfied, only UEs with rank1 transmission can do MU pairing (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10778\_replaced([11146450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksD9jPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) .

ELSE IF rrmRequiredMuPrbNum < = (availablePrbNumForPusch – rrmPrbNumNotAvailableForMu) \*rdUlPrbScaleRatio(5G\_UP\_ALG\_14881\_replaced([11149436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Skip UL spatial domain scheduling, start UL frequency domain scheduling

ELSE

* start UL spatial domain scheduling
* During virtual UE construction, L2PS should do cell physical PRBs checking (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10778\_replaced([11146450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksD9jPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) firstly and then number of available subcell PRBs checking 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10770\_replaced([11147657](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHn4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

END

where:

* maxNumPrbLimitToUsePerUlBw : the maximum number of physical (cell) PRBs within the UL cell BW that can be used for any scheduling per slot. The value can be determined as:
* maxNumPrbLimitToUsePerUlBw = rrmNumPuschPrbDedicatedBwp + numPrbToBeUsedForPucch
* rrmNumPuschPrbDedicatedBwp (defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4974\_replaced([11199486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwOEw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* numPrbToBeUsedForPucch: corresponds to the amount of PRB required for PUCCH in the considered UL slot excluding the PUCCH PRBs (if any) to be used for carrying A/N of RA-the common PUCCH (Msg4/SRB0...) or any transmissions for a UE without UE dedicated configuration activated (5G\_UP\_ALG\_4876\_replaced([11196884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwGI9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB010544-A] including the UE in the initial BWP without dedicated configuration [End CB010544-A].
* availablePrbNumForPusch: PRB avaliable only for PUSCH in the UL slot, excluding PRBs (if any) used for PRACH and PUCCH carrying A/N of Msg4/SRB0 or any transmissions for a UE without UE dedicated configuration activated as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4876\_replaced([11196884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwGI9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB010544-A] including the UE in the initial BWP without dedicated configuration [End CB010544-A].
* rrmPrbNumNotAvailableForMu is the number of PRB not available for MU-MIMO allocation as per 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11537\_replaced([11196874](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwGI9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ));
* rrmRequiredMuPrbNum (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10778\_replaced([11146450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksD9jPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));
* numAllocCellPrb is total number of usable subcel PRBs granted BBRM see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* rdUlPrbScaleRatio(5G\_UP\_ALG\_14881\_replaced([11149436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* ulSubcellDeactForARMAllowed is the flag to enable/disable the L1 ARM capacity based subcell deactivation procedure in UL (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18301\_replaced([11213855](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* numActiveUlSubcells is the number of subcells in UL activated for the current cell by the BBRM in the current BB pooling period (refer 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13411\_replaced([11212398](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxBWAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18301\_replaced([11213855](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxKf8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Rationale for the different cases defined above:
* when the total number of available subcell PRBs is not in excess of what can be used on a single subcell (i.e. maxNumPrbLimitToUsePerUlBw), there is no need to use secondary subcell, hence, only one (primary) subcell is used.
* when the total required PRBs of UEs in the rrmUlMuCandidateList is smaller than what is available, there is no gain from spatial domain multiplexing as the UEs could still be able to get the required PRB amount share with FDM. In addition, having sufficient PRBs, serving the UEs with SU provides better UE performance due to the better SINR in comparision to MU mode.
* Reason for preferring to use only one subcell to schedule rank2 UEs using FDM with SU mode when the total number of subcell PRBs (numAllocCellPrb) is less than or equal to what can be used on a single subcell, is described with example as below:-
* e,g UE1 requires 100 PRBs, UE2 requires 100PRBs, numAllocCellPrb = 100, the number of PRBs in the UL bandwidth =273. If UE1 and UE2 are paired to one virtual UE, allocated at two subcells, then UE1 is allocated to 50 PRBs and UE2 also is allocated to 50 PRBs. But If UE1 and UE2 does SU transmission, then each UE can be allocated to 50 PRBs. Although two UEs get same number of PRBs at MU and SU, but SINR of MU is less than SINR of SU. For performance point of view, it is better to allocate the two UE at one subcell.

---

##### 3.10.3.6.2.0-1 Correlation check Criterion for correlation check (ID: 11146572)

**3.10.3.6.2.0-1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11146598`)

Correlation check

**3.10.3.6.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11146607`)

Correlation check
Criterion of correlation check

---

**3.10.3.6.2.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11146610`)

Correlation check
min-max correlation check

---

**3.10.3.6.2.0-1.0-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11146635`)

Correlation check
11146635:
Correlation check
L2RT shall use below min-max algorithm to select candidate UEs which can be added into virtualUE(A).
 [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$I\_A = \underset{{i \in \text{rrmUlMuCandidateList}} \& \& {i \in \text{virtualUE}(A)}}{\operatorname{argmin}} \left( \underset{j \in \text{virtualUE}(A)}{\max} \max(\text{corr}*{i,j}, \text{corr}*{j,i}) \right)$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9253.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
where  [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "corrᵢ,ⱼ".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9253.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] and [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "CORRj,i".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9253.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9525\_replaced([11146916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFysPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
 
For example: assume there has 2 UEs (j1, j2) in virtual UE, and another 3 UEs (i1, i2, i3) in rrmMuCandidateList.
 
1) Calculate correlation for each MU candidate UE with virtual UE:
 corrUe(i1) = max{ max(corr(i1, j1), corr(j1, i1)), max(corr(i1, j2), corr(j2, i1)) }
 corrUe (i2) = max{ max(corr(i2, j1), corr(j1, i2)), max(corr(i2, j2), corr(j2, i2)) }
 corrUe(i3) = max{ max(corr(i3, j1), corr(j1, i3)), max(corr(i3, j2), corr(j2, i3)) }
 
2) Select a UE(i) with smallest correlation with UEs in virtual UE, and minCorr < NIDD:NRCELL/NRDLMUMIMO/dlMuMimoCorrThd or NRBTS.NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMuMimoCorrThd2.
 minCorr = min {corrUe(i1), corrUe(i2), corrUe(i3)}
 
   [image-3][image\_desc]The image displays a diagram illustrating correlations between different User Equipment (UE) entities. There are three UE entities on the left side, labeled UE\_i1, UE\_i2, and UE\_i3, arranged vertically. On the right side, there are two UE entities, labeled UE\_j1 and UE\_j2, arranged vertically.
Arrows indicate correlations between these UEs.
- A red arrow originates from UE\_i2 and points to UE\_j1, labeled "Corr\_i1j1". This label appears to be a typo and should likely be "Corr\_i2j1" given the arrow's origin.
- Another red arrow originates from UE\_i2 and points to UE\_j2, labeled "Corr\_i1j2". Similar to the previous label, this likely should be "Corr\_i2j2".
- A blue arrow originates from UE\_i3 and points to UE\_j1.
- Another blue arrow originates from UE\_i3 and points to UE\_j2.
The diagram visually represents potential interference or correlation relationships between different user devices in a network.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9253.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

---

**3.10.3.6.2.0-1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11146643`)

Correlation check
suboptimal correlation check

---

**3.10.3.6.2.0-1.0-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11146664`)

Correlation check
11146664:
Correlation check
In order to save CPU load, L2RT shall use below suboptimal algorithm to select candidate UEs which can be added into virtualUE(A).
 [image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or table present.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9255.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
where  [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "corrᵢ,ⱼ".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9255.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] and [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "CORRj,i".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9255.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9525\_replaced([11146916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFysPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
 
For example: assume there has 2 UEs (j1, j2) in virtual UE, and another 3 UEs (i1, i2, i3) in rrmMuCandidateList.
 
1) Calculate correlation for each MU candidate UE with virtual UE:
 corrUe(i1) = max{ max(corr(i1, j1), corr(j1, i1)), max(corr(i1, j2), corr(j2, i1)) }
 corrUe (i2) = max{ max(corr(i2, j1), corr(j1, i2)), max(corr(i2, j2), corr(j2, i2)) }
 corrUe(i3) = max{ max(corr(i3, j1), corr(j1, i3)), max(corr(i3, j2), corr(j2, i3)) }
 
 if (corrUe(i1)  < minCorr)
 {
                  L2RT shall add UE\_i1 into virtual UE
 }
 else if (corrUe (i2)  < minCorr)
 {
  L2RT shall add UE\_i2 into virtual UE
 }
 else  if (corrUe(i3) <  minCorr }
 {
  L2RT shall add UE\_i2 into virtual UE
 }
 
where, minCorr is equal to NRBTS.NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMuMimoCorrThd or NRBTS.NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMuMimoCorrThd2.
 
 
   [image-3][image\_desc]The image displays a diagram illustrating correlations between different User Equipment (UE) entities. Candidate UE(i) can be added into virtualUE(A) when the following two conditions are satisfied:

1)  If NRBTS.NRCELL.nrCellType is configured to xDL4UL, the correlation between the candidate [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains the letters "I" and "A" with a subscript "a" next to the "I". The letters are stylized and appear to be in a metallic or glass-like material with reflections. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9258.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]and virtualUE(A) shall be equal or smaller than the value of  NIDD:NRCELL/ULMUMIMOPARASET/ulMuMimoCorrThd.

2) If NRBTS.NRCELL.nrCellType is configured to xDL8UL,

* 2.1) If the rank of the root UE is 2, L2PS shall find candidate [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the letters "I" and "A" with a subscript "a" next to the "I". The letters are stylized and appear to be in a metallic or glass-like material with reflections. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9258.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]whose correlation with virtualUE(A) is equal or smaller than the value of  NIDD:NRCELL/ULMUMIMOPARASET/ulMuMimoCorrThd2 AND sinr diff satisfy 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17790\_replaced([11147104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFysvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* 2.2) If the rank of the root UE is 1, AND

- 2.2.1) If the candidate UE with the minimum correlation is NOT larger than NIDD:NRCELL/ULMUMIMOPARASET/ulMuMimoCorrThd2 and the sinr diff satisfy 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17790\_replaced([11147104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFysvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then other MU checks shall be performed until the maximum number of MU layers is reached. NOTE: The maximum number of layers for this virtual UE is NIDD:NRCELL/ULMUMIMOPARASET/ulMaxMuMimoLayer.

- 2.2.2) Else if the candidate UE with the minimum correlation is larger than NIDD:NRCELL/ULMUMIMOPARASET/ulMuMimoCorrThd2 but NOT larger than NIDD:NRCELL/ULMUMIMOPARASET/ulMuMimoCorrThd  without SINR diff check in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17790\_replaced([11147104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFysvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) , OR the candidate UEs whose correlation is NOT larger than NIDD:NRCELL/ULMUMIMOPARASET/ulMuMimoCorrThd2 but doesn't satisfy sinr diff check in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17790\_replaced([11147104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFysvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then other MU checks shall be performed until one rank1 candidate UE is added into this virtual UE.

NOTE: In step 2.2.2), MU checks shall not include SINR diff check in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17790\_replaced([11147104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFysvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) because only two rank1 UEs can be paired and MU-IRC receiver will be used for this virtual UE. Considering the performance of MU-IRC receiver, sinr diff check can be ignored in this case.

Rationale: Although MCS of user pairing is independent, the users with close channel quality will firstly be selected in order to prevent big demodulation performance difference between users, because strong signal user can generate large interference to the weak signal user.

If rdMuIrcCorr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31287\_replaced([11149936](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is equal to "1",**L2RT shall use** suboptimal**correlation check, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28847\_replaced([11146643](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFLpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**\*\*\*\*

L2RT shall find the UEs with the same DMRS configuration to be paired firstly only when suboptimal correlation check is used.

The candidate UEs can be added into virtualUE(A) when the following conditions are satisfied:

**step1: After the root UE is selected, during the period to find the first candidate UE(j) that can be paired with root UE, the correlation between root UE and the candidate UE(j) shall NOT be larger than the value of NRCELL/ULMUMIMOPARASET/ulMuMimoCorrThd;**

**step2: When the number of UEs in virtualUE(A) is euqal to or larger than two at stage N, only if the sinr diff for these UEs satisfy the condition in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17790\_replaced([11147104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFysvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), L2PS shall continue to add the next candidate UE(k) into this virtualUE(A) at stage N+1 if it satisfied the following conditions:**

- correlation between UE(k) and all of UEs in virtualUE(A) at stage N is NOT be larger than the value of NIDD:NRCELL/ULMUMIMOPARASET/ulMuMimoCorrThd2;

- SINR diff between UE(k) and the UEs in virtualUE(A) at stage N satisfy 5G\_UP\_ALG\_17790\_replaced([11147104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFysvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**Rationale: 1, When more than two UEs are paired, it will bring higher intra-cell interference. In order to avoid MU-SINR drop dramatically when the number of paired UEs increased, only the UEs which have low enough correlation with all of the UEs in the virtualUE(A) can be added into virtual UE.  2, During the procedure to add candidate UEs into virtualUE(A), L2PS have no knowledge how many UEs will be added into virutalUE(A) finally. So, two correlation thresholds shall be used.**

In order to avoid the possible CPU load issue, the following simplified algorithm is considered and it can be triggered by setting the value of NRCELL/ULMUMIMOPARASET/ulMuMimoCorrThd to 1.

If NRCELL/ULMUMIMOPARASET/ulMuMimoCorrThd is equal to 1 && NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is equal to or larger than 8RX.

L2PS shall check the horizontal and vertical degree separation between the candidate UE(j) and all of the UEs in virtualUE(A) according to the following condition:

The algorithm to estimate correlation based on interference between UE(i) and UE(j) is as following:

**Step1: Calculate correlation based on interference from UE(j) to UE(i):**

L2RT shall estimate UL BF gain of UE(i) based on the kth best beam.

[image-6][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is presented in a multi-line format, with several equalities shown.
The equation starts with $G\_{i,w\_{i,k}}$ and is followed by an equals sign.
The next part of the equation is the squared norm of a vector: $||w\_{i,k}^H h\_i||^2$.
This is then followed by another equals sign and the expansion of the squared norm: $(w\_{i,k}^H h\_i)(w\_{i,k}^H h\_i)^H$.
The next equality shows the result of the conjugate transpose: $w\_{i,k}^H h\_i h\_i^H w\_{i,k}$.
Finally, the last line shows another equality: $w\_{i,k}^H R\_i w\_{i,k}$.
The symbols used are:
- $G\_{i,w\_{i,k}}$: A variable or function name.
- $w\_{i,k}$: A vector, possibly a weight vector, with indices $i$ and $k$.
- $h\_i$: A vector, possibly a channel or channel estimate, with index $i$.
- $H$: Superscript indicating the conjugate transpose (Hermitian transpose).
- $|| \cdot ||^2$: The squared Euclidean norm.
- $R\_i$: A matrix, possibly a covariance matrix, with index $i$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9265.001.png[/image\_path][/image-6]

* **If the condition in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9866\_replaced([11148389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is satisfied, [image-7][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Wi,k" in a blurry, stylized font. The letters are a warm orange-brown color with a slight blue and red halo effect, suggesting a digital rendering or a photographic effect. The letters are a warm orange-brown color with a slight blue and red halo effect, suggesting a digital rendering or a photographic effect. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9265.002.png[/image\_path][/image-8] is beamforming weight vector of the kth best non-tapered beam for UE(i), where the size of [image-9][image\_desc]The image contains the text "Wi,k" in a blurry, stylized font. The interference from UE(j) to UE(i) is estimated as following:

$G\_{j,w\_{i,k}} = |w\_{i,k}^H h\_j|^2 = (w\_{i,k}^H h\_j)(w\_{i,k}^H h\_j)^H = w\_{i,k}^H h\_j h\_j^H w\_{i,k} = w\_{i,k}^H R\_j w\_{i,k}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9265.005.png[/image\_path][/image-12]

Note: Since osDFT beams are refreshed at the t0 of each beam update period, it is possible that NIDD:actUlMuMimoTapering and NIDD:actUlMuMimo become enabled after t0 but before the next update period begins. During this transient interval, if both parameters are set to true but no tapered beams are yet available, L2RT shall temporarily use the non‑tapered beam for MU-MIMO UEs until the tapered beams become available.

Considering L1 reports short-term CoMa on horizontal and vertical direction separately, 5G\_L2\_PS uses IIR filter to calculate long-term CoMa, and UL beams are oversampled 2D-DFT beams, then the UL BF gain can be approximately calculated as below equation:

[image-19][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in white text against a black background. The equation is presented in two lines.
The first line reads:
$G\_{l,w\_{l,k}} = w\_{l,k}^H R\_{i,k} w\_{l,k} = (w\_{l,k,v} \otimes w\_{l,k,h})^H (R\_{i,v} \otimes R\_{i,h}) (w\_{l,k,v} \otimes w\_{l,k,h})$
The second line reads:
$= (w\_{l,k,v}^H R\_{i,v} w\_{l,k,v}) (w\_{l,k,h}^H R\_{i,h} w\_{l,k,h})$
The equation involves several variables with subscripts and superscripts, including $G$, $w$, $R$, $i$, $l$, $k$, $v$, and $h$. The superscript $H$ denotes the conjugate transpose. The symbol $\otimes$ represents the Kronecker product.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9265.010.png[/image\_path][/image-19]

Until now, the correlation based on interference from UE(j) to UE(i) can be got as following:

If rdMuInfCorr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14885\_replaced([11149457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is configured to true,[image-27][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is for "Corri,j" and is presented as a fraction.
The numerator is:
$(G\_{j,w\_{i,1}} + G\_{j,w\_{i,2}})/(\text{trace}(R\_{j,v}) \* \text{trace}(R\_{j,h})/(N\_h \* N\_v))$
The denominator is:
$(G\_{i,w\_{i,1}} + G\_{i,w\_{i,2}})/(\text{trace}(R\_{i,v}) \* \text{trace}(R\_{i,h})/(N\_h \* N\_v))$
The formula can be written as:
$Corr\_{i,j} = \frac{(G\_{j,w\_{i,1}} + G\_{j,w\_{i,2}})/(\text{trace}(R\_{j,v}) \* \text{trace}(R\_{j,h})/(N\_h \* N\_v))}{(G\_{i,w\_{i,1}} + G\_{i,w\_{i,2}})/(\text{trace}(R\_{i,v}) \* \text{trace}(R\_{i,h})/(N\_h \* N\_v))}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9265.020.png[/image\_path][/image-27]

- trace(R) returns sum of diagonal elements in matrix R;

The letters are colored in shades of blue and orange, with a slight gradient effect. - rdVerticalCorr see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_18315\_replaced([11149620](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksO8pvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

if rdMuInfCorr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14885\_replaced([11149457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is configured to true,

**Step3: The final correlation between UE(i) and UE(j) is decided by the max value.**

[image-37][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a sans-serif font. The equation reads: Corr = max(Corr\_{i,j}, Corr\_{j,i}). The text is black and appears on a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9265.032.png[/image\_path][/image-37]

**Note:**

1) If **rdMuInfCorr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14885\_replaced([11149457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is configured to false, only the beamforming weights of the 1st best beam is used; otherwise, the beamforming weights of two best beams are used. The default value of rdMuInfCorr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14885\_replaced([11149457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is false.**

2) [image-38][image\_desc]Gj,w1,k[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9265.033.png[/image\_path][/image-38]and [image-39][image\_desc]The image contains the text "G₁,w₁,k".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9265.034.png[/image\_path][/image-39] are positive values which are represented by their real part.

3) When rdMuInfCorr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14885\_replaced([11149457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is configured to true and if the second best beam can't be found for at least one UE, L2RT shall calculate correlation according to the algorithm in case of rdMuInfCorr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14885\_replaced([11149457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuivvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is false.

#### 3.10.3.6.3 Spectrum efficiency check

##### 3.10.3.6.3-1 Spectral efficiency of virtual UE

**3.10.3.6.3-1.0-1**  (ID: `11147401`)

Spectral efficiency of virtual UE
When NRCELL.actUlMuMimo is TRUE:

IF (NIDD: ulMuMimoLinkAdaptionSwitch = 0)  // MU-SINR estimation

To simplify implementation(avoid prb compensation and don't use reserved mcs), Mu sinr of reTx UE in virtual UE should meet the condition in [11148330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksJdGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) if NIDD: numberOfRxBeamforming is equal to 4.

ELSE // ulMuMimoLinkAdaptionSwitch =1, MCS compensation

pairedLayers of reTx UE <= pairedLayers of the UE in initial transmission

where,

The definition of pairedLayers refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20424\_replaced([11149069](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksL5XvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

End

11147203:
Spectrum efficiency check
The normalized spectrum efficiency for UE(i) in virtualUE(A) at stage N is defined as below:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in white text against a black background. The equation is:
$\epsilon\_{i,N} = R\_i \* Qm\_i \* Layer\_i$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9272.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

-        Ri and Qmi are coding rate and modulation order of UE(i) according to selected MCS using MU-SINR if NIDD:NRBTS/NRCELL/ulMuMimoParaSet/ulMuMimoLinkAdaptionSwitch is configured to 0 (5G\_UP\_ALG\_8348\_replaced([11148500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEMfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), OR MCS adjustment if NIDD: NRBTS/NRCELL/ulMuMimoParaSet/ulMuMimoLinkAdaptionSwitch is configured to 1(5G\_UP\_ALG\_8349\_replaced([11148930](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksLSS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

##### 3.10.3.6.3.1 Spectral efficiency of virtual UE

###### 3.10.3.6.3.1.0-1 Spectral efficiency of virtual UE Blind pairing without Spectral efficiency check (ID: 11147255)

**3.10.3.6.3.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11147274`)

Spectral efficiency of virtual UE
**[Before CB008235-A]**

If PUSCH is received over 8 or larger than 8 spatial streams for a given subcell(5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

**[CB008235-A]**

If NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMaxMuMimoLayer is NOT larger than 4 and NRCELL.actUlMuMimo = true:

**[End CB008235-A]**

-If NRBTS.NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMuMimoSpectralEffThd is equal to 0, L2PS shall skip spectrual efficiency check**.**

-Else L2PS shall check spectral efficiency according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10481\_replaced([11147281](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksGZwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10482\_replaced([11147328](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksGZw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[CB008235-A]**

Else if NRCELL.actUlMuMimo = true and NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMaxMuMimoLayer is larger than 4, in order to save CPU load, L2PS shall skip spectrual efficiency check always no matter what is set for NRBTS.NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMuMimoSpectralEffThd.

**[End CB008235-A]**
