###### 3.10.3.6.3.1.0-2 Spectral efficiency of virtual UE Spectral efficiency check if root UE paired with candidate UEs (ID: 11147281)

**3.10.3.6.3.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11147324`)

Spectral efficiency of virtual UE
11147324:
Spectral efficiency of virtual UE
To add one UE(i) at stage N+1 into virtualUE(A):
1) For each existing UE in stage N, the normalized spectrum efficiency (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9529\_replaced([11147182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFyvfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) at stage N+1 is compared to the normalized spectrum efficiency (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9529\_replaced([11147182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFyvfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) at stage N. It is required that  [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical inequality. The inequality is written as:
∀ j ∈ AN, εj,N+1 > γ *εj,N*N / (N+1)
The text is in a mathematical notation. The symbols used are:
- ∀: for all
- ∈: element of
- AN: a set indexed by N
- εj,N+1: a variable or term indexed by j and N+1
- >: greater than
- γ*: a variable or constant gamma with a superscript asterisk
- εj,N: a variable or term indexed by j and N
- N: a variable or constant N
- N+1: N plus 1
The inequality states that for all j belonging to the set AN, the term εj,N+1 is greater than the product of γ*, εj,N*N, divided by N+1.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9281.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
where:
- [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "AN" in a stylized font. The letters are colored with a gradient of blue, orange, and yellow, giving them a metallic or iridescent appearance. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9281.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] is the virtualUE(A) at stage N. N is the size of UEs which are included in the virtual UE.
- [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "E1,N" in a stylized font with a gradient effect. The letters are colored with shades of blue, yellow, and brown, giving them a somewhat metallic or iridescent appearance. The background is white, and the text is positioned in the lower left quadrant of the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9281.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] is the normalized spectrum efficiency (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9529\_replaced([11147182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFyvfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of UE(j) in virtualUE(A) at stage N.
 
-    [image-3][image\_desc]The image is a close-up, blurry, and abstract depiction of what appears to be a stylized letter "Y" or a similar branching symbol. The colors are muted, with shades of brown, beige, and blue blending into each other. The background is a gradient of white to light gray, with a dark border on the right and bottom edges. The overall impression is one of movement and fluidity, with soft edges and a lack of sharp detail.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9281.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] is a R&D parameter of spectrum efficiency threshold which is defined as rdSpectralEfficiency (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14887\_replaced([11149471](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNujPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
 
2) For the new UE(i) to be added at stage N+1, the normalized spectrum efficiency (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9529\_replaced([11147182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFyvfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) at stage N+1 is compared to the SU normalized spectrum efficiency (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9529\_replaced([11147182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFyvfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). It is required that [image-4][image\_desc]$\epsilon\_{i,N+1} > \frac{\gamma \* \epsilon\_{i,SU}}{N+1}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9281.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]
where:
- [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains the text "e₁,su" in a stylized font. The letters are blurred and have a gradient effect, with colors ranging from orange to blue. The text is positioned on a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9281.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5] is the normalized SU spectrum efficiency;
- [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in white text against a white background. The equation is:
$\epsilon\_{i,su} = R\_i \* Qm\_i \* Layer\_i$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9281.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6] where Ri and Qmi are coding rate and modulation order of UE(i) according to selected MCS using SU-SINR.
 
3) An additional checking shall be done as below:
         [image-7][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
$\sum\_{j \in A\_N} \epsilon\_{j,N+1} > \text{ulMuMimoSpectralEffThd} \* (\epsilon\_{1,su} + N^* \sum\_{j \in A\_N} \epsilon\_{j,N}) / (N+1)$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9281.008.png[/image\_path][/image-7]
 -    ulMuMimoSpectralEffThd shall be an O&M parameter with 1.0 by default and further optimized by simulations.

---

###### 3.10.3.6.3.1.0-3 Spectral efficiency of virtual UE Spectral efficiency check if root UE paired with candidate UE group (ID: 11147328)

**3.10.3.6.3.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11147388`)

Spectral efficiency of virtual UE
11147388:
Spectral efficiency of virtual UE
To add one candidate UE group Z (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9690\_replaced([11148139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksI2BPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) at stage N+1 into virtualUE(A):

1) For each existing UE in stage N, the normalized spectrum efficiency (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9529\_replaced([11147182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFyvfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) at stage N+1 is compared to the normalized spectrum efficiency (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9529\_replaced([11147182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFyvfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) at stage N. It is required that [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical inequality. The inequality states that for all $j$ in $A\_N$, $\epsilon\_{j,N+1}$ is greater than $\frac{\gamma^ *\epsilon\_{j,N}^* N}{N+1}$. The symbols used are:
- $\forall$: for all
- $j \in A\_N$: $j$ belongs to the set $A\_N$
- $\epsilon\_{j,N+1}$: epsilon subscript $j, N+1$
- $> $: greater than
- $\gamma^*$: gamma star
- $\epsilon\_{j,N}^*$: epsilon subscript $j, N$ star
- $N$: N
- $N+1$: N+1[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9283.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

where,

- [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "AN" in a stylized font. The letters are colored with a gradient of blue, orange, and yellow, giving them a metallic or iridescent appearance. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9283.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] is the virtualUE(A) at stage N.

- [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "E1,N" in a stylized font with a gradient effect. The letters are colored with shades of blue, yellow, and brown, giving them a somewhat metallic or iridescent appearance. The background is white, and the text is positioned in the lower left quadrant of the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9283.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] is the normalized spectrum efficiency of UE(j) in virtualUE(A) at stage N.

-    [image-3][image\_desc]The image is a close-up, blurry, and abstract depiction of what appears to be a stylized letter "Y" or a similar branching symbol. The colors are muted, with shades of brown, beige, and hints of blue and white. The lighting creates a soft, diffused effect, with a gradient from darker tones on the left to lighter tones on the right. The overall impression is one of movement or flow, with blurred edges and a lack of sharp definition. The background is predominantly white, with a subtle shadow or glow effect around the edges of the central element.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9283.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] is a R&D parameter of spectrum efficiency threshold which is defined as rdSpectralEfficiency (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14887\_replaced([11149471](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNujPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

2) For the candidate UE group Z to be added at stage N+1, assume this candidate UE group Z as one UE ,and assume all the UEs in the candidate UE group Z allocate the same PRB number and then estimate the normalized spectrum efficiency at stage N+1 compared to the SU normalized spectrum efficiency. It is required that[image-4][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical inequality. The inequality reads: "For all j in A\_N, epsilon\_{z,N+1} > gamma \* epsilon\_{z,N} / (N+1)". The symbols used are: "∀" (for all), "j" (a variable), "∈" (element of), "A\_N" (a set indexed by N), "ε" (epsilon, a Greek letter often used for error or small quantities), "z" (a subscript, likely representing a dimension or index), "N" (an index), "+1" (addition), ">" (greater than), and "γ" (gamma, another Greek letter often used as a constant or parameter). The expression is typeset in a standard mathematical format, with subscripts and a fraction.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9283.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4], where

-   [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$\epsilon\_{Z,N} = \sum\_{ue(i) \in Z} \epsilon\_{i,SU} / M$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9283.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5]

-  [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$\varepsilon\_{Z,N+1} = \sum\_{ue(i) \in Z} \varepsilon\_{i,N+1} / M$
The equation defines $\varepsilon\_{Z,N+1}$ as the sum of $\varepsilon\_{i,N+1}$ for all $i$ in the set $Z$, divided by $M$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9283.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6]

- [image-7][image\_desc]The image contains the text "e₁,su" in a stylized font. The letters are blurred and have a gradient effect, with colors ranging from orange to blue. The text is positioned on a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9283.008.png[/image\_path][/image-7] is the normalized SU spectrum efficiency,[image-8][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in white text against a white background. The equation is:
$\epsilon\_{i,su} = R\_i \* Qm\_i \* Layer\_i$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9283.009.png[/image\_path][/image-8] where Ri and Qmi are coding rate and modulation order of UE(i) according to selected MCS using SU-SINR.

-   M is the UE number in candidate UE group Z.

- [image-9][image\_desc]The image is a close-up, blurry, and abstract depiction of what appears to be a stylized letter "Y" or a similar branching symbol. The colors are muted, with shades of brown, beige, and hints of blue and white. The lighting creates a soft, diffused effect, with a gradient from darker tones on the left to lighter tones on the right. The overall impression is one of movement or flow, with blurred edges and a lack of sharp definition. The background is predominantly white, with a subtle shadow or glow effect around the edges of the central element.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9283.004.png[/image\_path][/image-9] is a R&D parameter of spectrum efficiency threshold which is defined as rdSpectralEfficiency (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14887\_replaced([11149471](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNujPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The default value of rdSpectralEfficiency (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14887\_replaced([11149471](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNujPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be 1.

3) An additional checking shall be done as below, assume candidate UE group Z as one UE for SE checking and step2 result [image-10][image\_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression "εz,N+1".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9283.010.png[/image\_path][/image-10] is used:

[image-11][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
$\sum\_{j \in A\_{N+1}} \varepsilon\_{j, N+1} > ulMuMimoSpectralEffThd \* (\varepsilon\_{z,N} + N^\* \sum\_{j \in A\_N} \varepsilon\_{j,N}) / (N+1)$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9283.011.png[/image\_path][/image-11]

-    ulMuMimoSpectralEffThd shall be an O&M parameter with 1.0 by default and further optimized by simulations.

#### 3.10.3.6.4 Allocate DMRS ports

##### 3.10.3.6.4.0-1 Allocate DMRS ports DMRS ports allocation (ID: 11147413)

**3.10.3.6.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11147420`)

Allocate DMRS ports
**DMRS ports allocation in 4RX**

---

**3.10.3.6.4.0-1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13256462`)

Allocate DMRS ports
If NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming = 4RX and NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMaxMuMimoLayer <= 4

* When the number of subcells per cell equals 1 (as defined in 5G\_UP\_2470\_replaced ([11389618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufPCk_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), only a single 4RX MU-IRC receiver is available in the system.

Under this configuration, up to two rank1 UEs can be paired.

* [CB008148-C] If both UEs use the same waveform, [End CB008148-C] DMRS ports 0 and 1 shall be allocated to the first and second UE, respectively.
* [CB008148-C]

If the two UEs use different waveforms, L2RT shall instead allocate DMRS ports 0 and 2 to the two UEs, respectively.

[End CB008148-C]

* When the number of subcells per cell = 2 (5G\_UP\_2470\_replaced([11389618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufPCk_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), two 4RX receivers are available, and each virtual UE can support up to four MU-MIMO layers.
* For the scenario where all MU-MIMO layer for this virtual UE has only one UE after pairing in [11146323](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksD9hPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksD9hPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9").

  + [CB008148-C] If all UEs have the same waveform [End CB008148-C], the DMRS port allocation shall follow 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10445\_replaced([11104156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kn5POvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  + [CB008148-C] If the virtual UE includes the mixed CP-OFDM and DFT-s-OFDM UEs , L2RT shall allocate DMRS ports for the same waveform UEs in the same CDM group. The 1st CDM group includes the DMRS port0 and port1. The 2nd CDM group includes the DMRS port2 and port3. [End CB008148-C]
* For the scenario where the root UE is paired with a candidate UE group (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9690\_replaced([11148139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksI2BPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB008148-C] regardless the UEs use the same waveform or different waveform [End CB008148-C] ,the DMRS ports shall be assigned as follows:
* Root UE:
  + {0} for 1 layer transmission
  + {0,1} for 2 layer transmission
* The UEs in Candidate UE group ([11148139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksI2BPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):
  + DMRS ports always start from {2}
  + {2} for 1 layer UEs
  + {2,3} for 2 layer UEs

Note:

* For re-transmission UEs included in an MU pair, the DMRS port assignment may differ from that used in the initial transmission.
* DMRS ports allocation shall be different for the paired UEs which share the same frequency domain resource.

**3.10.3.6.4.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11147431`)

Allocate DMRS ports
**DMRS ports allocation in 8RX and 16RX**

---

**3.10.3.6.4.0-1.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `13256542`)

Allocate DMRS ports
If (( NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming = 8RX or 16RX ) and (NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMaxMuMimoLayer <= 4))

* For the scenario where the root UE is paired with several normal UEs,
* If the NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamformin is 8RX**, the DMRS ports allocation shall refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19623\_replaced([11104222](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kn6dUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**
* If the NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamformin is 16RX**, the DMRS ports allocation shall refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_26117\_replaced([11104363](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kn7re_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**
* For the scenario where the root UE is paired with a candidate UE group ([11148139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksI2BPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the DMRS ports allocation shall follow the description for this scenario in [11147420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksGZyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
* [CB008148-C] For the scenario where the same virtual UE include mixed CP-OFDM and DFT-s-OFDM UEs, the DMRS ports allocation shall follow the description for this scenario in [11147420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksGZyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). [End CB008148-C]

If (( NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming = 16RX ) and (NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMaxMuMimoLayer > 4)), refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_28014\_replaced([11147480](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHA0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

* For re-transmission UEs included in an MU pair, the DMRS port assignment may differ from that used in the initial transmission.
* DMRS ports allocation shall be different for the paired UEs which share the same frequency domain resource.

**3.10.3.6.4.0-1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `13248481`)

Allocate DMRS ports
13248481:
Allocate DMRS ports
When NIDD: ulMaxMuMimoLayer is larger than 4, this requirement shall be applied  [CB008148-E] to virtual UE which is constructed by CP-OFDM UEs only.[End CB008148-E]

**1. If the number of MU-MIMO layer for virtualUE(A) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29199\_replaced([11147973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksIO-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is NOT larger than 4, L2PS shall make sure the UEs in virtualUE(A) satisfy the following conditions:**

* UE's capability 'maxLength' in *DMRS-UplinkConfig could be different, but the 'Number of front-load symbols' used in Antenna Port(s) in DCI 0\_1 shall be equal to 1.*
* DMRS port(s) for the paired UEs shall NOT be overlapped.
* 'dmrs-AdditionalPosition' in *DMRS-UplinkConfig shall be the same;*

**2. If the number of MU-MIMO layers for virtualUE(A) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29199\_replaced([11147973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksIO-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is larger than 4, “Number of front-load symbols” and “DMRS ports” for rank1 and rank2 UEs shall belong to index 6-13 in Table 7.3.1.1.2-12 or index 4-7 in Table 7.3.1.1.2-13 defined in 38.212 separately.**

**Example:**

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a grid-like structure, resembling a table, with rows labeled "PRB" from 0 to 15 and columns labeled "layer1" through "layer8". Several cells within this grid are filled with different colors and contain text indicating user equipment (UE) and port assignments.
Here's a breakdown of the filled cells:
\* **layer1:**
\* PRB 0-3: Light green, no text.
\* PRB 4-9: Light blue, labeled "UE1: port 0".
\* PRB 10-12: Dark blue, labeled "UE3: port 0".
\* **layer2:**
\* PRB 4-9: Light blue, labeled "UE2: port 0&1".
\* **layer3:**
\* PRB 3-4: Brown, labeled "UE4: port2".
\* PRB 5-12: Red, labeled "UE5: port2".
\* **layer4:**
\* PRB 3-8: Yellow, no text.
\* **layer5:**
\* PRB 3-8: Dark green, labeled "UE7: port5".
\* **layer6:**
\* PRB 10-12: Peach, labeled "UE6: port3".
\* PRB 13-15: Peach, labeled "UE8: port4".
The remaining cells in the grid are empty and white. A white plus sign cursor is visible over the "UE4: port2" cell in layer3, PRB 3-4.
```markdown

| PRB | layer1 | layer2 | layer3 | layer4 | layer5 | layer6 | layer7 | layer8 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 0 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 1 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 2 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 3 |  |  | UE4: port2 |  |  |  |  |  |
| 4 | UE1: port 0 |  | UE4: port2 |  |  |  |  |  |
| 5 | UE1: port 0 | UE2: port 0&1 | UE5: port2 |  | UE7: port5 |  |  |  |
| 6 | UE1: port 0 | UE2: port 0&1 | UE5: port2 |  | UE7: port5 |  |  |  |
| 7 | UE1: port 0 | UE2: port 0&1 | UE5: port2 |  | UE7: port5 |  |  |  |
| 8 | UE1: port 0 | UE2: port 0&1 | UE5: port2 |  | UE7: port5 |  |  |  |
| 9 | UE1: port 0 | UE2: port 0&1 | UE5: port2 |  |  |  |  |  |
| 10 |  |  | UE5: port2 |  |  | UE6: port3 |  |  |
| 11 |  |  | UE5: port2 |  |  | UE6: port3 |  |  |
| 12 |  |  | UE5: port2 |  |  | UE6: port3 |  |  |
| 13 | UE3: port 0 |  |  |  |  | UE8: port4 |  |  |
| 14 | UE3: port 0 |  |  |  |  | UE8: port4 |  |  |
| 15 | UE3: port 0 |  |  |  |  | UE8: port4 |  |  |
| ```[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-11041916.png[/image\_path][/image-0] |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

Note:

* For re-transmission UEs included in an MU pair, the DMRS port assignment may differ from that used in the initial transmission.
* DMRS ports allocation shall be different for the paired UEs which share the same frequency domain resource.
* The number of DMRS symbols may be different between initial transmission traffic and re-transmission traffic, the detailed algorithm refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27799\_replaced([11148312](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksJdF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

**3.10.3.6.4.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `13248488`)

Allocate DMRS ports
**"Antenna ports "allocation if NIDD:ulMaxMuMimoLayer is larger than 4 and at least one DFT-s-OFDM UE is present in virtual UE(A)**

---

**3.10.3.6.4.0-1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13248489`)

Allocate DMRS ports
When NIDD: ulMaxMuMimoLayer is larger than 4, this requirement shall be applied to virtual UE which includes at least one DFT-s-OFDM UE.

**1. If the number of MU-MIMO layer for virtualUE(A) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29199\_replaced([11147973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksIO-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))) is NOT larger than 4, L2PS shall make sure the UEs in virtualUE(A) satisfy the following conditions:**

* UE's capability 'maxLength' in *DMRS-UplinkConfig could be different, but the 'Number of front-load symbols' used in Antenna Port(s) in DCI 0\_1 shall be equal to 1.*
* DMRS port(s) for the paired UEs shall NOT be overlapped.
* 'dmrs-AdditionalPosition' in *DMRS-UplinkConfig shall be the same;*

2. If all UEs within a virtual UE are DFT-s-OFDM UEs, and each MU-MIMO layer contains only one UE, then L2RT shall determine "Antenna Port(s)" according to Section 2.1 & 2.2 below.

**2.1 If the number of MU-MIMO layers for virtualUE(A) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29199\_replaced (**[11147973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksIO-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))) is larger than 4, “Number of front-load symbols” and “DMRS ports” for DFT-s-OFDM UEs shall belong to index 4~11 in Table 7.3.1.1.2-7 from 3gpp 38.212

**Table 7.3.1.1.2-7: Antenna port(s), transform precoder is enabled, dmrs-Type=1, maxLength=2,  
except that dmrs-UplinkTransformPrecoding and tp-pi2BPSK are both configured and  
π/2-BPSK modulation is used**

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Value** | **Number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data** | **DMRS port(s)** | **Number of front-load symbols** |
| 0 | 2 | 0 | 1 |
| 1 | 2 | 1 | 1 |
| 2 | 2 | 2 | 1 |
| 3 | 2 | 3 | 1 |
| 4 | 2 | 0 | 2 |
| 5 | 2 | 1 | 2 |
| 6 | 2 | 2 | 2 |
| 7 | 2 | 3 | 2 |
| 8 | 2 | 4 | 2 |
| 9 | 2 | 5 | 2 |
| 10 | 2 | 6 | 2 |
| 11 | 2 | 7 | 2 |
| 12-15 | Reserved | Reserved | Reserved |

**2.2 For SU-MIMO UE (initial transmission traffic or re-transmission traffic) or virtualUE(A) whose number of MU-MIMO layers (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29199\_replaced([11147973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksIO-vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is equal or smaller than 4:**

**2.2.1 If they have the capability to support** two front-load DMRS symbols, the value for "Antenna Ports(s)" for DFT-s-OFDM UEs shall belong to index 0-3 in Table Table 7.3.1.1.2-7\*\*\*\*

**Table 7.3.1.1.2-7: Antenna port(s), transform precoder is enabled, dmrs-Type=1, maxLength=2,  
except that dmrs-UplinkTransformPrecoding and tp-pi2BPSK are both configured and  
π/2-BPSK modulation is used**

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Value** | **Number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data** | **DMRS port(s)** | **Number of front-load symbols** |
| 0 | 2 | 0 | 1 |
| 1 | 2 | 1 | 1 |
| 2 | 2 | 2 | 1 |
| 3 | 2 | 3 | 1 |
| 4 | 2 | 0 | 2 |
| 5 | 2 | 1 | 2 |
| 6 | 2 | 2 | 2 |
| 7 | 2 | 3 | 2 |
| 8 | 2 | 4 | 2 |
| 9 | 2 | 5 | 2 |
| 10 | 2 | 6 | 2 |
| 11 | 2 | 7 | 2 |
| 12-15 | Reserved | Reserved | Reserved |

**2.2.2  If they have the capability to support** one front-load DMRS symbols, the value of "Antenna Ports(s)" for DFT-s-OFDM UEs shall belong index 0-3 in Table 7.3.1.1.2-6\*\*\*\*

**Table 7.3.1.1.2-6: Antenna port(s), transform precoder is enabled, dmrs-Type=1, maxLength=1,  
except that dmrs-UplinkTransformPrecoding and tp-pi2BPSK are both configured and  
π/2-BPSK modulation is used**

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Value** | **Number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data** | **DMRS port(s)** |
| 0 | 2 | 0 |
| 1 | 2 | 1 |
| 2 | 2 | 2 |
| 3 | 2 | 3 |

3.If a virtual UE contains at least one DFT-s-OFDM UE and there is at least one MU-MIMO layer that includes more than one UE (regardless of whether the UEs use DFT-s-OFDM or CP-OFDM), or if the virtual UE contains UEs with different waveforms but each MU-MIMO layer has only one UE, then L2RT shall allocate DMRS ports according to the rules below.

3.1 virtual UE contains both CP-OFDM and DFT-s-OFDM UEs and each MU-MIMO layer contains at most one UE.

3.1.1 If the virtual UE’s MU-MIMO layer number is > 4

The DMRS port allocation in each CDM group shall follow Table 6.4.1.1.3-1 of 3GPP 38.211:

* CDM group 0: DMRS ports {0, 1, 4, 5}
* CDM group 1: DMRS ports {2, 3, 6, 7}

When assigning DMRS ports, UEs with the same waveform type shall be placed in the same CDM group. Under this pre-condition, "Antenna Ports(s)" for each UE shall then be determined based on its waveform type.

* For CP-OFDM UEs, the “Antenna Port(s)” shall follow the rule defined in [11147480](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHA0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for cases where the virtual UE’s MU-MIMO layer number is greater than 4
* For DFT-s-OFDM UEs, the “Antenna Port(s)” shall follow the rule defined in Section 2.1 above.

3.1.2 If the virtual UE’s MU-MIMO layer number is ≤ 4

The DMRS port allocation for each CDM group shall follow Table 6.4.1.1.3-1 of 3GPP 38.211:

* CDM group 0: DMRS ports {0, 1}
* CDM group 1: DMRS ports {2, 3}

When assigning DMRS ports, UEs with the same waveform type shall be placed in the same CDM group. Under this pre-condition, "Antenna Ports(s)" for each UE shall then be determined based on its waveform type.

* For CP-OFDM UEs, the “Antenna Port(s)” shall follow the rule in [11147480](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHA0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for cases where the virtual UE’s MU-MIMO layer number is not greater than 4
* For DFT-s-OFDM UEs, the “Antenna Port(s)” shall follow the rule defined in Section 2.2 above.

3.2  Add DFT-s-OFDM beam group in existed virtual UE in Step3 ([11145918](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCIV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

According to the pairing algorithm in Step3 ([11145918](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCIV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the maximum MU-MIMO layer definition after extension in [11145984](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCvYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), if any DFT-s-OFDM beam group is added to the available MU-MIMO layers, the DMRS port allocation for the UEs in such a beam group shall be:

* DMRS ports shall always start from {2}.
* {2} shall be used for 1-layer transmission.
* {2, 3} shall be used for 2-layer transmission.

Because the MU-MIMO layer number for such a virtual UE shall not exceed 4, the “Antenna Port(s)” for each UE shall be determined as follows:

* For CP-OFDM UEs, the “Antenna Port(s)” shall follow the rule defined in [11147480](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHA0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for cases where the virtual UE’s MU-MIMO layer number is not greater than 4.
* For DFT-s-OFDM UEs, the “Antenna Port(s)” shall follow the rule defined in Section 2.2 above.

Example refer to[13254886](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_OgDnEMhyEfCYBIz6acpPHw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

3.3 virtual UE constructed in step5([13284435](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Uc6tMMuKEfCYBIz6acpPHw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))

In step5([13284435](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Uc6tMMuKEfCYBIz6acpPHw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), because at most two beam groups are allowed to share the same PRBs, for the two beam groups that share the same PRBs, the DMRS port allocation for the UEs in the first beam group on the same PRB shall follow the configuration below,

* {0} for 1 layer transmission
* {0,1} for 2 layer transmission

while the DMRS port allocation for the UEs in the second beam group on the same PRB shall be as follows.

* DMRS ports always start from {2}
* {2} for 1 layer UEs
* {2,3} for 2 layer UEs

Because the MU-MIMO layer number for such a virtual UE shall not exceed 4, the “Antenna Port(s)” for each UE shall be determined as follows:

* For CP-OFDM UEs, the “Antenna Port(s)” shall follow the rule defined in [11147480](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHA0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for cases where the virtual UE’s MU-MIMO layer number is not greater than 4.
* For DFT-s-OFDM UEs, the “Antenna Port(s)” shall follow the rule defined in Section 2.2 above.

**4. If only two UEs with one layer are paired no matter they have the same waveform or different waveform, their DMRS antenna ports shall be allocated from different CDM groups. DMRS port 0 shall be assigned to the first UE, and DMRS port 2 shall be assigned to the second UE.**

Note:

* For re-transmission UEs included in an MU pair, the DMRS port assignment may differ from that used in the initial transmission.
* DMRS ports allocation shall be different for MU-MIMO UEs which share the same frequency domain resource. However, their “Antenna Port(s)” may still appear the same because CP-OFDM UEs and DFT-s-OFDM UEs refer to different 3gpp defined tables.
* The number of DMRS symbols may be different between initial transmission traffic and re-transmission traffic, the detailed algorithm refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27799\_replaced([11148312](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksJdF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 3.10.3.6.4.0-2 Allocate DMRS ports About 'Antenna port(s) ' and 'DMRS sequence initialization' in DCI 0_1**** (ID: 11147524)

**3.10.3.6.4.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `13105417`)

Allocate DMRS ports
The value of “Antenna port(s)” in DCI Format 0\_1 shall be determined by the combination of the following parameters:

If NRBTS.NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMaxMuMimoLayer is equal to or smaller than 4, "“Antenna port(s)” is decided as follows:

* Number of front-loaded DMRS symbols is equal to 1.
* DMRS ports, determined according to [11147413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksGZyPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)
* Number of DMRS CDM groups without data is decided by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3098\_replaced([11137832](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krbravvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* DMRS Sequence Initialization:  This is a 1-bit field, and scramblingID0 shall be used.
* [CB008148-C] For CP-OFDM UE, [End CB008148-C] the look up table of "Antenna Port(s) " for rank1 and rank2 UE, refer to Table 7.3.1.1.2-8 and Table 7.3.1.1.2-9 defined in 38.212 separately.
* [CB008148-C] For DFT-s-OFDM UE, the look up table of "Antenna Port(s) ", refer to Table 7.3.1.1.2-6 defined in 38.212.

**Table 7.3.1.1.2-6: Antenna port(s), transform precoder is enabled, dmrs-Type=1, maxLength=1,  
except that dmrs-UplinkTransformPrecoding and tp-pi2BPSK are both configured and  
π/2-BPSK modulation is used**

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Value** | **Number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data** | **DMRS port(s)** |
| 0 | 2 | 0 |
| 1 | 2 | 1 |
| 2 | 2 | 2 |
| 3 | 2 | 3 |

[End CB008148-C]

If NRBTS.NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMaxMuMimoLayer is larger than 4, the number of front-load DMRS symbol is 1 or 2 according to UE's capability. "Antenna port(s)" is decided by [11147480](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHA0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [CB008148-E] and [13248488 separately according](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_YP_6oMSiEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) to UE's waveform [End CB008148-E] and DMRS Sequence Initialization is the same as the description above.

[CB008148-C]

Note:

* If the virtual UE includes the mixed CP-OFDM and DFT-s-OFDM UEs, the value of "Antenna port(s)" may be the same but the DMRS port(s) shall not be overlapped among paired UEs.

[End CB008148-C]

#### 3.10.3.6.5 Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration

#### 3.10.3.6.5-1 Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration

##### 3.10.3.6.5-1.0-1 Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration Number of required PRBs for the virtual UE(A) (ID: 11147797)

**3.10.3.6.5-1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11147866`)

Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration
L2RT shall update it when a new candidate UE is added into virtual UE(A) successfully.

The number of required PRBs for the virtual UE(A):

1.1) If UEs included in the virtual UE(A) are all initial transmission traffic,

[image-0][image\_desc]NumOfRequiredPRB$*{vUE(A)}$ = max$*{l \in L}$ ($\sum\_{i \in U\_1} \alpha\_i \cdot$ NumOfRequiredPRB$\_i$)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04281124.png[/image\_path][/image-0]([CB008360 formular.docx](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:w:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CB/CB008000%20-%20CB008499/CFAM/CB008360%20UL%20MU%20MIMO%20-%204%20layers%20for%20FR1%20TDD/CB008360%20formular.docx?d=w88566cbc9b6a46afaa209a53df7ebfa0&csf=1&web=1&e=vOBRNP))

where：

* L:  the set of all MU-MIMO layers included in virtual UE(A)
* l:  a specific layer
* Ul:  the set of all UEs located on layer l
* NumOfRequiredPRBi: the number of PRBs requested by UE i (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5010\_replaced([11201008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwTkUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5016\_replaced([11201086](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwULYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the Greek letter alpha with a subscript i, written as $\alpha\_i$.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-04281127.png[/image\_path][/image-1]: PRB compensation factor of UE i (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9571\_replaced([11148009](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksI2APvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

1.2) If at least one re-transmission UE is present in virtual UE(A),

1.2.1) If virtual UE(A) is composed by re-transmission UEs entirely AND all of them were paired before in the initial transmission traffic with the same HARQ process ID **[Before PR710589][CB010659-B] AND all of them are allocated with the same number of PRBs as by the initial transmission** [End CB010659-B][End PR710589], the number of required PRB for these re-transmission UEs shall be the same as the ones in initial transmission traffic**[PR710589], if the adaptive retransmission is deactivated (NRBTS/NRCELL/actAdaptiveReTxResMcsEnh is set to FALSE). If the adaptive retransmission is activated (NRBTS/NRCELL/actAdaptiveReTxResMcsEnh is set to TRUE), the number of required PRBs shall be calculated by adaptive retransmission as give in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11970\_replaced([11202476](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwdVX_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**[End PR710589] The number of required PRB for this virtual UE(A) at current slot shall be decided by the max number of PRBs.***\****\*

1.2.2) otherwise, the number of required PRBs for this virtual UE(A) shall be decided by the max number of required PRBs among the re-transmission UEs **[CB010659-B] independent if the UEs are scheduled with an initial MCS or a reserved MCS** [End CB010659-B].\*\*\*\*

1.3)  If at least one MPR UE is included in the virtual UE(A), the number of reuiqred PRBs for this virtual UE(A) shall be decided by the max number of required PRBs among the MPR UEs.

---

##### 3.10.3.6.5-1.0-2 Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration schedulWeight of a virtual UE(A) (ID: 11147872)

**3.10.3.6.5-1.0-2.0-5**  (ID: `13422623`)

Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration
13422623:
Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration
1) If all UEs are initial non-GBR transmission UEs (including [CB014699-E]critical non-GBR and [End CB014699-E]NBR configured non-GBR initTx, see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4794\_replaced([11194709](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv24YfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the virtual UE(A), the schedulWeight of a virtual UE(A) is decided by the following equation:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
schedulWeight$*{vUE(A)}$ = $\sum*{UE(i) \in vUE(A)}$ schedulWeight$\_{i}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9326.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0],

2) If a root UE is paired with a candidate UE group (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9690\_replaced([11148139](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksI2BPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the schedulWeight of a virtual UE(A) shall be as following:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
schedulWeight$*{UE(A)}$ = schedulWeight$*{rootUE}$ + max$*{UE(j) \in candidateUEGroup(Z)}$ schedulWeight$*{j}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9326.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

3) If the virtual UE is constructed UEs from beam groups (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29211\_replaced([11149207](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksMgcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), there may be one or several UEs per layer, the schedulWeight of a virtual UE(A) is as following:

L2RT shall find the maximum scheduled weight per layer and sum the schedule weight over all of layers as the final schedule weight as this virtual UE.

If enhanced slice aware scheduler is activated (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_12233\_replaced([11278970](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpS0kvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "schedWeightᵢ" in a blurry, italicized font. The text is dark on a light background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9326.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] is derived from (NRBTS/NRDRB.schedulWeight \* RG weight) of [CB014699-E]critical/non-critical [End CB014699-E]non-GBR and deprioritized GBR DRBs from LCGs with nonempty transmission buffer of UE i; otherwise, it is derived from NRBTS/NRDRB.schedulWeight of [CB014699-E]critical/non-critical [End CB014699-E]non-GBR and deprioritized GBR DRBs from LCGs with nonempty transmission buffer of UE i.

##### 3.10.3.6.5-1.0-4 Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration virtual UEs formed with 'normal' pairing (ID: 13348509)

**3.10.3.6.5-1.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `13348510`)

Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration
13348510:
Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration
If NRCELL.actCarPoolLaneMuPairingES is set to 'disabled' or 'DL' gNB-DU shall skip the following actions.

gNB-DU shall perform the following for all the virtual UEs constructed with more than one constituent MU paired users paired using [11145856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCIUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) (See the concept by referring to [11355535](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucR1OvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) ,where each constituent user is with initial transmission and belongs to same traffic priority class:

1. Compute the TD metric of the vUE as described below:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in blue text. The equation is: TD\_metric\_{vUE} = \sum\_{i \in UEs \ in \ vUE} TD\_metric\_i.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-01041218.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

where [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the text "TD\_metrici" in a blue, italicized font. The text is slightly blurry.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-01041219.png[/image\_path][/image-1]is the sub-priority for each user 'i' and is given by [11195815](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv-0NPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "TD\_metricvue" in blue. The text is slightly blurry.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-01041254.png[/image\_path][/image-2] is the sub-priority of the virtual UE as a whole.

1. If NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.actFdBoostFactorMuPairsUl is set to a value other than zero, further update the TD Metric of the virtual UE as described below:

[image-3][image\_desc]TD\_metric\_{vUE} = (numUesinVUE)^γ \* TD\_metric\_{vUE}[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-01051410.png[/image\_path][/image-3]

where [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains the text "{numUesInVUE" in a blue font. The text is slightly blurry and appears to be on a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-01041231.png[/image\_path][/image-4] is the number of constituent users in the virtual UIE

[image-5][image\_desc]The image contains a blurry, blue letter "y".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-01041231.png[/image\_path][/image-5]is given by the NIDD parameter NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.actFdBoostFactorMuPairsUl.

13348601:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in blue text. The equation is: TD\_metric\_{vUE} = (numUesInVUE)^γ \* TD\_metric\_{vUE}.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/img-01051351.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

##### 3.10.3.6.5-1.0-6 Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration priority/sub-priority of virtual UE(A) (ID: 11147939)

**3.10.3.6.5-1.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `13348529`)

Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration
L2RT shall update it when a new candidate UE is added into virtual UE(A) successfully.

[CB015010-B]If NRCELL.actCarPoolLaneMuPairingES is set to 'disabled' or 'DL' [End CB015010-B]

The priority/sub-priority of a virtual UE is decided by the max priority/sub-priority among the UEs in the virtual UE.

[CB015010-B] Else, the sub-priority of the virtual UE shall be decided based on [13348508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ZXVS5eoBEfCnwLcpJWh_Zw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). In case the virtual UE consists of a UE from a higher priority class than drbTraffic class, then the priority of the virtual UE shall be decided by the max priority class among the UEs in the virtual UE. For e.g in a virtual UE if there is atleast one retransmission user, the priority of the virtual UE shall be be higher than another virtual UE consisting only initial transmission users. In such case actions defined in [13348508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ZXVS5eoBEfCnwLcpJWh_Zw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) are not performed.

[End CB015010-B]

##### 3.10.3.6.5-1.0-10 Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration Minimum number of PRBs for virutal UE(A) (ID: 11147997)

**3.10.3.6.5-1.0-10.0-3**  (ID: `13429324`)

Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration
**Step1: L2RT shall calculate the minimum number of PRBs in each MU-MIMO layer which is equal to the sum of minimum number of PRBs for the UEs in the same MU-MIMO layer.**

1) For non-GBR initial UEs without NBR category and UCI multiplexing with PUSCH, the min number of required PRB is minAllowedPuschPrbWithUci (5G\_UP\_ALG\_6391\_replaced([11197037](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwHXHPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));

2) For non-GBR UEs without NBR category and UCI is NOT multiplexing with PUSCH, the min number of required PRB is rrmMinSupportedPuschPrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31776\_replaced([11199457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwNdvvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

3) For the re-transmission UEs, If the adaptive re-transmission scheme is deactivated (/NRBTS/NRCELL/actAdaptiveReTxResMcs is set to FALSE) or the conditions defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11945\_replaced([11202437](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwdVWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are not fulfilled, **the same amount of resources as their initial transmission**and if the adaptive re-transmission scheme is activated (/NRBTS/NRCELL/actAdaptiveReTxResMcs is set to TRUE) and the conditions defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11945\_replaced([11202437](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwdVWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are fulfilled, the same amount of resources or a different amount of resources as their initial transmission is possible.\*\*\*\*

[CB014699-E]

Note: for critical non-GBR UEs in the same Mu-MIMO layer, the minimum required PRB is determined in same way as above 1) & 2) for normal nonGBR UE with/without UCI multiplexing.

[End CB014699-E]

**Step2: The minimum number of PRBs for this virtual UE(A) is equal to the maximum PRB number among all MU-MIMO layers.**

#### 3.10.3.6.5-2 Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration

##### 3.10.3.6.5-2.0-4 Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration 12567352: Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration [Before CNI-137616-B] If rdPrbCompensation(5G_UP_ALG_14889_replaced( 11149480 )) is configured to true, [CNI-137616-B] If NRULMUMIMO.ulMaxMuMimoLayer &lt;= 4 [End CNI-137616-B], L2RT shall make a compensation for UE(j) which is not power limited after UE(j) is paired with other UEs successfully .  [image-0][image_desc]The image contains the text "or ()". The text is in a stylized font with a gradient effect, appearing in shades of blue, orange, and white. The background is white, and the text is framed by a black border.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_9341.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] is initialized with 1 in each slot. Rationale: In order to keep the same data buffer size of UE(j) before and after pairing, additional compensation for the number of required PRBs is needed after pairing because MCS is decreased. Based on the following equation,[image-1][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in white text against a black background. The equation is: $N_{info} = N_{PRB} \times N' {RE} \times R \times Q_m \times V = N' {PRB} \times N_{RE} \times R' \times Q'_m \times V$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_9341.002.png[/image_path][/image-1], L2RT shall get compensation factor [image-2][image_desc]The image contains the text "α(j)".[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_9341.003.png[/image_path][/image-2] as following: [image-3][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is: $$ \alpha(j) = \frac{R_i(j) * Qm_i(j)}{R'_i(j) * Qm'_i(j)} $$ The formula defines alpha of j as a fraction. The numerator is the product of R sub i of j and Qm sub i of j. The denominator is the product of R prime sub i of j and Qm prime sub i of j.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_9341.004.png[/image_path][/image-3], [image-4][image_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression "Rᵢ(j), Qmᵢ(j)". The expression consists of two terms separated by a comma. The first term is "Rᵢ(j)", where "R" is a capital letter, "i" is a subscript, and "j" is in parentheses. The second term is "Qmᵢ(j)", where "Q" and "m" are capital letters, "i" is a subscript, and "j" is in parentheses.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_9341.005.png[/image_path][/image-4] and [image-5][image_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression "R'(,), Qm'(,)". The expression consists of the letter R with a prime symbol and a subscript, followed by parentheses. Then, there is a comma, the letter Q, the letter m with a prime symbol and a subscript, and finally, parentheses.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_9341.006.png[/image_path][/image-5] are coding rate and modulation order of UE(j) according to MCS before and after pairing with another UE. For example, when UE2 is going to paried with UE1, before pairing, the MCS selected for UE2 is 27, and after pairing, the MCS is decreased to 25. [image-6][image_desc]The image contains the mathematical expression "Rᵢ(j), Qmᵢ(j)". The expression consists of two terms separated by a comma. The first term is "Rᵢ(j)", where "R" is a capital letter, "i" is a subscript, and "j" is in parentheses. The second term is "Qmᵢ(j)", where "Q" and "m" are capital letters, "i" is a subscript, and "j" is in parentheses.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_9341.007.png[/image_path][/image-6] are the coding rate and modulation order for MCS 27, and [image-7][image_desc]R'ᵢ(j), Qm'ᵢ(j)[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_9341.008.png[/image_path][/image-7] are the coding rate and modulation order for MCS 25.  [Before CNI-137616-B]If rdPrbCompensation(5G_UP_ALG_14889_replaced( 11149480 )) is configured to false, [image-8][image_desc]The image contains a close-up of a mathematical expression. The expression is written in a light orange color with a slight blur. The expression consists of the Greek letter alpha, denoted by "α", followed by a parenthesis containing the letter "i". The "i" is also in a light orange color and appears slightly bolder than the "α". The overall impression is that of a mathematical variable or function notation.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m22dng_5G_UP_Algorithms_file_9341.009.png[/image_path][/image-8]is always equal to 1 no matter this UE is paired with other or not. The default value of rdPrbCompensation(5G_UP_ALG_14889_replaced( 11149480 )) is true. [End CNI-137616-B] Note: For MU eligible re-transmission UEs (see 5G_UP_ALG_11084_replaced( 11148246 )), - If MCS in re-transmission is not lower than initial transmission and the retransmission isn’t scheduled with a reserved MCS, the number of PRBs shall keep the same as the one in initial transmission. - The PRB compensation shall not be applied to retransmissions using a reserved MCS Note: In order to save CPU load and not impact the legacy MU-MIMO performance in CB008360, when NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMaxMuMimoLayer is larger than 4, the algorithm in this requirement shall be skipped [Before CNI-137616-B] no matter rdPrbCompensation(5G_UP_ALG_14889_replaced( 11149480 )) is set to true or false. [End CNI-137616-B] * * (ID: 12567352)

##### 3.10.3.6.5.0-1 Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration Criterion to update list and PRB information (ID: 11147551)

**3.10.3.6.5.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11147609`)

Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration
[CB009363-F] If PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and number of subcells per cell is two (5G\_UP\_2470\_replaced([11389618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufPCk_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then: [End CB009363-F]

* During the period of virtual UE(A) construction, L2RT should re-estimate the values of the parameters in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10770\_replaced([11147657](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHn4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and rrmSchedWeights (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10778\_replaced([11146450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksD9jPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), before the first virtual UE creation and after every virtual UE(A) creation if completed successfully.
* As per definition in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_10778\_replaced([11146450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksD9jPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the PRBs in rrmAvailablePrbForMu are for all non-GBR UEs in rrmUlMuCandidateList and rrmUlNonMuCandidateList (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9554\_replaced([11146147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCvavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The PRB share for these non-GBR UEs and/or already added to the virtual UEs in rrmvUEList (5G\_UP\_ALG\_8272\_replaced([11146198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksDWcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is estimated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21187\_replaced([11147689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHn5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in proportion to the scheduling weights of each UE and/or virtual UE. Thus, for proper estimation and in order to avoid allocating a PRB share to UE(s) in rrmUlNonMuCandidateList and/or a virtual UE more than what is needed, the procedure defined below updates the rrmUlNonMuCandidateList/rrmvUEList by comparing the amount of the PRB required by the UE and estimated share value. Thus,
* for UEs in rrmNonMuCandidateList, if the (re-)estimated PRB number (NjestPrb) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21187\_replaced([11147689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHn5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is equal or larger than the required PRB number (Njreq) (5G\_UP\_ALG\_5010\_replaced([11201008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwTkUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5016\_replaced([11201086](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwULYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2RT shall remove those UEs from rrmUlNonMuCandidateList.
* after each virtual UE(A) is created successfully, L2RT first estimates the PRB share for the virtual UE(A), vUEAestPrb, (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21187\_replaced([11147689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHn5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Then, after allocating the vUEAestPrb, L2RT shall distribute any remaining available PRBs to the remaining UEs or virtual UEs, re-estimate their PRB shares.  If the NestvUE(A) of any of the virtual UEs in rrmvUEList is equal or larger than the required PRB number, vUEAreq, L2RT shall remove those vUEs (which are already satisfied) from rrmvUEList.
* if UEs and/or vUEs are removed from rrmNonMuCandidateList and/or rrmvUEList , respectively, L2RT shall re-estimate rrmAvailablePrbForMu, rrmSchedWeights and rrmRequiredMuPrbNum, which are used for the next round as follows:
* rrmAvailablePrbForMu        = rrmAvailablePrbForMu - SUM[ UE(j)  rrmUlNonMuCandidateList with NjestPrb≥ Njreq]{ NjestPrb } - SUM[vUE(A)  rrmvUEList with vUEAestPrb≥ vUEAreq]{ vUEAestPrb }
* rrmRequiredMuPrbNum      = rrmRequiredMuPrbNum - SUM[ UE(j)  rrmUlNonMuCandidateList with NjestPrb≥ Njreq]{ Njreq } - SUM[ vUE(A)  rrmvUEList with vUEAestPrb≥ vUEAreq]{ vUEAreq }
* rrmSchedWeights             = rrmSchedWeights - SUM[ UE(j)  rrmUlNonMuCandidateList with NjestPrb≥ Njreq]{schedulWeightj } - SUM[ vUE(A)  rrmvUEList with vUEAestPrb≥ vUEAreq]{schedulWeightA }
* rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMu= rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMu - SUM[ UE(j)  rrmUlNonMuCandidateList with NjestPrb≥ Njreq]{ NjestPrb } - SUM[vUE(A)  rrmvUEList with vUEAestPrb≥ vUEAreq]{ alphaA\*vUEAestPrb }
* rrmRequiredMuPrbNum       = rrmRequiredMuPrbNum - SUM[ UE(j)  rrmUlNonMuCandidateList with NjestPrb≥ Njreq]{ Njreq } - SUM[ vUE(A)  rrmvUEList with vUEAestPrb≥ vUEAreq]{ alphaA\*vUEAreq }
* where:
* schedulWeightj is the schedule weight of UE(j) and
* schedulWeightA is scheduling weight of vUE(A) which is the total schedule weight of UEs included in the virtual UE(A).
* vUEAreq : the required PRB number is the maximum required PRB number among the UEs which are included in the virtual UE(A).
* alphaA: if vUE(A) is to be scheduled on one subcell, alphaA=1, else if two subcells is used, i alphaA=2.
* rrmNonMuCandidateList update (if above condidition satisfied) can be done after PRB share estimation is made before starting the first virtual UE creation and/or after every successful virtual creation completion.
* rrmvUEList update (if above condidition satisfied), after PRB share (re-)estimation is done after a successful virtual UE creation
* Rationale: For the virtual UE(A), it is easier to get more PRBs which may exceed the required PRB number because the schedule weight for virtual UE(A) is the total schedule weight of UEs which are included in virtual UE(A) but the required PRB number is the maximum required PRB number among the UEs which are included in virtual UE(A).

Refer to example in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9547\_replaced([11147615](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHA4PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: As indicated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8267\_replaced([11145665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksBhQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), this PRB estimation step is required to estimate the PRB share for the non-GBR UEs  in proportion to the scheduling weight of the UEs ( same as simplified WRR) as WRR can not be used as as SD scheduling comes before FD scheduling. This estimated PRB is to be used to calculate the available PRBs for MU.

---

##### 3.10.3.6.5.0-2 Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration Some examples of updating PRB information #1 (ID: 11147615)

**3.10.3.6.5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11147630`)

Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration
11147630:
Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration
[Before CB007113-I-UPD002]

For example, if rrmAvailablePrbForMu is initialized with 70, UE1, UE2, UE3 and UE4 are included in rrmUlMuCandidateList and UE5 is included in rrmUlNonMuCandidateList. In this case, the required number of PRB (reqPRB) of UE5 and UE4 is 10 for each, the estimated number for PRB allocation EstimatePrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21187\_replaced([11147689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHn5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of UE5 and UE4 is also 10 in the 1st round ( while UE-5 is still in the list). In the 2nd round, rrmAvailablePrbForMu should be updated by excluding the estimated number for PRB allocation EstimatePrb of UE5 which is non-MU candidate because the estimated number for PRB allocation has reached the required number of PRB of this UE.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a table with financial data related to User Equipment (UE) scheduling. The table has columns for different UEs (UE1, UE2, UE3, UE4, UE5) and rows detailing various metrics like "schedule weight per UE", "reqPRB", "PrbNum by schWeight", and "EstimatePrb". There are also summary calculations on the right side of the table.
The table is divided into two main sections, separated by a green row. The top section calculates initial values, while the bottom section shows updated values after UE5 is removed.
Here is the table represented in markdown:
| Row Header | UE1(MU candidate) | UE2(MU candidate) | UE3(MU candidate) | UE4(MU candidate) | UE5(non-MU candidate) | Summary Calculation[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9308.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

[CB007113-I-UPD002]

For example, if rrmAvailablePrbForMu is initialized with 70 and rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMu =130, UE1, UE2, UE3 and UE4 are included in rrmUlMuCandidateList and UE5 is included in rrmUlNonMuCandidateList. In this case, the required number of PRB (reqPRB) of UE5 and UE4 is 10 for each, the estimated number for PRB allocation EstimatePrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21187\_replaced([11147689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHn5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of UE5 and UE4 is also 10. At this state L2PS checked the estimated PRB for the UEs if there is any UEs whose required PRB can be satisfied with the estimated PRB share. UE-5 gets 10 PRBs as estiamted PRB share which is enough to satisfy its required PRB share (10 PRB), thus, UE-5 is removed from rrmUlNonMuCandidateList and will no longer be involved in any future steps (indicated by x). Then, the list of UEs in rrmUlNonMuCandidateList and the values of parameters rrmAvailablePrbForMu /rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMu shall be updated by deducting the estimated PRB share of the removed UE (UE-5). The updated list and parameter values are used during the next round of vUE creation process (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9573\_replaced([11147551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHA3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). After the first vUE is created,vUE(Ue1,Ue2), required PRB and estimated PRB shares are computed based on the available PRBs (physical/subcell), and a check is done if the estimated share is enough to satisfy the required PRB for the UEs/vUEs. Accordingly, the stimated shares of vUE (Ue1,Ue2) is equal to the required PRB of the vUE. In this case, this vUE shall not be kept in rrmvUEList (vUE is removed (x)) and corresponding rrmvUEList and  rrmAvailablePrbForMu /rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMu are updated as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9573\_replaced([11147551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHA3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).  And, next virtual UE creation step is proceed with this new updated list and parameter values as presented in the table below.

11147651:
Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration
Here is one example, if rrmAvailablePrbForMu is initialized with 70 and UE1, UE2, UE3, UE4 and UE5 are included in rrmUlMuCandidateList, the estimated PRB number before and after paring is as following. L2RT shall estimate PRB number as EstimatePrb(2) which is shown in the following table.

Note: 1) Estimated PRB number as EstimatePrb(1) is not accepted because that there will be more PRB wasted. It will impact the spectrum efficiency result.              2) To make a simplification, [image-0][image\_desc]The image is a blurry, close-up shot of what appears to be a screen displaying a colorful, abstract pattern. ##### 3.10.3.6.5.0-4 Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration Procedure For Determining and Updating The Number of Available Subcell PRBs (ID: 11147657)

**3.10.3.6.5.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11147669`)

Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration
This section determines the amount of subcell PRBs available for MU.  First, the maximum value is determined at the beginning of the slot before any virtual UE construction and then, this value is updated after completion of any vitual UE construction by subtructing the number of subcell PRB allocated to the virtual UE.

[CB009363-F] If PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and number of subcells per cell is two (5G\_UP\_2470\_replaced([11389618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufPCk_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the following steps shall be executed.[End CB009363-F]

Step1: When slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed = TRUE (5G\_CP\_ARC\_ALG\_4283\_replaced([11278751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_TpSNc_vcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and NRBTS.actUlMuMimo = TRUE and numAllocCellPrb is larger than maxNumPrbLimitToUsePerUlBw (5G\_UP\_ALG\_14781\_replaced([11146479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksEkkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), at the beginning of the slot before any virtual UE construction, L2RT should also calculate:

* maxNumSubcelPrbAvailableForPusch, rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMu for non-GBR UEs which are included in rrmUlMuCandidateList  and rrmUlNonMuCandidateList  (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9554\_replaced([11146147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCvavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
* maxNumSubcelPrbAvailableForPusch =  numAllocCellPrb - numPrbToBeUsedForPucch - exclude number of PRBs, if any, used for PRACH and/or common PUCCH (as described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4876\_replaced([11196884](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwGI9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

-rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMu = min {maxNumSubcelPrbAvailableForPusch – rrmPrbNumNotAvailableForMu - (beta-1)*rrmPRBNumForReTxMu, 2*rrmAvailablePrbForMu)}

* where:
* rrmPRBNumForReTxMu:  PRBs allocated to virtual UE(A) in which only re-transmission UEs are paired (5G\_UP\_ALG\_11537\_replaced([11196874](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwGI9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), if no such virtual UE(A) exist, its value is zero
* beta is equal to two if the above retransmission virtual UE(A) are scheduled on two sub-cells, otherwise, beta should be equal to one.
* numAllocCellPrb is total number of usable subcell PRBs granted by the BBRM see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6500\_replaced([11212285](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxAH9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))
* rrmNumPuschPrbDedicatedBwp (defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_4974\_replaced([11199486](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwOEw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* Before the first virtual UE creation, L2PS shall initialize the available physical Cell PRBs and subcell PRBs as below, these value shall be updated after every virtual UE construction in Step2
* rrmAvailablePrbForMuLeft = rrmAvailablePrbForMu;
* rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMuLeft =  rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMu,
* The value of rrmAvailablePrbForMu and rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMu may be updated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9573\_replaced([11147551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHA3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Step2: After virtual UE is constructed completely, the remaining physical cell PRBs and subcell PRBs shall be updated as below:

* rrmAvailablePrbForMuLeft            = rrmAvailablePrbForMu – SUM[all virtual UEs in rrmvUEList]{estNumSubcelPrbAllocationForUe/alpha}
* rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMuLeft   = min{rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMu – SUM[all virtual UEs in rrmvUEList]{estNumSubcelPrbAllocationForUe}, 2\*rrmAvailablePrbForMuLeft}
* where:-
* estNumSubcelPrbAllocationForUe is the estimated number of subcell PRB allocation to a virtual UE as determined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21187\_replaced([11147689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHn5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). And,
* alpha =2, if the virtual UE is scheduled on two subcells, else alpha=1,if shceduled one one subcell.
* rrmvUEList contains list of virtual UEs whose required PRBs are not yet satisfied (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9573\_replaced([11147551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHA3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Step3: Before each virtual UE cretation, L2PS shall check :

IF rrmRequiredMuPrbNum < rrmAvailablePrbForMu \* rdUlPrbScaleRatio(5G\_UP\_ALG\_14881\_replaced([11149436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) && rrmRequiredMuSubcellPrbNum < rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMu \* rdUlPrbScaleRatio(5G\_UP\_ALG\_14881\_replaced([11149436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

* Skip UL spatial domain scheduling, start UL frequency domain scheduling

ELSE IF rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMuLeft   <= rrmAvailablePrbForMuLeft

* only one subcell (primary) is used to allocate UEs
* start UL spatial domain scheduling for only UEs with rank1 transmission which can do MU pairing, rest UE will do SU transmission on the primary subcell

ELSE

* do UL spatial domain scheduling and UEs upto rank2 transmission can do MU pairing
* two subcells can be used
* In case of a virtual UE with reTx as root UE, MU-pairing decision to use one or two subcell depends on the required and available subcell PRBs, thus solution may need to be further optimized and hence details are left for CP3.

END

* once allocation to UEs in rrmUlMuCandidateList and/or virtual UEs in rrmvUEList is(are) satisfied, any remaining usable PRB/subcellPRBs can be given/allocated to UEs in rrmUlNonMuCandidateList and virtual UEs in rrmvUEList (5G\_UP\_ALG\_8272\_replaced([11146198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksDWcvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

where:-

* rrmRequiredMuPrbNum (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10778\_replaced([11146450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksD9jPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));
* rrmPrbNumNotAvailableForMu (5G\_UP\_ALG\_11537\_replaced([11196874](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwGI9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)));
* rrmAvailablePrbForMu value updated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9573\_replaced([11147551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHA3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* rdUlPrbScaleRatio(5G\_UP\_ALG\_14881\_replaced([11149436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
* rrmRequiredMuSubcellPrbNum:  the sum of the required subcell PRBs of the virtual UEs and the remaining UEs in rrmUlMuCandidateList  and rrmUlNonMuCandidateList, where:
* required subcell PRBs of avirtual UE = alpha\*required PRB of virtual UE updated in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9548\_replaced([11147793](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHn8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and alpha=2 if virtual UE is scheduled on two subcells, else alpha=1, if one subcell is used.
* required PRB for SU UEs, refer to refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5010\_replaced([11201008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwTkUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_UP\_ALG\_5016\_replaced([11201086](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwULYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ( same way as used in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9573\_replaced([11147551](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHA3fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

---

##### 3.10.3.6.5.0-5 Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration Some examples of virtual UE construction when slowPrbPoolingTddFr1UlAllowed is true (ID: 11147678)

**3.10.3.6.5.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11147684`)

Update list and PRB information in two subcells configuration
For example, if numAllocCellPrb= 150, the number of PRBs in the UL bandwidth = 100, numPrbToBeUsedForPucch = 20, UE1, UE2, UE3, UE4, UE5 and UE6 are included in rrmUlMuCandidateList. In this case, the required number of PRB (reqPRB) of UE1, UE2, UE3, UE4, UE5 and UE6 is 50, 48, 30, 28, 20 and 20 separately, UE1 and UE2 construct virtual UE(A), UE3 and UE4 construct virtual UE(B). The estimated number for PRB allocation EstimatePrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21187\_replaced([11147689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHn5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of virtual UE(A) and virtual UE(B) is 30 and 20 separately. Before any virtual UEs construction, L2PS should caculate:

rrmAvailablePrbForMu= 100-20=80

rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMu= 150-20=130

rrmRequiredMuPrbNum = 50+48+30+28+20+20=196

Step 1: cell physical PRB checking (5G\_UP\_ALG\_10778\_replaced([11146450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksD9jPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

rrmRequiredMuPrbNum > rrmAvailablePrbForMu \* rdUlPrbScaleRatio(5G\_UP\_ALG\_14881\_replaced([11149436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

196> 88 ---> virtual UE can be constructed.

Step 2: UE1 and UE2 constructed virtual UE(A), the estimated number for PRB allocation EstimatePrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21187\_replaced([11147689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHn5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of virtual UE(A) is 30, after virtual UE(A) is constructed, update

rrmAvailablePrbForMuLeft = 80-30=50

rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMuLeft= 130-30\*2=70

Step 3: BBRM PRB checking: rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMuLeft is less than updated cell physical PRBs number, if yes, only one subsell, if not two subcell

70>50 - two subcell

Step 4: before construct next virtual UE, do cell physical PRB checking:

rmRequiredMuPrbNum > rrmAvailablePrbForMu \* rdUlPrbScaleRatio(5G\_UP\_ALG\_14881\_replaced([11149436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNuhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

rrmRequiredMuPrbNum = sum {reqPBR for (virtual UE(A), UE3, UE4, UE5, UE6)} = 50+30+28+20+20=148

148>88, continue construct virtual UE.

Step 5: UE3 and UE4 constructed virtual UE(B), the estimated number for PRB allocation EstimatePrb (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21187\_replaced([11147689](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksHn5_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of virtual UE(B) is 20, after virtual UE(B) is constructed, updates

rrmAvailablePrbForMuLeft = 80-30-20=30

rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMuLeft= 130-30*2-20*2=30

Step 6: BBRM PRB checking: whether rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMuLeft is less than or equal to cell physical PRBs number, 30<=30 - only primary subcell is used in follow steps.

Step 7: Case 1: UE5 with 2 layers, UE6 with 2 layers

Case 2: UE5 with 2 layers, UE6 with 1 layer

Case 3: UE5 with 1 layer, UE6 with 2 layers

Case 4: UE5 with 1 layer, UE6 with 1 layer

For case1, 2, 3, UE5 and UE6 will do SU transmission at primary subcell.

For case4, L2PS shall check whether rrmRequiredMuPrbNumForLeftUEs < rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMuLeft is met or not. In case4, rrmRequiredMuPrbNumFor UE5 and UE6 = 20+20 > 30 (rrmAvailableSubcelPrbForMuLeft ), UE5 and UE6 can construct virtual UE(C).

---

#### 3.10.3.6.6 Candidate UE group

#### 3.10.3.6.6-1 Candidate UE group

**3.10.3.6.6-1.0-2**  (ID: `13422635`)

Candidate UE group
For the [CB014699-E] critical non-GBR MU and [End CB014699-E] non-GBR MU eligible re-transmission UEs in rrmUlMuCandidateList, only the re-transmission UEs which satisfy the following condition can be paired with other UEs:

1) PUSCH is not DTX;

2) MCS switching point is not reached in the initial transmission for the power limited UEs;

3) Not ATB in initial transmission traffic.

4) the number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data in initial transmission is 2 (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_3098\_replaced([11137832](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krbravvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

5) This UE is not MPR UE with re-transmission traffic

**NOTE:**

1) If (PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and number of subcells per cell is two (5G\_UP\_2470\_replaced([11389618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufPCk_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) AND (primary and secondary subcells are located in the different L1 pool (5G\_UP\_4000\_replaced([11382080](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uev6afvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))), the subcell index for this UE in re-transmission traffic shall keep the same as the one in initial transmission traffic; otherwise if the primary and secondary subcells are located in the same L1 pool(5G\_UP\_400\_replaced([11349418](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ubej_fvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the subcell index for this UE in re-transmission traffic can be different from the one in initial transmission traffic.

2) MPR UEs shall not be paired with re-transmission UEs no matter this MRP UE is with non-GBR initial transmission traffic or non-GBR re-transmission traffic.
