#### 3.10.3.6.6-2 Candidate UE group

**3.10.3.6.6-2.0-2**  (ID: `13464022`)

Candidate UE group
13464022:
Candidate UE group
[CB015122-J]

if NRCELL.actInternalImprovements1.Bit1 equals 1

The calculation of powerRatio has been moved to L1-DU, see [13455365](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_p6SPVizSEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). L2-PS receives the decision about applicability of LOS and NLOS channel from L1-DU.

else

[End CB015122-J]

Assume that for UE i:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$Rsrp\_h = \frac{W\_{1stbest,h}^H \* R\_{srs,h} \* W\_{1stbest,h}}{W\_{1stbest,h}^H \* W\_{1stbest,h}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9359.002.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

in horizontal,

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$Rsrp\_v = \frac{W\_{1stbest,v}^H \* R\_{srs,v} \* W\_{1stbest,v}}{W\_{1stbest,v}^H \* W\_{1stbest,v}}$
Where:
- $Rsrp\_v$ is on the left side of the equation.
- The right side is a fraction.
- The numerator is $W\_{1stbest,v}^H \* R\_{srs,v} \* W\_{1stbest,v}$.
- The denominator is $W\_{1stbest,v}^H \* W\_{1stbest,v}$.
- The superscript 'H' denotes the conjugate transpose.
- The asterisk '\*' denotes matrix multiplication.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9359.004.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

in vertial,

[image-2][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is:
powerRatio = sqrt( (Rsrp\_h \* Rsrp\_v) / (trace(R\_srs,h) \* trace(R\_srs,v)) )[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9359.006.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

where,

-  [image-3][image\_desc]The image contains the text "RSRS,h" in a stylized font. The letters are a light blue color with a white outline, and they appear to be slightly blurred. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9359.007.png[/image\_path][/image-3] is a covariance matrix Cov(H) **without normalization. See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2166\_replaced([11154579](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2tPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

-  [image-4][image\_desc]The image contains the text "RSRS,v". The text is in a light blue color against a white background. The letters are slightly blurred.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9359.008.png[/image\_path][/image-4] is a covariance matrix Cov(V) **without normalization. See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_2166\_replaced([11154579](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kss2tPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

- [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains the text "W₁stbest,h" in a blurry, low-resolution format. The text is white with a slight yellow tint and is set against a white background. The letters are somewhat distorted and difficult to read clearly.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9359.009.png[/image\_path][/image-5]is the vertical vector of the 1st best horizontal beam.

- [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains the text "W₁stbest,v". The text is blurry and appears to be in a mathematical or scientific context.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9359.010.png[/image\_path][/image-6]is the vertical vector of the 1st best vertical beam.

If powerRatio > **rdUlPowerRatio(5G\_UP\_ALG\_19959\_replaced([11149658](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksO8rfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

, then L2PS shall assume that UE i located in LOS channel; otherwise, L2PS shall assume that UE i located in NLOS channel.

#### 3.10.3.6.6-3 Candidate UE group

**3.10.3.6.6-3.0-2**  (ID: `11148323`)

Candidate UE group
If the adaptive re-transmission scheme is deactivated (/NRBTS/NRCELL/actAdaptiveReTxResMcs is set to FALSE) or the conditions defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11945\_replaced([11202437](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwdVWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are not fulfilled, the HARQ retransmission for UE(i) is applied as follows.

- Reserved MCS shall be used in re-transmission traffic if the number of FL DMRS symbols is different but the same TBS, PRB number and Rank is used as in the initial transmission traffic and re-transmission traffic.

**[CB008235-D] If the adaptive re-transmission scheme is activated (/NRBTS/NRCELL/actAdaptiveReTxResMcs is set to TRUE) and the conditions defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11945\_replaced([11202437](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwdVWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are fulfilled, the allocation of the adaptive retransmission is applied as defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11970\_replaced([11202476](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwdVX_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and reserved MCS could be used as defined by 5G\_UP\_ALG\_12913\_replaced([11202887](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwd8aPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).** [End CB008235-D]\*\*\*\*

Note: if DTX is detected for an initial UL transmission, it is the same behavior as defined in [11202437](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwdVWfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ). The number of DMRS symbols in the re-transmisison traffic is the same as the initial UL transmission

#### 3.10.3.6.6-4 Candidate UE group

11148350:
Candidate UE group
[Before PR785992]

[CB009363-F] Considering the poor intra-cell interference rejection with 4RX receiver and avoid frequent re-transmissions, if NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is 4RX [End CB009363-F], for re-transmission MU-MIMO UE with the same harq process, the MU-SINR in re-transmission slot shall be equal or larger than the SINR in initial transmission if NIDD:ulMuMimoLinkAdaptionSwitch is "MU-SINR estimation" or the paired UE size(5G\_UP\_ALG\_20424\_replaced([11149069](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksL5XvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in re-transmission slot shall be equal or smaller than the one in initial transmission if NIDD:ulMuMimoLinkAdaptionSwitch is "MCS compensation".

[PR785992]

If NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is 4RX, for re-transmission MU-MIMO UE(i) with the same harq process:

If rdMuSinrReTx (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29851\_replaced([11149895](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to TRUE, L2RT shall check whether the following condition is satisfied before adding it into virtual UE:

- If NIDD:ulMuMimoLinkAdaptionSwitch is "MU-SINR estimation", [image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9365.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] shall be larger than rdUlDeltaMuSinr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29853\_replaced([11149910](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx1_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: [image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible objects, text, or features.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9365.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] may be different from the final one because it is calculated in the pairing procedure and tapered/non-tapered beams are decided in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9866\_replaced([11148389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) but final beams used in re-transmission scheduling are decided in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15693\_replaced([11148418](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEKfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- If NIDD:ulMuMimoLinkAdaptionSwitch is "MCS compensation", the paired UE size(5G\_UP\_ALG\_20424\_replaced([11149069](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksL5XvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in re-transmission slot shall be equal or smaller than the one in initial transmission.

Else

L2RT shall skip the above check.

End

[End PR785992]

---

#### 3.10.3.6.6-5 Candidate UE group

**3.10.3.6.6-5.0-1**  (ID: `11148362`)

Candidate UE group
Step1: L2RT shall find the layers with the first and second maximum number of PRBs and calculate the PRB diff between the first two layers.

Step2: L2RT shall sort the UEs in the first layer according to the number of PRBs with the descending order.

Step3: L2RT shall check the NprbDiff in step1 and the UE with the smallest PRB allocation in step2 as following:

for (i = maxNumofUEsInStep2; i>0;i--)

{

If (NprbDiff >= UE(i)'s PRB number)

{

Mark UE(i)’s status as SU-MIMO status.

Update NprbDiff = NprbDiff – UE(i)'s PRB number

}

}

---

##### 3.10.3.6.6.0-1 Candidate UE group Build candidate UE group (ID: 11148145)

**3.10.3.6.6.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11148171`)

Candidate UE group
If the following conditions is met

* (NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is equal to 4 and the number of subcells per cell = 2 (5G\_UP\_2470\_replaced([11389618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufPCk_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))), or (NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is equal to 8 [CB010708-E] or larger than 8 [End CB010708-E] ) ,and
* [CB010708-E] NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMaxMuMimoLayer is NOT larger than 4 [End CB010708-E] , and
* NRBTS/NRCELL/NRULMUMIMO.actUlMuMimoGroupParing = TRUE

then L2RT shall perform the following steps.

Step 1: L2RT shall attempt to construct one candidate UE group, ensuring that the total number of required PRBs of the UEs in this group is similar to that of the root UE, as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9522\_replaced([11146531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksEkmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The UEs included in the UE group shall satisfy the conditions defined  in [11148176](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksI2CvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

Step 2: If the candidate UE group could be found, then L2RT shall schedule root UE and UE group under different receiver configurations:

* When the number of subcells per cell = 2 (5G\_UP\_2470\_replaced([11389618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufPCk_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming = 4, two 4RX receivers are available.The root UE shall be scheduled on the first 4RX receiver, and the UEs in UE group shall be scheduled on the second 4RX receiver.
* When NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming = 8 [CB010708-E] or larger than 8 [End CB010708-E], one MU-IRC receiver is available. The root UE and UEs in UE group shall be scheduled in the same MU-IRC receiver.

Note:

* There is only one root UE, while the UE group may contain multiple UEs, which are FDMed within the group.

---

##### 3.10.3.6.6.0-2 Candidate UE group The conditions of UEs in the candidate UE group (ID: 11148176)

**3.10.3.6.6.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `13247206`)

Candidate UE group
In the scenario where a root UE is paired with a UE group, the root UE shall be a new transmission UE and not an MPR UE.

If UE(i) is the root UE, L2RT shall add UE(j) to the UE group if UE(j) satisfies all of the following conditions:

* UE(j) is selected from rrmUlMuCandidateList [(11146147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCvavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) and has not been paired with any other UE before.
* UE(j) is a new transmission UE.
* UE(j) is not an MPR UE.
* The correlation between root UE(i) and UE(j) satisfies the correlation check defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9524\_replaced([11146572](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksEkn_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* The sum of requested PRBs of UE(j) and the UEs already included in the UE group meets the requirement defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9522\_replaced([11146531](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksEkmfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* The DMRS configuration, including the number of front-loaded DMRS symbols and additional DMRS symbols, shall be the same as that of the root UE, as specified in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9544\_replaced([11146519](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksEklvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
* [CB008148-C] The waveform of UE(j) could be the same or different from root UE. [End CB008148-C]

**NOTE:**

If rdActPrbAllocOptForFr1CCA (see [12698005](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_qkqXM1yLEfCPFofqMEsORA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is equal to true

1) If root UE(i) is FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA UE with current cell as lower sub-band serving cell, FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA UE with current cell as upper sub-band serving cell can’t be added to the candidate group, vice versa.

2) FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA UE with current cell as upper sub-band serving cell and FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA UE with current cell as lower sub-band serving cell can’t be added to the same candidate group.

else

1) If root UE(i) is FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA UE with current cell as lower sub-band serving cell, which transmission buffer in UL is split between PCell and SCell (see [11122349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqfQNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA UE with current cell as upper sub-band serving cell, which transmission buffer in UL is split between PCell and SCell (see [11122349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqfQNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), can’t be added to the candidate group, vice versa.

2) FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA UE with current cell as upper sub-band serving cell, which transmission buffer in UL is split between PCell and SCell (see [11122349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqfQNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)),  and FR1 intra-band contiguous UL CA UE with current cell as lower sub-band serving cell, which transmission buffer in UL is split between PCell and SCell (see [11122349](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqfQNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), can’t be added to the same candidate group.

endif

---

### 3.10.3.7 MU-SINR estimation

### 3.10.3.7-1 MU-SINR estimation

#### 3.10.3.7-1.0-1 MU-SINR estimation Instantaneous SU-SINR estimation in case of 4RX receiver (ID: 11148754)

**3.10.3.7-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148757`)

MU-SINR estimation
L2PS shall convert MU-SINR to SU-SINR according to the algorithm in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21939\_replaced([11148794](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksLSQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.10.3.7-1.0-2 MU-SINR estimation Instantaneous SU-SINR estimation in case of higher order receiver (&gt;4RX) (ID: 11148764)

**3.10.3.7-1.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11148789`)

MU-SINR estimation
If PUSCH is received over 8 or larger than 8 spatial streams for a given subcell(5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), for the MU-MIMO UE:

1) If RD parameter X is true, where X = rdSuSinrFlag (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21893\_replaced([11149710](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksPjt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is equal to 8; X = rdSuSinrFlag16RX (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27713\_replaced([11149730](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksPjuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is equal to 16.

- L2RT shall inform L1-ULPHY to report post SU-SINR (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21967\_replaced([11108937](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koxY_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

- If the value of post SU-SINR(5G\_UP\_ALG\_21967\_replaced([11108937](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koxY_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) reported from L1 is a valid value, [Before CB010708-K-UPD001] post SU-SINR(5G\_UP\_ALG\_21967\_replaced([11108937](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koxY_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB010708-K-UPD001] max (post SU-SINR (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21967\_replaced([11108937](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koxY_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), MU-SINR) [End CB010708-K-UPD001] shall be the input to calculate rrmInstSinr; otherwise, L2RT shall use post MU-SINR(5G\_UP\_ALG\_1701\_replaced([11108899](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kowx7_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as the input to calculate rrmInstSinr. The algorithm to calculate rrmInstSinr refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11115\_replaced([11130748](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krANnPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

2) Else, L2RT shall not inform L1-ULPHY to report post SU-SINR (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21967\_replaced([11108937](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koxY_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). L2RT shall convert MU-SINR to SU-SINR according to the algorithm in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22078\_replaced([11148917](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksLSSfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

NOTE: Post MU-SINR (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1701\_replaced([11108899](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kowx7_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be reported from L1-ULPHY always no matter rdSuSinrFlag (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21893\_replaced([11149710](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksPjt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is true or false.

NOTE: Post MU-SINR (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1701\_replaced([11108899](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kowx7_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be reported from L1-ULPHY always no matter rdSuSinrFlag is true or false.

EndIf

EndIf

#### 3.10.3.7-1.0-3 MU-SINR estimation Convert MU-SINR to SU-SINR (ID: 11148794)

**3.10.3.7-1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11148800`)

MU-SINR estimation
Overview

---

**3.10.3.7-1.0-3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148804`)

MU-SINR estimation
For UE i, if at the previous UL scheduling slot t0, UE i is paired with other UE. And at data slot t1, L1 will report corresponding SINR according to PUSCH measurement and L2RT should convert MU-SINR to SU-SINR and feed SU-SINR to the filter exponent if NIDD:NRCELL/ulMuMimoParaSet/ulMuMimoLinkAdaptionSwitch =0 (MU-SINR estimation).

Rationale: In the corresponding UL scheduled slot, UE i is paried with other UEs.

---

**3.10.3.7-1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11148809`)

MU-SINR estimation
Convert MU-SINR to SU-SINR if UEs are scheduled in different receivers

---

**3.10.3.7-1.0-3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11148911`)

MU-SINR estimation
11148911:
MU-SINR estimation
If PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and number of subcells per cell is two (5G\_UP\_2470\_replaced([11389618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufPCk_vkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) AND both of subcells are scheduled for the virtual UE(k) at slot t0, L2PS shall estimate UE(i)'s SU-SINR rmInstSinr on PUSCH which is included in virtual UE(k) in the corresponding data slot t1 for the same harqID and send this estimated SU-SINR rmInstSinr to the filter exponent.

step1: calculate UE(i)'s noise per prb

[Before CNI-126050-A]

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9406.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0],

[CNI-126050-A]

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9406.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1],

[End CNI-126050-A]

where K1prb(i) is the noise per prb i averaged over all the receiving antennas (spatial streams); Nprb is the number of PRBs carrying the PUSCH; numofStreams is equal to NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming. The unit of noisePerPrb is linear.

step2: calculate rxPower:

[image-2][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9406.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]

[image-3][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9406.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3], where the unit of[image-4][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9406.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4]is linear.

step3: calculate post SU-SINR:

[image-5][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9406.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5], the unit is linear,

[image-6][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9406.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6],

the unit is dB.

If the number of layer for this UE is 1: //three rank1 , rank1 + rank2 or four rank1 UEs paired

[image-7][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9406.008.png[/image\_path][/image-7], the unit is dB.

else if the number of layer for this UE is 2:

[image-8][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9406.009.png[/image\_path][/image-8], the unit is dB

End

rrmInstSinr[i,j,t] = MIN(rdTargetMaxSinr,rrmInstSinr[i,j,t]);

i: index of UE

j: index of the carrier

t1: UL slot for that the SINR is predicted

[image-9][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9406.010.png[/image\_path][/image-9]: SINR (in dB) of the first layer combined over all the received antennas and averaged over the scheduled subcarriers (5G\_L1\_8334\_replaced([11404269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9S9tPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[image-10][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9406.011.png[/image\_path][/image-10]: SINR (in dB) of the second layer combined over all the received antennas and averaged over the scheduled subcarriers (5G\_L1\_8334\_replaced([11404269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9S9tPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

rdTargetMaxSinr: refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19889\_replaced([11149631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksO8qPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rrmTaperingCompensation: refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13871\_replaced([11148444](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKELfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

**3.10.3.7-1.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11148917`)

MU-SINR estimation
Convert MU-SINR to SU-SINR if UEs are scheduled in the same receiver

---

**3.10.3.7-1.0-3.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11148924`)

MU-SINR estimation
If all paired UEs are scheduled in the same receiver in the scheduling slot, L2PS shall convert MU-SINR to SU-SINR in the corresponding data slot and feed it to the filter exponent as following:

rmInstSinr[i,j,t1] = MIN(rdTargetMaxSinr, rrmInstSinr[i,j,t1] - rrmDeltaSINRMuMimo[i,j,t0]), where rrmDeltaSINRMuMimo see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8348\_replaced([11148500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEMfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The default value of rdTargetMaxSinr is 35dB.

rrmInstSinr[i,j,t1] = MIN(rdTargetMaxSinr, Linear2dB (dB2Linear (rrmInstSinr[i,j,t1] - rrmDeltaSINRMuMimo[i,j,t0]) / rrmTaperingCompensation ) ), where rrmDeltaSINRMuMimo see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8348\_replaced([11148500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEMfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), where rrmTaperingCompensation refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13871\_replaced([11148444](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKELfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

End

rdTargetMaxSinr: refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19889\_replaced([11149631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksO8qPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

### 3.10.3.7-2 MU-SINR estimation

#### 3.10.3.7-2.0-1 MU-SINR estimation MCS compensation offset (4RX) (ID: 11148936)

**3.10.3.7-2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148959`)

MU-SINR estimation
11148959:
MU-SINR estimation
The following algorithm shall be implemented when NIDD: ulMuMimoParaSet/ulMuMimoLinkAdaptionSwitch = 1 (MCS compensation) and NIDD:NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is set to 4RX.

In the current slot t0, L2RT shall adjust UE(i)’s current MCS according to [image-0][image\_desc]deltaMcsUE(i)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9411.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] and check the consistency of the MCS selection to make sure the UE's MCS in a valid range:

(1)  [image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9411.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]if the paired UE size (5G\_UP\_ALG\_20424\_replaced([11149069](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksL5XvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the current slot t0 is larger than the paired UE size (5G\_UP\_ALG\_20424\_replaced([11149069](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksL5XvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the nearest previous slot t0-delta.

(2)  [image-2][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9411.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] if the paired UE size (5G\_UP\_ALG\_20424\_replaced([11149069](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksL5XvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the current slot t0 is smaller than the paired UE size (5G\_UP\_ALG\_20424\_replaced([11149069](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksL5XvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in the nearest previous slot t0-delta.

where, [image-3][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible objects, text, or features.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9411.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] = ulMuMimoMcsOffset[deltaPairSize], *UlMuMimoMCSOffset is a O&M parameter, the default value is given by below table.*

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| deltaPairSize | ulMuMimoMcsOffset |
| 0 | NIDD:mcsOffsetLayerDiffZero |
| 1 | NIDD:mcsOffsetLayerDiffOne |
| 2 | NIDD:mcsOffsetLayerDiffTwo |
| 3 | NIDD:mcsOffsetLayerDiffThree |

---

#### 3.10.3.7-2.0-2 MU-SINR estimation MCS compensation offset (&gt;4RX) (ID: 11148966)

**3.10.3.7-2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11148985`)

MU-SINR estimation
11148985:
MU-SINR estimation
The following algorithm shall be implemented when NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMuMimoLinkAdaptionSwitch = 1 (MCS compensation) and NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMaxMuMimoLayer is larger than 4.
 
If UE(i) is scheduled with MU-MIMO status, L2RT shall feed **rrmUlMuMiMoDeltaSinrOffset to ILLA in order to get final MCS in FD scheduler; otherwise,** rrmUlMuMiMoDeltaSinrOffset is equal to zero.***\*

### 3.10.3.7-3 MU-SINR estimation

#### 3.10.3.7-3.0-1 MU-SINR estimation Beam selection for MU-MIMO UEs in 8RX (ID: 11148996)

**3.10.3.7-3.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11149030`)

MU-SINR estimation
If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/numberOfRxBeamforming = 8:

After a virtual UE is constructed completely, L2PS shall decide the beams for each UE in virtualUE(A) to receive PUSCH.

1. If two UEs are paired:

1.1) If both of UEs located in NLOS or LOS channel (5G\_UP\_ALG\_19956\_replaced([11148257](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksJdFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2PS shall select the first two best beams for each UE.

1.2) If one UE located in LOS channel and another UE located in NLOS channel :

If rdBeamsOpt (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25272\_replaced([11149785](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQKwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to **1:**

L2PS shall select the first two best beams(5G\_UP\_ALG\_20242\_replaced([11154912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for each UE.

If rdBeamsOpt (5G\_UP\_ALG\_25272\_replaced([11149785](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQKwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to **2:**

L2PS shall select the first best beam for the LOS UE and select the first three best beams(5G\_UP\_ALG\_20242\_replaced([11154912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the NLOS UE. **[CB015692-A]**If beam probing is enabled by NRBTS.NRCELL.actProbingUlSrsBeams = 'Beams3rd4th', third beam of the NLOS UE shall be the old 3rd beam until the probing decision is completed. **[End CB015692-A]**\*\*\*\*

1. If three UEs are paired,

-  If the number of layer for the paired UEs is the same, L2PS shall select the 1st best beam and 2nd best beam(5G\_UP\_ALG\_20242\_replaced([11154912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the UE with the lowest rescaled SINR(5G\_UP\_ALG\_17271\_replaced([11131543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to the number of required PRBs and the WB-SINR rrmCorrAvgSinr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3074\_replaced([11130160](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq-_e_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **which doesn't include rrmDeltaSinr[i,j,t] (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3151\_replaced([11137856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krbrbvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) ; L2PS shall select the 1st best beam(5G\_UP\_ALG\_20242\_replaced([11154912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the remaing two UEs.** NOTE: IF several UEs have the same lowest rescaled SINR. In order to make a simplify, L2PS shall randomly select one UE from them and assign two beams to it. The remaining UEs will be assigned with one beam.\*\*\*\*

-  otherwise, L2RT shall allocate more beams to the UEs with higher rank.

1. If four rank1 UEs are paired, L2PS shall select the 1st best beam(5G\_UP\_ALG\_20242\_replaced([11154912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for each UE. Only one candidate UE group could be paired with root UE.
2. If root UE paired with a candiate UE group, L2PS shall allocate two best beams(5G\_UP\_ALG\_20242\_replaced([11154912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for each UE.

**NOTE: 1) The 1st, 2nd, 3rd and 4th best beam selection refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20242\_replaced([11154912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 2) The identify of LOS/NLOS UEs refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19956\_replaced([11148257](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksJdFfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

---

#### 3.10.3.7-3.0-2 MU-SINR estimation Beam selection for MU-MIMO UEs in 16RX (ID: 11149038)

**3.10.3.7-3.0-2.0-3**  (ID: `11149061`)

MU-SINR estimation
11149061:
MU-SINR estimation
If MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/numberOfRxBeamforming = 16:

1. If root UE paired with normal UEs, the number of beams allocation for the paired UEs refer to the below table:

- If the number of layer for the paired UEs is different, L2RT shall re-order the UEs from high rank to low rank.L2RT shall allocate the number of beams to each UE according to the following table. The UEs with higher rank shall be assigned with more beams;

- Otherwise, L2RT shall skip rank re-order and allocate the beams directly according to the following table.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| UE number | UE1 | UE2 | UE3 | UE4 | UE5 | UE6 | UE7 | UE8 |
| 2 UEs | 4 | 4 |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| 3 UEs | 4 | 2 | 2 |  |  |  |  |  |
| 4 UEs | 2 | 2 | 2 | 2 |  |  |  |  |
| 5 UEs | 2 | 2 | 2 | 1 | 1 |  |  |  |
| 6 UEs | 2 | 2 | 1 | 1 | 1 | 1 |  |  |
| 7 UEs | 2 | 1 | 1 | 1 | 1 | 1 | 1 |  |
| 8 UEs | 1 | 1 | 1 | 1 | 1 | 1 | 1 | 1 |

1. If root UE paired with one candiate UE group, L2PS shall allocate four best beams(5G\_UP\_ALG\_20242\_replaced([11154912](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE0fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for each UE.
2. [CB008235-C]

When vUE(A) is contructed completely with the combination of  "normal UE" and "beam groups" (5G\_UP\_ALG\_29026\_replaced([11145918](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCIV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , OR "only beam groups"(5G\_UP\_ALG\_29140\_replaced([11146093](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCvZvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) :

- step1: L2RT shall get the number of paired beam groups [image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9423.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0], refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_29243\_replaced([11149324](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksNHd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

- step2: L2RT shall treat one beam group as one UE and allocate the number of beams according to the above table. The UEs in the same beam group will be allocated with the same number of beams. Note: When the UEs with different number of layers are FDMed in the same MU-MIMO layer, the same number of beams shall be allocated to those UEs.

[End CB008235-C]

### 3.10.3.7-5 MU-SINR estimation

#### 3.10.3.7-5.0-1 MU-SINR estimation The rescaled SINR of UE(i) shall be calculated according to the number of required PRBs (see 5G_UP_ALG_5010_replaced( 11201008 ) and 5G_UP_ALG_5016_replaced( 11201086 )) and the WB-SINR rrmCorrAvgSinr (5G_UP_ALG_3074_replaced( 11130160 )) which doesn't include rrmDeltaSinr[i,j,t] (ID: 11149161)

### 3.10.3.7-6 MU-SINR estimation

**3.10.3.7-6.0-5**  (ID: `11149201`)

MU-SINR estimation
This requirement is only applied when higher order receiver (>4RX) is used .

If PUSCH is received over 8 or larger than 8 spatial streams for a given subcell (5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

For the UEs whose data transmission are with UL MU-MIMO:

- the new IE "suPostCombSinr" which represents post SU-SINR after equalization (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21967\_replaced([11108937](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koxY_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be added in UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs.

- the 'sinr' in UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs represents post MU-SINR (5G\_UP\_ALG\_1701\_replaced([11108899](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kowx7_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) .

**For the UEs with MU-MIMO traffic, L2RT shall get post SINR from different sources as following:**

If RD parameter X is true **[CB008235-H] OR (NRBTS/NRCELL/NRULMUMIMO.ulMuMimoLinkAdaptionSwitch is equal to "MCS compensation" AND NRCELL.ulMaxMuMimoLayer is larger than 4)** [End CB008235-H], where X **= rdSuSinrFlag (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21893\_replaced([11149710](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksPjt_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is set to 8 and X = rdSuSinrFlag16RX (5G\_UP\_ALG\_27713\_replaced([11149730](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksPjuvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming is set to 16**\*\*\*\*

**Step1.1: L2RT shall calculate rrmInstSinr which is used to feed filter exponent.**

**Step1.1.1 For rank2 UE, rrmInstSinr shall be calculated according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22710\_replaced([11131439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krCp7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the input in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_22710\_replaced([11131439](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krCp7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is "rrmpostSuSinr[0] & rrmpostSuSinr[1] ", where rrmpostSuSinr[0]/[1] are as follows:**

- If at least one element of "suPostCombSinr[0]" and "suPostCombSinr[1]" in UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs is valid, rrmpostSuSinr[0]/[1] shall be equal to IE "suPostCombSinr[0] /[1]" separately ; otherwise, postSuSinr[0]/[1] shall be equal to "sinr[0]/[1]" in UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs. Note, if only one layer's SINR measurement is valid, L2RT shall handle it with the requirement in **Step1.1.2.**

**Step1.1.2 For rank1 UE, rrmInstSinr = rrmpostSuSinr[0], where  rrmpostSuSinr[0] is equal to IE "suPostCombSinr[0]" in UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs if it is a valid value; otherwise, rrmpostSuSinr[0] is equal to IE "sinr[0]" in UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs.**

**NOTE: L2RT shall NOT convert "suPostCombSinr" or "sinr" in UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs to post SU-SINR according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8348\_replaced([11148500](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEMfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) in step1.1.1 and step1.1.2 because they are estimated post SU-SINR by L1 in this branch.**

**Step1.2: If ((NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMaxMuMimoLayer > 4 && NRBTS/NRCELL/NRULMUMIMO.actUlMuMimoTapering == TRUE) && tapered beams are used for this UE according to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9866\_replaced([11148389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) && (rdUlTaperingSuSinrCompFlag (5G\_UP\_ALG\_30355\_replaced([11149923](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx2fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) == TRUE))**

- rrmInstSinr = rrmInstSinr in **Step1.1 - 10\*log10(rrmTaperingCompensation in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13871\_replaced([11148444](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKELfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

**Else**

L2PS shall follow the legacy behavior to get 'sinr' in UlData\_PuschReceiveRespPs and convert it to SU-SINR (5G\_UP\_ALG\_21939\_replaced([11148794](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksLSQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) before feeding it to exponential filter.

**End //Else**

**End //If RD parameter X is true**

---

### 3.10.3.7-7 MU-SINR estimation

#### 3.10.3.7-7.0-1 MU-SINR estimation Separation of Beam groups (ID: 11149214)

**3.10.3.7-7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11149221`)

MU-SINR estimation
L2RT shall decide the number of groups and DoA range for each group, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31395\_replaced([11149227](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksMgfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The UEs selected into groups shall satisfy 5G\_UP\_ALG\_32742\_replaced([11149261](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksMgfvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 3.10.3.7-7.0-2 MU-SINR estimation Number of beam groups and the DoA range for each beam group (ID: 11149227)

**3.10.3.7-7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11149253`)

MU-SINR estimation
11149253:
MU-SINR estimation
L2RT shall decide the number of beam groups and the DoA range for each beam group as below:
**Step1: L2RT shall calculate the absolute DoA diff between NRCELL.beamSet.leftEdgeAngle and NRCELL.beamSet.rightEdgeAngle**
diffDoA = absolute(NRCELL.beamSet.rightEdgeAngle - NRCELL.beamSet.leftEdgeAngle);
**Step2: Calculate the number of beam groups**
[image-0][image\_desc]The image is entirely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9440.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0], where rdUlGapDegree refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31948\_replaced([11149963](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksRY4fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), rdCoffGroupGap refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31950\_replaced([11149973](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksRY4_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
**Step3: Decide the start and end DoA for the jth beam group, where [image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, indicating it is either an empty image or a black screen. There is no discernible content, text, or objects within the image.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9440.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] and [image-2][image\_desc]The image is entirely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9440.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2]**
DoAj-th beamgroup,start=  ROUNDUP(minDoA) + (j - 1) \* ( rdUlGapDegree  + rdCoffGroupGap \*  rdUlGapDegree) ;
DoAj-th beam group,end=   DoAj-beamGroup,start + rdCoffGroupGap \*  rdUlGapDegree ;
[CB008235-H-UPD002]
Step4: Decide the start and end DoA for the ith gap group, where 1≤ k ≤ numofBeamGroups and DoAk,start < DoAk< DoAk,end
DoAk-th gap,start=  DoAj-th beamGroup,end;
DoAk-th gap,end=  DoAk-th gap,star+ rdUlGapDegree;
[End CB008235-H-UPD002]
Note，the gap defined in the above formulas is also treated as a beam group.

---

#### 3.10.3.7-7.0-3 MU-SINR estimation Beam groups eligible UEs (ID: 11149261)

**3.10.3.7-7.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11149266`)

MU-SINR estimation
L2RT shall add UE from rrmUlMuCandidateList ([11146147)](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCvavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) to beam groups only if they meet the following conditions:

con1: The UE’s DMRS capability shall be "len2", in order to simplify the algorithm

con2: Only UEs with initial transmission traffic are allowed, due to PRB allocation limitations in the sub-area; UEs with retransmission traffic shall be skipped.

con3: The UE shall be a non-MPR UE.

---

#### 3.10.3.7-7.0-4 MU-SINR estimation Beam groups assignment procedure for UEs (ID: 13250962)

**3.10.3.7-7.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `13250970`)

MU-SINR estimation
When NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.actUlMuMimoGroupPairing is TRUE and NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMaxMuMimoLayer is larger than 4, in each scheduling slot, L2RT shall determine the beam group based on its first best beam for available MU eligible UE which satisfied [11149261](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksMgfvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

[CB008148-E]

If the eligible UE set contains both CP-OFDM UEs and DFT-s-OFDM UEs, and two types of beam groups are required: one for DFT-s-OFDM and one for CP-OFDM, then L2RT shall perform the following procedure.

* For each CP-OFDM UE, L2RT shall identify the beam groups (group = 1…N, if maximum number of groups is N in [11149227](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksMgfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) corresponding to its first best beam and marks the group as CP-OFDM type.
* Similarly, for each DFT-s-OFDM UE, L2RT determines the beam group(s)  it can belong to and marks the group as DFT-s-OFDM type.
* L2RT shall separately maintain two separate beam groups sets for different waveforms by marking different waveform type as [13254093](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_AzgDgMbdEfCYBIz6acpPHw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

The number of beam groups may be doubled , because CP-OFDM UEs and DFT-s-OFDM UEs are not allowed to fall into the same beam group. For example, if both a DFT-s-OFDM UE and a CP-OFDM UE have their first best beam DoA located in beam group (1), then two separate beam groups labeled “1” will be created: one beam group (1) marked for CP-OFDM, and another beam group (1) marked for DFT-s-OFDM.

[End CB008148-E]

---

#### 3.10.3.7-7.0-5 MU-SINR estimation Beam group waveform property (ID: 13254093)

**3.10.3.7-7.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `13254094`)

MU-SINR estimation
If a beam group contains only CP-OFDM UEs, then L2RT shall mark its attribute as CP-OFDM.  
Conversely, if the group contains only DFT-s-OFDM UEs, L2RT shall mark its attribute as DFT-s-OFDM.

Note: A single group shall not contain a mixture of CP-OFDM and DFT-s-OFDM UEs. Refer to [13250962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_iRYg88VbEfCnuMJFWtMTpQ)

---

#### 3.10.3.7-7.0-7 MU-SINR estimation Number of required PRBs for beam group (ID: 11149288)

The number of layer for each beam group rrmBeamGroupLayerStep is defined as follows:

**Step1: L2RT shall find the maximum number of layer among the UEs included in beam group j;**

**Step2: In order to simplify algorithm, L2RT shall find the maximum number of layer among all of beam groups in step1 and update rrmBeamGroupLayerStep with it**

### 3.10.3.7-8 MU-SINR estimation

#### 3.10.3.7-8.0-1 MU-SINR estimation Overall view of Friend list creation and removal (ID: 13340155)

**3.10.3.7-8.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13340156`)

MU-SINR estimation
A Friend List (FL) is a logical group which shall include multiple MU paired users paired by the UL pairing algorithm. The FL(s) are maintained per MU paired user which shall include all the partner UEs that the user paired within one or multiple virtual UEs.

The FLs shall be maintained such that , for any UE, only the most recent pairing history is remembered. This need not be only for consecutive “slots”.

The FL is a mechanism to favor set of UEs that are MU paired to be selected together for scheduling in the current slot by adjusting their individual sub-priority, on the account of their recent pairing history. These FLs are created at the end of MU pairing in the FD scheduler for those MU paired users.

The principles to add, remove and maintaining of the FLs are same as in DL (See [13339999](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3gGHsNvTEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) however with the following UL specific criteria for the eligible users :

* The UEs shall satisfy the "con7" mentioned in the [11146147](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCvavvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). The required number of PRBs shall be determined based on the final Mcs used for scheduling the UE in this slot.
* [CB015010-C]The actions defined under overload protection shall be same as in DL and shall use the parameter rdFriendListDeactOlcUlPerCent ([13365961](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fZe_8PahEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) instead.[End CB015010-C]

The mechanism to adjust ("boost") the sub-priority of these friend users is specified in [13343526](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-eomEN8TEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

---

### 3.10.3.7-9 MU-SINR estimation

#### 3.10.3.7-9.0-1 MU-SINR estimation Adaptive vUE construction algorithm (ID: 12703468)

**3.10.3.7-9.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12703634`)

MU-SINR estimation
L2RT shall proactively adjust the MU-MIMO pairing strategy as follows:

[CB008235-H-UPD002] If  ((NIDD: actUlMuMimo == TRUE) and (NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMaxMuMimoLayer ≤ 4)): [End CB008235-H]

As SE check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9528\_replaced(11147177)) and muSinr/layer check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26274\_replaced(11147395)) is done at the end of virtual UE construction, it takes long time to have the result of these checks. So if SE check or muSinr/layer check failed many times, it will cost much CPU.

And since min-max algorithm is used for correlation, UE most likely to be paired successfully will be selected firstly.

So L2-PS will limit the times of SE check failure or muSinr/layer check failure according to the size of virtual UE. When failure reaches the limitation, the construction of this virtual UE will be ended and new root UE(if any) will be selected.

When virtual UE size = 1(only root UE), the maximum failure should be rdMaxSeFailureSize (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26276\_replaced(11149821))  & 0x0000000F.

When virtual UE size = 2, the maximum failure should be rdMaxSeFailureSize (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26276\_replaced(11149821))  & 0x000000F0

When virtual UE size = 3, the maximum failure should be rdMaxSeFailureSize (5G\_UP\_ALG\_26276\_replaced(11149821)) & 0x00000F00.

[CB008235-H-UPD002]

Else if ((NIDD: actUlMuMimo == TRUE) and (NRCELL.NRULMUMIMO.ulMaxMuMimoLayer >4), then

If the number of UEs in the CS1 list of the current slot is less than or equal to rdUlMaxUEProportionInCS1 ([12723162](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_G_apgm4EEfCmnYHxzZN44w?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) \*rdMaxNumUeTdUl (5G\_L2\_3702\_replaced([11182963](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27fs-fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then:

* Regardless of whether rdUlMuMimoGroupPairing.bit3 ([11149883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))  is set to true or false, L2RT shall follow the behavior defined for rdUlMuMimoGroupPairing.bit3 ([11149883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) being set to false, by selecting only retransmission UEs as the root UE as specified in [11145856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCIUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [PR852020] no matter the number of sub-area. [End PR852020]  
  Meanwhile, L2RT shall skip the SINR difference check ([11147104](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFysvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), skip the pairing of initial transmission UEs as defined in [12706379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_GS2lMGIhEfC3KtQ77je1xA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [PR852020] no matter the number of sub-area [End PR852020] and apply a sub-optimal correlation check as described in [11146643](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFLpfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).
* Regardless of whether rdUlMuMimoGroupPairing.bit1 ([11149883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) and rdUlMuMimoGroupPairing.bit2 ([11149883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) are set to true or false, L2RT shall continue following the behavior corresponding to rdUlMuMimoGroupPairing.bit1 ([11149883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) and rdUlMuMimoGroupPairing.bit2 ([11149883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) set to true by performing pairing algorithm in [11145918](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCIV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ) and [11146093](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCvZvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).
* For very closed UE pairing define in [11145811](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksBhSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), L2RT shall perform according to the RD parameter setting: if rdUlMuMimoGroupPairing.bit0 ([11149883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) is true, the very closed UE pairing algorithm define in [11145811](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksBhSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) is executed; otherwise, the algorithm define in [11145811](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksBhSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) shall not be executed, and this behavior is not affected by CPU overload or other bits of rdUlMuMimoGroupPairing  ([11149883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksQx0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9))

[End CB008235-H-UPD002]

End

---

#### 3.10.3.7-9.0-2 MU-SINR estimation Dynamic vUE Construction Limitation Based on RT Processing Load Severity (ID: 12703472)

**3.10.3.7-9.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13367708`)

MU-SINR estimation
If NRBTS.tmpActFeat1(Bit 0) *is set to 0,* *and HwVariant used is not ABIL, due to potential scheduler processing overload issue, the maximum number virtual UEs per TTI shall be restricted as described below. Note that this number shall include only those virtual UEs that have more than one paired UEs only initial Tx UEs.*\*\*

If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric (See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31301\_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU overload control handler, is below the value set for **rdMuMimoRedvUeLowOlcUlPerCent (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31858\_replaced([11217015](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcMxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then, gNB-DU shall not apply any restriction to number of vUE construction,**

Else if the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric is greater than or equal to the value set for **activation threshold of** rdMuMimoRedvUeLowOlcUlPerCent (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31858\_replaced([11217015](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcMxfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and less than the activation threshold of rdMuMimoRedvUeMedOlcUlPerCent (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31859\_replaced([11217029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcMx_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))then, gNB-DU shall allow the number of vUEs upto rdMaxNumVueInMedLoad (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32414\_replaced([11217267](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxeB8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))\*\*\*\*

Else if real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric value is greater than or equal to the value set for **activation threshold of rdMuMimoRedvUeMedOlcUlPerCent (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31859\_replaced([11217029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcMx_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and less than the activation threshold of** rdMuMimoRedvUeHighOlcUlPerCent (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31860\_replaced([11217041](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcMyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then, gNB-DU shall low the number of vUEs upto rdMaxNumVueInHighLoad (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32418\_replaced([11217280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxeB8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*\*\*

Else if real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric value is greater than or equal to the value set for **activation threshold of** rdMuMimoRedvUeHighOlcUlPerCent (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31860\_replaced([11217041](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcMyfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and less than the activation threshold of **rdMuMimoDeactOlcUlPerCent (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31861\_replaced([11217055](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcMy_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then, gNB-DU shall allow the number of vUEs upto rdMaxNumVueInCriticalLoad (5G\_UP\_ALG\_32420\_replaced([11217293](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxeB9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**\*\*\*\*

Else if real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric value is greater than or equal to the value set for **activation threshold of** rdMuMimoDeactOlcUlPerCent (5G\_UP\_ALG\_31861\_replaced([11217055](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxcMy_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then, gNB-DU shall disable vUE construction with more than one paired UEs.\*\*\*\*

[CB015010-C]If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric (See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_31301\_replaced([11216081](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxXUQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) value provided by the gNB-DU overload control handler, is below the value set forrdCplDeactOlcUlPerCent ([13367692](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-9uQQfdFEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) then, gNB-DU shall perform or resume TD metric of vUE update ([13348508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ZXVS5eoBEfCnwLcpJWh_Zw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) if suspended.

If the real-time scheduling (RT) processing load severity metric is greater than or equal to the value set for **activation threshold of** rdCplDeactOlcUlPerCent ([13367692](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_-9uQQfdFEfC0Z6kKit-MzQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) then, gNB-DU shall suspend TD metric of vUE update ([13348508](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ZXVS5eoBEfCnwLcpJWh_Zw?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), if already being performed [End CB015010-C].

#### 3.10.3.7.0-1 MU-SINR estimation MU-SINR estimation for the root UE and paired UEs (ID: 11148506)

**3.10.3.7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11148549`)

MU-SINR estimation
11148549:
MU-SINR estimation
The following algorithm shall be implemented when NIDD: ulMuMimoParaSet/ulMuMimoLinkAdaptionSwitch = 0 (MU-SINR estimation algorithm is active) ,
If UE(i) paired with another UE,
[Before CB008360-B]
[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation. The equation is:
$SINR\_{i,mu} = \frac{1}{\frac{1}{dB2Linear(SINR\_{i,su})} + \alpha \* \sum\_{j \in J^*} corr\_{i,j}}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9384.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]
[CB008360-B]
[image-1][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9384.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]
where,
 - J* is the set of paired UEs in one virtual UE excluding the UE i.
 [Before PR672232]
  -[image-2][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9384.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] is the resacled SINR(5G\_UP\_ALG\_22977\_replaced([11149153](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksMgYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to the number of required PRBs;
 [PR672232]
 - In SE check, [image-3][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9384.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] is the resacled SINR(5G\_UP\_ALG\_22977\_replaced([11149153](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksMgYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to the number of required PRBs; In final MCS decision, [image-4][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9384.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4] is the resacled SINR(5G\_UP\_ALG\_17271\_replaced([11131543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) which is calculated according to the number of scheduled PRBs , the WB-SINR rrmCorrAvgSinr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3074\_replaced([11130160](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq-_e_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rrmDeltaSinr[i,j,t](5G_UP_ALG_3151_replaced([11137856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krbrbvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The unit is dB;
 [End PR672232]
 - rrmTaperingCompensation refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13871\_replaced([11148444](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKELfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
-The calculation of [image-5][image\_desc]The image contains the letters "cr" in a stylized font. The letters are a gradient of brown and blue, with a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9384.006.png[/image\_path][/image-5] refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_16377\_replaced([11148680](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKrNvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
- The calculation of [image-6][image\_desc]The image contains the text "corr i,j" in a blurry, italicized font. The text is colored in shades of orange and yellow.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9384.007.png[/image\_path][/image-6] in this equation is the same as correlation calculation based on interference from UE(j) to UE(i) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9525\_replaced([11146916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFysPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
- [image-7][image\_desc]SINR$\_{i,mu}$[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9384.008.png[/image\_path][/image-7] is the MU-SINR of UE(i) whose unit is linear.
- The calculation of [image-8][image\_desc]The image contains the text "corr i,j" in a blurry, italicized font. The text is colored in shades of orange and yellow.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9384.009.png[/image\_path][/image-8] in this equation is the same as correlation calculation based on interference from UE(j) to UE(i) (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9525\_replaced([11146916](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFysPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). In the final MCS decision, the normalized corrlation shall be calculated based on tapered or non-tapered beams which are decided in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15693\_replaced([11148418](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEKfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), otherwise, the normalized correlation in SE check (5G\_UP\_ALG\_9528\_replaced([11147177](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksFytvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be decided in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9866\_replaced([11148389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKEI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
The delta SINR rrmDeltaSINRMuMimo  is calculated as following:
 [image-9][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula written in a sans-serif font. The formula is:
rrmDeltaSINRMuMimo = linear2dB(SINRi,mu) - linear2dB(dB2linear(SINRi,su) \* rrmTaperingCompensation)[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9384.010.png[/image\_path][/image-9], where  rrmTaperingCompensation refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13871\_replaced([11148444](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKELfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
[End CB008360-B]
NOTE: rrmDeltaSINRMuMimo is a negative value because MU-SINR should always be smaller than SU-SINR. rrmDeltaSINRMuMimo should be calculated after FD allocation and is used in the next UL data slot in order to transfer MU-SINR to SU-SINR and then go to filter.

#### 3.10.3.7.0-2 MU-SINR estimation MU-SINR estimation for the root UE and paired candidate UE group (ID: 11148556)

MU-SINR estimation

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9388.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

where,

- In SE check, [image-3][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9388.004.png[/image\_path][/image-3] is the resacled SINR(5G\_UP\_ALG\_22977\_replaced([11149153](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksMgYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to the number of required PRBs; In final MCS decision, [image-4][image\_desc]The image is completely black, with no discernible features or content.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9388.005.png[/image\_path][/image-4] is the resacled SINR(5G\_UP\_ALG\_17271\_replaced([11131543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to the number of scheduled PRBs               and the WB-SINR rrmCorrAvgSinr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3074\_replaced([11130160](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq-_e_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rrmDeltaSinr[i,j,t](5G_UP_ALG_3151_replaced([11137856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krbrbvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The unit is dB;

* rrmTaperingCompensation refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_13871\_replaced([11148444](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKELfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

#### 3.10.3.7.0-3 MU-SINR estimation alpha calculation (ID: 11148680)

**3.10.3.7.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `11148741`)

MU-SINR estimation
11148741:
MU-SINR estimation
 In the procedure to decide the final MCS according to MU-SINR (5G\_UP\_ALG\_8350\_replaced([11148506](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKrMPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_UP\_ALG\_9869\_replaced([11148556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksKrMvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the alpha used in MU-SINR equation shall be decided with the following steps:
Step1: L2PS shall always calculate alpha based on the following equation:
  [image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula defines a variable 'a' as the minimum of 1.0 and a fraction. The numerator of the fraction is "dB2Linear(rdMuSuSINRDiff)-1". The denominator of the fraction is "dB2Linear(SINRi,su)*rdMaxInterf*correlation". The formula is written in a standard mathematical notation.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9392.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0], where
- [image-1][image\_desc]The image contains the word "correlation" written in a dark blue, sans-serif font. The letters are slightly blurred, giving the text a soft appearance. The background is white.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9392.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1] shall be always equal to the value of  NIDD:NRCELL/ULMUMIMOPARASET/ulMuMimoCorrThd no matter whether NRBTS.NRCELL.nrCellType is configured to xDL4UL or xDL8UL or the number of paired UEs.
- [image-2][image\_desc]The image contains the text "SINR₁, eu".[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_m22dng\_5G\_UP\_Algorithms\_file\_9392.003.png[/image\_path][/image-2] is min(rdRescaledSuSINR(5G\_UP\_ALG\_14891\_replaced([11149495](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksOVkfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), rounding-off(rrmRescaledCorrAvgSinr)). In SE check, rdRescaledSuSINR shall be the resacled SINR(5G\_UP\_ALG\_22977\_replaced([11149153](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksMgYPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to the number of required PRBs ; In final MCS decision, rdRescaledSuSINR is the resacled SINR(5G\_UP\_ALG\_17271\_replaced([11131543](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krDQ6vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to the number of scheduled PRBs and the WB-SINR rrmCorrAvgSinr (5G\_UP\_ALG\_3074\_replaced([11130160](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq-_e_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rrmDeltaSinr[i,j,t](5G_UP_ALG_3151_replaced([11137856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krbrbvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The unit is dB;And the unit is dB.
- rdMuSuSINRDiff (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14893\_replaced([11149506](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksOVk_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
- rdMaxInterf (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_14896\_replaced([11149520](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksOVlfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
Step2: The alpha in step1 shall be used if the following condition is satisfied:
 - NRBTS.NRCELL.nrCellType == xDL4UL(x = 2,4,8 or 16) OR
 - NRBTS.NRCELL.nrCellType == xDL8UL(x = 8 or 16) and PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams for a given subcell(5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and only one subcell is scheduled for the paired UEs
        - OR PUSCH is received over 8 [CB010708-C] or larger than 8 [End CB010708-C] spatial streams for a given subcell(5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
Step3: If NRBTS.NRCELL.nrCellType == xDL8UL(x = 8 or 16) AND NRBTS.NRCELL.numberOfRxBeamforming == 4  AND two subcells are scheduled for the paired UEs, alpha shall be decided by the following table:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Rescaled SU-SINR range | alpha |
| <=15 | rdAlpha1 |
| 1540 | rdAlpha7 |
| The default value of rdAlpha1~rdAlpha7 refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_19891\_replaced([11149645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksO8q_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). |  |
|  In the procedure of SE check, if NIDD:nrCellType is xDL8UL, alpha used in MU-SINR equation shall be decided in step3; else if NIDD:nrCellType is xDL4UL, alpha shall be decided in step1. |  |

## 3.10.4 R&amp;D Parameters

### 3.10.4.0-1 R&amp;D Parameters rdUlMuReceiverBeamUsedOverlappingPRB (ID: 11149352)

**3.10.4.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12632019`)

R&D Parameters
12632019:
R&D Parameters
[Before CNI-137616-B] This parameter is used to select which UE beam is used on overlapping PRB for MU receiver if PUSCH is received over 4 spatial streams in a given UL subcell (5G\_UP\_8362\_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The detailed information refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_20408\_replaced([11104212](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kn52T_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Value range: **TRUE or FALSE**

Default value: TRUE

Description:

1) If this RD parameter is set to true, the beam of UE1 and UE2 is as following in case of UE2 and UE1 entering to the MU-IRC receiver. The number of PRB for UE1 is smaller than UE2 in this example.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image contains a table with two rows and two columns. The first column contains the labels "UE1" and "UE2". The second column contains information about data streams.

|  | Column 2 | Column 3 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| UE1 | 2 streams from UE1 1st best beam | 2 streams from UE2 2nd best beam |
| UE2 | 2 streams from UE2 1st best beam |  |

2)  If this RD parameter is set to false, the beam of UE1 and UE2 is as following in case of UE2 and UE1 entering to the MU-IRC receiver.The number of PRB for UE1 is smaller than UE2 in this example.

[image-1][image\_desc]The image contains a table with two rows and two columns. The first column contains the labels "UE1" and "UE2". The second column contains information about data streams.
The table can be represented as follows:

|  | Column 1 | Column 2 |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Row 1 | UE1 | 2 streams from UE1 1st best beam 2 streams from UE1 1st best beam |
| Row 2 | UE2 | 2streams from UE2 1st best beam |

Unit: -

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 1

Specified in: 5G\_UP\_ALG\_11355\_replaced([11104143](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kn5PNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[End CNI-137616-B]

Note: R&D parameter removed by CNI-137616.

### 3.10.4.0-4 R&amp;D Parameters rdSINR64QAM (ID: 11149409)

**3.10.4.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11149416`)

R&D Parameters
Short description: This value is used to control whether the UE whose SINR is higher than this parameter can't be selected as MU eligible UE when long term FO is higher than a threshold and MCS-64QAM table is used in UL MU MIMO.

Value range: 0 ... 50

Step size: 1

* [PR836770] bit3 = true, legacy pairing for initial transmission and re-transmission UEs with correlation check in step2 ([11145856](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCIUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). bit3 = false, only support re-transmission UE as root UE pairing with correlation check in step2 and partial initial transmission UEs that satisfy [12706379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_GS2lMGIhEfC3KtQ77je1xA). Note, when rdUlMuMimoGroupPairing.bit3 is set to false, rdUlMuMimoGroupPairing.bit2 shall be set to true to guarantee that pairing will be performed in [11146093](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksCvZvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). [End PR836770]

### 3.10.4.0-51 R&amp;D Parameters rdDlMuZfPairingRank (ID: 12446081)

**3.10.4.0-51.0-2**  (ID: `13322044`)

R&D Parameters
[Before CB012971-F-UPD002]

This parameter is used to optimize DL pairing option if only two SB BF UEs are paired with rank downgrade.  If averaged DL SU rank among two SB BF UEs >= value of this RD parameter, the DL pairing shall be avoided.

If both UEs are at rank 4 and this RD value is higher than 4, L2 shall also check averaged reported CQI with threshold, see [12827655: rdDlMuZfPairingCQIThd](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_RFwWka5eEfCyQasEtWkQ4A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).

For example, two UEs (rank 4 + rank 3), the averaged rank is 3.5. They can be paired if rdDlMuZfPairingRank = 4. They cannot be paired if rdDlMuZfPairingRank  = 3.

value range: 2, 3, 4, 5

default value: 5

Unit: 1

Online modifiable: Yes

step size: 1

Used in: [11144070: Virtual UE construction](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr7ao_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

[End CB012971-F-UPD002]

---

[Before CB012971-F-UPD002]

This parameter is CQI threshold for pairing two SB BF UEs which are at rank 4. If averaged report CQI of any UE is higher than this threshold, the DL pairing shall be avoided.
